# cs.CV [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [What DINO saw: ALiBi positional encoding reduces positional bias in Vision Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16840)
*Moritz Pawlowsky,Antonis Vamvakeros,Alexander Weiss,Anja Bielefeld,Samuel J. Cooper,Ronan Docherty*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本研究通过线性探测发现视觉变换器（ViTs）存在位置偏差，并通过微调使用ALiBi相对位置编码来减少这种偏差，使模型在复杂显微镜图像分割中保持良好语义特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 视觉变换器（Vision transformers, ViTs）特别是像DINOv2这样的特征基础模型，虽然学习到丰富的表示，但其架构选择（如位置编码）可能导致与语义内容无关的位置偏差和伪影。这使得在材料科学等领域的零样本适应变得困难，因为这些领域的图像通常是均匀微观结构的横截面（即没有优先方向）。

Method: 通过线性探测（linear probing）研究ViTs中的位置偏差，发现这种偏差存在于多种目标和位置编码中。随后通过微调模型使用ALiBi相对位置编码（relative positional encoding）来减少这种偏差。

Result: 研究表明这些模型保留了理想的通用语义特征，其无偏特征可以成功应用于复杂显微镜图像的可训练分割（trainable segmentation）。

Conclusion: 通过采用ALiBi相对位置编码进行微调，可以有效减少ViTs中的位置偏差，同时保持模型的语义表示能力，这对于材料科学等领域的图像分析应用具有重要意义。

Abstract: Vision transformers (ViTs) - especially feature foundation models like DINOv2 - learn rich representations useful for many downstream tasks. However, architectural choices (such as positional encoding) can lead to these models displaying positional biases and artefacts independent of semantic content. This makes zero-shot adaption difficult in fields like material science, where images are often cross-sections of homogeneous microstructure (i.e. having no preferred direction). In this work, we investigate the positional bias in ViTs via linear probing, finding it present across a range of objectives and positional encodings, and subsequently reduce it by finetuning models to use ALiBi relative positional encoding. We demonstrate that these models retain desirable general semantics and their unbiased features can be used successfully in trainable segmentation of complex microscopy images.

</details>


<div id='physics.med-ph'></div>

# physics.med-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [2] [The FLASH enigma](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15913)
*Diana Shvydka,Victor Karpov,Nilendu Gupta*

Main category: physics.med-ph

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了FLASH放射治疗（FLASH radiotherapy）的物理机制，解释了为何超高剂量率（ultra high dose rates）能在保持抗肿瘤效果的同时显著减少正常组织损伤（sparing effect）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在解释FLASH放射治疗模式的物理基础，即为何在极短治疗时间内使用超高剂量率能够维持传统的抗肿瘤效果，同时显著减少对正常组织的损伤（sparing effect）。

Method: 通过分析正常组织和肿瘤组织的结构形态差异：正常组织有序（ordered）而肿瘤组织无序（disordered），及其在电离辐射下不同的电荷密度和电子-空穴液体（electron-hole liquid, EHL）形成机制。

Result: 正常组织中高电荷密度形成电子-空穴液体（EHL），其低扩散性抑制了化学反应和自由基生成，从而产生保护效应。相反，无序的肿瘤组织提供有效的能量弛豫通道，形成抗肿瘤自由基。研究描述了FLASH治疗的剂量和剂量率阈值。

Conclusion: 正常组织和肿瘤组织对FLASH放射治疗的不同响应源于其结构形态差异导致的电荷密度和电子-空穴液体形成机制不同，这解释了保护效应的物理基础，并为FLASH治疗的剂量参数提供了理论依据。

Abstract: We consider physics behind the FLASH modality of cancer radiation treatment where extremely short treatment times are achieved with ultra high dose rates maintaining the conventional antitumor effectiveness and yet substantially reducing damage to normal tissues (sparing effect). The difference in responses between normal and tumor tissues is attributed here to different recombination rates related to their structure morphologies: ordered in normal vs disordered in the tumor tissues. Correspondingly different are their charge densities under ionizing radiation. In normal tissues it is high enough to form electron-hole liquid (EHL). Because of low EHL diffusivities, the chemical reaction and generation of free radicals are suppressed; hence, sparing effect. To the contrary, a disordered tumor tissue renders efficient energy relaxation channels forming antitumor free radicals. We describe the FLASH thresholds for doses and dose rates.

</details>


<div id='cond-mat.mtrl-sci'></div>

# cond-mat.mtrl-sci [[Back]](#toc)

### [3] [Production of Low-Density Aerogel Nuclear Fuels for Use in Fission Fragment Rockets and Novel Reactor Design](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15673)
*Noah D'Amico,Sandeep Puri,Ian Jones,Andrew Gillespie,Cuikun Lin,Bo Zhao,R. V. Duncan*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该论文开发了一种基于石墨烯气凝胶（graphene aerogel）的新型核燃料，其超低密度特性允许高能粒子逸出而不完全转化为热能，在空间推进和地面应用方面具有潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统核燃料中高能离子会将全部能量沉积为热能，限制了某些应用场景。本研究旨在开发一种新型核燃料形式，允许高能粒子逸出燃料颗粒，从而拓展核燃料在空间推进等领域的应用。

Method: 通过制备石墨烯水凝胶（graphene hydrogels），加载硝酸铀酰（uranyl nitrate）或硝酸钍（thorium nitrate），然后进行冷冻干燥（freeze-drying）来生产石墨烯气凝胶核燃料。样品密度控制在0.018-0.035 g/cm³，铀/钍质量分数约为7.3±0.5%。

Result: 测得气凝胶的α活性约为16 pCi/mg，通过减少样品厚度使所有α粒子逸出，可将活性提升至约49 pCi/mg。利用高能中子诱发裂变，成功从气凝胶燃料中获得裂变碎片源。

Conclusion: 这种新型核燃料形式在裂变碎片火箭发动机（fission fragment rocket engines）、模块化反应堆、直接转换方法以及医疗放射治疗等领域具有潜在应用价值。

Abstract: Graphene hydrogels were created and loaded with uranyl nitrate or thorium nitrate and freeze-dried to produce graphene aerogel nuclear fuels. These aerogels had densities between 0.018-0.035 g/cm3 and consisted of ~7.3 +- 0.5% uranium/thorium by mass. The ultra-low density of the aerogels allows for high energy ions to escape the fuel particles without depositing all their energy as heat, as is typical in nuclear fuels. Their measured alpha activity was ~16 pCi/mg, which could be enhanced up to ~49 pCi/mg by decreasing the thickness of aerogel samples to allow all alpha particles to escape. Additionally, high energy neutrons were used to induce fission to provide a source of fission fragments from the aerogel fuels. This novel form of nuclear fuel has potential applications in space propulsion such as fission fragment rocket engines, as well as in terrestrial applications for modular reactors, direct conversion methods, and in medical radiotherapeutics.

</details>


### [4] [LLM-Driven Discovery of High-Entropy Catalysts via Retrieval-Augmented Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15712)
*AI Scientists,Xinyi Lin,Danqing Yin,Ying Guo*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于检索增强生成（retrieval-augmented generation）的大语言模型框架，用于加速CO2还原催化剂（CO2 reduction catalysts）的发现过程。该框架通过访问包含50,000多种已知材料的数据库，将通用语言理解能力应用于高通量材料设计，显著提高了催化剂探索效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: CO2还原需要高效催化剂，但材料发现过程受限于长达10-20年的开发周期，且需要深厚的领域专业知识。传统方法在探索化学空间和解释结果方面存在瓶颈，需要更高效的工具来加速催化剂发现流程。

Method: 本文引入了检索增强生成（retrieval-augmented generation）框架，使GPT-4能够通过访问包含50,000多种已知材料的数据库来导航化学空间。该方法将通用语言理解能力适应于高通量材料设计，同时满足多目标约束条件。

Result: 该方法生成了超过250个催化剂候选物，其中82%具有热力学稳定性。68%的候选物实现了<100美元/公斤的成本，同时具备金属导电性（带隙<0.1eV）和机械稳定性（B/G>1.75）。最佳催化剂Fe0.2Co0.2Ni0.2Ir0.1Ru0.3的极限电位为0.285V，比IrO2提高了25%。火山图分析显示78%的LLM生成催化剂聚集在理论活性最优值附近，且系统计算效率比传统高通量筛选提高了200倍。

Conclusion: 研究表明检索增强生成能够在物理约束条件下保持AI创造力而不牺牲探索能力。该方法展示了自然语言界面如何简化材料发现工作流程，使研究人员能够更高效地探索化学空间，同时大语言模型协助结果解释和假设生成。

Abstract: CO2 reduction requires efficient catalysts, yet materials discovery remains bottlenecked by 10-20 year development cycles requiring deep domain expertise. This paper demonstrates how large language models can assist the catalyst discovery process by helping researchers explore chemical spaces and interpret results when augmented with retrieval-based grounding. We introduce a retrieval-augmented generation framework that enables GPT-4 to navigate chemical space by accessing a database of 50,000+ known materials, adapting general-purpose language understanding for high-throughput materials design. Our approach generated over 250 catalyst candidates with an 82% thermodynamic stability rate while addressing multi-objective constraints: 68% achieved <$100/kg cost with metallic conductivity (band gap<0.1eV) and mechanical stability (B/G>1.75). The best-performing Fe0.2Co0.2Ni0.2Ir0.1Ru0.3 achieves 0.285V limiting potential (25% improvement over IrO2), while Cr0.2Fe0.2Co0.3Ni0.2Mo0.1 optimally balances performance-cost trade-offs at $18/kg. Volcano plot analysis confirms that 78% of LLM-generated catalysts cluster near the theoretical activity optimum, while our system achieves 200x computational efficiency compared to traditional high-throughput screening. By demonstrating that retrieval-augmented generation can ground AI creativity in physical constraints without sacrificing exploration, this work demonstrates an approach where natural language interfaces can streamline materials discovery workflows, enabling researchers to explore chemical spaces more efficiently while the LLM assists in result interpretation and hypothesis generation.

</details>


### [5] [Synthesis and Transfer of Freestanding Strain-Engineered Vertically Aligned Nanocomposite Thin Films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15772)
*Carlos Rodríguez Cortéz,Moussa Mebarki,Bruno Berini,Dominique Demaille,Vincent Polewczyk,Yunlin Zheng,Pal Bhuyan,Boris Vodungbo,Emmanuelle Jal,Horia Popescu,Nicolas Jaouen,Yves Dumont,Marcel Hennes,Franck Vidal*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究开发了一种通过SrVO3介导的剥离工艺制备自支撑氧化物薄膜的方法，成功将超薄CoxNi1-x纳米线阵列嵌入SrTiO3基质的异质结构完整转移，并保持了纳米柱的结构完整性和磁性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自支撑氧化物薄膜（freestanding oxide thin films）的近期发展为设计具有增强功能的新型异质结构提供了机遇。研究旨在探索如何制备和转移包含超薄CoxNi1-x纳米线阵列的薄膜，同时保持其结构和化学完整性。

Method: 采用SrVO3介导的剥离工艺（SrVO3-mediated lift-off process）来创建和转移薄膜。通过结合X射线吸收光谱（x-ray absorption spectroscopy）、X射线共振磁散射（x-ray resonant magnetic scattering）、X射线衍射（x-ray diffraction）和磁光实验（magnetooptical experiments）进行表征。

Result: 该方法成功保持了自组装金属CoxNi1-x纳米柱（self-assembled, metallic CoxNi1-x nanopillars）的结构和化学完整性。嵌入纳米结构的大轴向变形保持完整，纳米复合薄膜的磁性能在衬底移除后基本保持不变。

Conclusion: 该研究为合成自支撑、应变工程垂直排列异质结构（freestanding, strain-engineered vertically aligned heterostructures）提供了一条新途径，为其未来集成到自旋电子（spintronic）和光磁（optomagnetic）器件中铺平了道路。

Abstract: The recent development of freestanding oxide thin films opens up exciting opportunities for the design of novel heterostructures with enhanced functionalities. Here, we explore the fabrication of membranes consisting of dense arrays of ultrathin CoxNi1-x nanowires epitaxially embedded in a SrTiO3 matrix. Through combined x-ray absorption spectroscopy, x-ray resonant magnetic scattering, x-ray diffraction and magnetooptical experiments, we show how a SrVO3-mediated lift-off process can be used to create and transfer these membranes while simultaneously preserving the structural and chemical integrity of the self-assembled, metallic CoxNi1-x nanopillars. With this approach, the large axial deformation of the embedded nanostructures is kept intact and, as a direct consequence, the magnetic properties of the nano-composite thin films remain largely unaltered after substrate removal. Our findings thus highlight a novel route for the synthesis of freestanding, strain-engineered vertically aligned heterostructures and pave the way for their future integration into spintronic and optomagnetic devices.

</details>


### [6] [Assessing the suitability of the Thomas-Fermi-von Weizsäcker density functional for itinerant magnetism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15850)
*Bishal Thapa,Phanish Suryanarayana,Igor I. Mazin*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究评估了Thomas-Fermi-von Weizsacker（TFW）泛函在轨道自由密度泛函理论（orbital-free DFT）中描述巡游磁性（itinerant magnetism）的能力，发现其与Kohn-Sham DFT结果存在显著差异，突显了TFW泛函在描述巡游磁性方面的基本局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于评估轨道自由密度泛函理论（orbital-free DFT）中的Thomas-Fermi-von Weizsacker（TFW）泛函描述巡游磁性（itinerant magnetism）的能力，这是对简化DFT方法在磁性系统应用的重要检验。

Method: 通过计算总能量对净磁化强度的二阶导数获得磁化率（susceptibility），以此评估磁性稳定性。研究对顺磁金属Al和Pd以及典型铁磁体Fe、Co、Ni进行计算，并将结果与Kohn-Sham DFT进行基准测试。

Result: 轨道自由（orbital-free）结果与Kohn-Sham预测的一致性较差，甚至无法捕捉定性趋势。使用轨道自由基态密度进行非自洽Kohn-Sham泛函计算可获得合理的定性一致性，但定量一致性仍然有限。

Conclusion: 研究结果突显了Thomas-Fermi-von Weizsacker（TFW）泛函在描述巡游磁性（itinerant magnetism）方面的基本局限性，表明该简化方法在磁性系统应用中存在显著不足。

Abstract: We assess the ability of the Thomas--Fermi--von Weizsacker (TFW) functional within orbital-free density functional theory (DFT) to describe itinerant magnetism. Magnetic stability is evaluated through the susceptibility obtained from the second derivative of the total energy with respect to the net magnetization. Calculations are performed for the paramagnetic metals Al and Pd and the canonical ferromagnets Fe, Co, and Ni, with the results benchmarked against Kohn--Sham DFT. The orbital-free results show poor agreement with the Kohn--Sham predictions, failing to capture even the qualitative trends. Using the orbital-free ground-state density with the Kohn--Sham functional in a non-self-consistent calculation yields reasonable qualitative agreement, although the quantitative agreement remains limited. These results highlight fundamental limitations of the TFW functional for describing itinerant magnetism.

</details>


### [7] [Tuning the optoelectronic properties of graphene quantum dots by BN-ring doping: A density functional theory study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15906)
*Samayita Das,Alok Shukla*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究通过第一性原理密度泛函理论计算，系统研究了硼氮环掺杂对石墨烯量子点（GQDs）光学性质的影响。结果显示，硼氮环掺杂能显著调控GQDs的光学吸收谱，实现从红外到可见光区的光谱展宽，为光电子应用提供了可调谐性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 石墨烯单层材料由于零带隙限制了其在光电子领域的应用。本研究旨在探索通过掺杂异质原子（如硼和氮）来调控石墨烯量子点的光电性质，特别是用硼氮环（borazine rings）替代碳环对光学性质的影响。

Method: 采用第一性原理密度泛函理论（DFT）详细研究了14种不同硼氮环掺杂的菱形石墨烯量子点的几何结构、电子结构和光学吸收谱。使用含时密度泛函理论（TDDFT）计算光学吸收谱，并分析单环和双环掺杂体系中环的位置、间距和取向对光学性质的影响。同时进行了群论分析，研究对称性降低对光学性质的影响。

Result: 硼氮环掺杂能实现对石墨烯量子点光学性质的显著调控。与原始石墨烯量子点相比，BN-GQDs的光学吸收谱显示出显著的光谱展宽，光学带隙覆盖从红外到可见光区域。前沿分子轨道分析揭示了低能光学激发的本质，群论分析表明对称性降低影响光学性质。

Conclusion: 系统性的硼氮环掺杂为BN-GQDs的电子和光学性质提供了易于调控的方法，这在光电子应用方面具有很大潜力。该研究证实了通过异质原子掺杂可以有效调控石墨烯量子点的光电性质。

Abstract: Graphene monolayer is a material with zero band gap, because of which its applications in optoelectronics are limited. The question arises, can we modify the optoelectronic properties of graphene by doping it with other atoms? Synthesis of 2D monolayer of graphene doped with hetero-atoms such as boron and nitrogen, and a few computational studies of their structural and electronic properties were previously reported. In this work, we aim to answer this question for graphene quantum dots (GQDs) by replacing their carbon rings with $(BN)_3$ (borazine) hexagonal rings. We have studied in detail the geometry, electronic structure, and optical absorption spectra of fourteen different borazine-ring doped diamond-shaped GQDs using first-principles density functional theory (DFT). These BN-GQDs differ in the location, orientation, and the number of borazine rings. We computed their optical absorption spectra using time-dependent DFT (TDDFT) and examined: (a) for single-ring doped BN-GQDs the influence of ring location on optical properties, and (b) for double-ring doped systems, the influence of location, mutual distance and orientation of the rings on their absorption spectra. Frontier molecular orbitals are studied in detail to understand the nature of low-lying optical excitations. We also performed a group-theoretic analysis of the influence of their reduced symmetries on their optical properties. Our results indicate that BN-ring doping can achieve significant control over the optical properties of GQDs. The comparison of the optical absorption spectra of the BN-GQDs with the parent GQD shows remarkable spectral broadening with optical gap spanning over infrared to visible region. Thus, systematic BN-ring doping provides easy tunability of the electronic and optical properties of BN-GQDs, which is very promising for optoelectronic applications.

</details>


### [8] [Mechanical Control of Polar Order](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15984)
*Pushpendra Gupta,Peter Meisenheimer,Xinyan Li,Sajid Husain,Vishantak Srikrishna,Ashley Cortesis,Yimo Han,Ramamoorthy Ramesh*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究发现了BiFeO3薄膜中机械辅助的铁电极化翻转途径，通过施加机械压力可显著降低翻转电压甚至实现自发翻转，为多铁性氧化物中耦合序参量的控制提供了新框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: BiFeO3作为典型多铁性材料，其铁电极化与铁弹晶格畸变耦合，但高翻转电场和竞争性极化变体限制了对其畴结构的确定性控制。需要探索新的翻转机制来克服这些限制。

Method: 研究采用外延BiFeO3薄膜，比较仅施加面外电场与同时施加机械压力两种情况下的极化翻转行为。通过压电力显微镜（piezoresponse force microscopy）测量分析机械压力对铁弹畴竞争的影响。

Result: 仅施加电场时翻转需要约4V电压并稳定共存极化态；同时施加机械压力可显著降低矫顽电压（甚至降至0V），实现自发翻转。机械压力抑制了铁弹畴竞争，降低了与极化旋转和畴壁运动相关的电能垒。

Conclusion: 应力作为主动热力学控制参数，能够访问仅电场下无法达到的翻转路径。机械辅助翻转通过直接耦合晶格畸变与极化反转，为控制多铁性氧化物中耦合序参量提供了通用框架，可用于器件级架构以降低铁电极化翻转能量。

Abstract: BiFeO3 is a model multiferroic in which the ferroelectric polarization is coupled to ferroelastic lattice distortions, yet deterministic control of its domain structure remains limited by high switching fields and competing polarization variants. Here, we identify a mechanically assisted polarization switching pathway in epitaxial BiFeO3 thin films that fundamentally alters the switching energetics. Using just out-of-plane electric fields, polarization reversal requires voltages of approximately 4 V and stabilizes coexisting polarization states. In contrast, when mechanical pressure is applied concurrently, the coercive voltage can be significantly reduced (even to 0V), resulting in spontaneous switching. Piezoresponse force microscopy measurements reveal that applied mechanical pressure suppresses ferroelastic domain competition, indicating a decrease in the required electrical energy barrier associated with polarization rotation and domain wall motion. These results demonstrate that stress acts as an active thermodynamic control parameter, enabling access to switching pathways that are inaccessible under only an electric field. By directly coupling lattice distortions to polarization reversal, mechanically assisted switching provides a general framework for controlling coupled order parameters in multiferroic oxides, which can be directly applied in the device-level architecture, where a small mechanical pressure can help in achieving lower switching energy of ferroelectric polarization. This work advances the fundamental understanding of electromechanical coupling in complex ferroics and establishes mechanical energy as a powerful tool for probing and manipulating ferroelastic ferroelectric interactions.

Abstract: Understanding and controlling interfacial electronic coupling in two-dimensional (2D) heterostructures is essential for designing functional materials for electronic, optoelectronic, and catalytic applications. The resulting Janus heterobilayers are energetically favorable and elastically stable, with electronic band gaps ranging from metallic and near-metallic to semiconducting regimes. Interlayer interactions induce significant band renormalization, including transitions between type I and type II alignment upon structural relaxation. To rationalize these effects, we establish a descriptor-based framework based on the metal metal interlayer distance, interfacial electron localization, and Bader charge redistribution. This combined analysis discriminates vdW-like, polar covalent, and ionic interaction regimes, with systematic trends governed by the average atomic number of the constituent elements. Optical absorption calculations indicate visible-to-near-infrared activity in selected systems, and band-edge alignment identifies promising candidates for selective redox processes. Overall, the proposed descriptor-based strategy provides a physically grounded route for identifying and engineering interfacial coupling in XP3 heterostructures and can be extended to other classes of two-dimensional material interfaces.

### [10] [Plasticity from Symmetry: A Gauge-Theoretic Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16619)
*Kevin T. Grosvenor,Mario Solís,Piotr Surówka*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该论文提出塑性变形具有非耗散、对称性决定的核心结构，通过构建有效场论将弹性和几何重组为耦合的高阶张量矢量规范结构，澄清了缺陷规范理论中基本变量的长期模糊性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上塑性变形被视为本质上的耗散现象，其理论描述主要基于唯象方法。本文旨在论证塑性实际上具有非耗散、对称性决定的核心结构，缺陷运动学在耗散之前就由对称性固定，并与本构假设分离。

Method: 从晶体相中时空对称性的自发破缺出发，构建有效场论（effective field theory），将弹性和几何重组为耦合的高阶张量矢量规范结构（higher-rank tensor vector gauge structure）。规范场并非假设，而是从应力和缺陷守恒定律中自然涌现。

Result: 位错（dislocations）、向错（disclinations）和扭转缺陷（torsional defects）表现为不可积几何的规范电荷，其连续性方程和迁移约束直接从高斯定律（Gauss laws）推导得出。这澄清了缺陷规范理论中哪些变量是基本变量的长期模糊性。

Conclusion: 塑性变形允许理想的规范理论表述，耗散流作为这种保守理论的可控变形出现。该研究为塑性理论提供了基于对称性和规范结构的新框架，超越了传统的唯象描述。

Abstract: Plastic deformation is widely regarded as an intrinsically dissipative phenomenon and its theoretical description is largely phenomenological. We argue instead that plasticity possesses a non-dissipative, symmetry determined backbone: defect kinematics are fixed by symmetry prior to dissipation and separate from constitutive assumptions. Starting from the spontaneous breaking of spacetime symmetries in a crystalline phase, we construct an effective field theory in which elasticity and geometry reorganize into a coupled higher-rank tensor vector gauge structure. The gauge fields are not postulated, rather they emerge naturally from stress and defect conservation laws. Dislocations, disclinations, and torsional defects appear as gauge charges of non-integrable geometry whose continuity equations and mobility constraints follow directly from Gauss laws. This clarifies the long-standing ambiguity over which variables are fundamental in the gauge theory of defects and shows that plasticity admits an ideal gauge-theoretic formulation, with dissipative flow arising as a controlled deformation of this conservative theory.

Result: 使用显式水中的丙氨酸二肽（alanine dipeptide）实现了多纳秒/天的增强采样，获得了与已知势能面盆地一致的拉氏图（Ramachandran plot）。对于极性溶剂环境中的分子内亲核加成反应，重现了自由能剖面中预期的溶剂诱导稳定化效应。进一步将该方法应用于细胞色素P450化合物I羟基化反应，获得了与公认反应机制一致的自由能景观。

Conclusion: 这些结果表明，基于uMLIP的反应性模拟可以应用于大型真实环境中的多种凝聚相过程，为复杂化学系统的计算研究提供了高效可行的解决方案。

Abstract: Universal machine-learning interatomic potentials (uMLIPs) enable reactive molecular simulations with near-DFT accuracy, yet applying them efficiently to large, realistic condensed-phase systems remains computationally demanding. Here we present PFP/MM, a hybrid approach that combines a uMLIP, PreFerred Potential (PFP), with molecular mechanics (MM) to enable both large-scale and long-time simulations that are challenging for uMLIP-only calculations. Using an alanine dipeptide in explicit water, we achieve multi-ns/day enhanced sampling and obtain a Ramachandran plot consistent with established basins. For an intramolecular nucleophilic addition reaction in a polar solvent environment, we reproduce the expected solvent-induced stabilization in the free-energy profile. We further apply the approach to a cytochrome P450 Compound I hydroxylation reaction and obtain a free-energy landscape consistent with the accepted reaction mechanism. These results demonstrate that uMLIP-based reactive simulations can be applied to diverse condensed-phase processes in large, realistic environments.

### [12] [Pressure and strain tuning of the alternating bilayer-trilayer Ruddlesden-Popper nickelate: crystal and electronic structure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16072)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations），通过分析高对称性P4/mmm结构中动态不稳定声子模式（dynamically unstable phonon modes）的不可约表示（irreducible representations），识别出包含八面体倾斜（octahedral tilts）的动态稳定低对称性C2/c结构。

Result: 压力与应变均倾向于抑制八面体倾斜，实现结构四方化（tetragonalizing），这与传统RP材料类似。电子结构在压力与应变下具有相似性，但三层区块的d_z²成键带（d_{z^2} bonding band）位置不同：在30 GPa压力下该带穿过费米能级（Fermi level），而在任何压缩应变下均保持在费米能级以下。

Abstract: We use first-principles calculations to investigate the crystal and electronic structure of the hybrid bilayer-trilayer Ruddlesden-Popper (RP) nickelate La$_7$Ni$_5$O$_{17}$ under hydrostatic pressure and biaxial compressive strain. By analyzing the irreducible representations of the dynamically unstable phonon modes in the high-symmetry $P4/mmm$ structure, we identify a dynamically stable lower-symmetry $C2/c$ structure containing octahedral tilts. The application of both pressure and compressive strain tends to suppress the octahedral tilts, effectively tetragonalizing the structure, in analogy with the conventional RPs. The electronic structure under hydrostatic pressure and strain has similarities, but it differs in the position of the $d_{z^2}$ bonding band from the trilayer block. This band crosses the Fermi level at a pressure of 30 GPa, but it remains below it for any level of compressive strain. This strain-induced modification mirrors the electronic structure changes observed in the conventional bilayer nickelate.

Abstract: Rutile RuO$_2$ has been proposed as an altermagnet, but its bulk magnetic ground state is still under debate because density-functional calculations give conflicting predictions. ### [14] [Pressure-driven vibrational and structural peculiarities in the honeycomb layered magnetoelectrics Mn4(B)2O9 (B= Nb, Ta)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16132)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用拉曼光谱（Raman spectroscopy）、同步辐射X射线衍射（synchrotron x-ray diffraction）和密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）计算相结合的方法，系统研究材料在高压下的结构演化。

Result: MTO在0.5 GPa即发生局部对称性破缺（local symmetry breaking）驱动的同构相变（isostructural transition），随后在约3.2、6和10 GPa出现三个额外同构相变，14 GPa附近开始从P-3c1相向P2/c相的长程结构转变（long-range structural transition）。MNO表现出类似同构相变但起始压力较低，两种材料均显示显著各向异性晶格压缩（anisotropic lattice compression），c/a比明显减小。

Conclusion: MTO比MNO在更低压力下发生局部对称性破缺，这归因于Nb5+和Ta5+阳离子的自旋轨道耦合强度（spin-orbit coupling strength）和轨道杂化（orbital hybridization）差异。各向异性压缩可能增强层间耦合并促进压缩下的磁有序（magnetic ordering）。

Abstract: The high-pressure behavior of two Mn-based honeycomb-structured magnetoelectric materials, Mn4Nb2O9 (MNO) and Mn4Ta2O9 (MTO), was investigated using Raman spectroscopy, synchrotron x-ray diffraction, and density functional theory (DFT) calculations. In MTO, the application of a small pressure of only 0.5 GPa induces an isostructural transition driven by local symmetry breaking. With further increase in pressure, three additional isostructural transitions are observed at about 3.2, 6, and 10 GPa, followed by the onset of a long-range structural transition near 14 GPa, where the ambient P-3c1 phase begins to transform into a P2/c phase. These two phases coexist up to 27 GPa. The Nb analogue, MNO, also exhibits similar isostructural transitions at about 2, 6.6, and 10 GPa. However, the onset of the mixed P2/c and P-3c1 phases occurs at a slightly lower pressure of 12.5 GPa, with phase coexistence extending up to 26.5 GPa. These long-range transitions are supported by pressure-dependent enthalpy changes obtained from DFT calculations. Rietveld refinement reveals pronounced anisotropic lattice compression, with a 42 to 49 percent difference between the c and a axes, leading to a notable reduction in the c/a ratio. This anisotropy may strengthen interlayer coupling and promote magnetic ordering under compression, consistent with the appearance of Raman modes similar to those reported at low temperatures, together with anomalous changes in Raman mode linewidth and intensity. The marked changes in Raman self-energy parameters, anomalies in the reduced pressure-Eulerian strain profile, and the onset of local symmetry breaking at much lower pressures in MTO than in MNO highlight the important role of differences in spin-orbit coupling strength and orbital hybridization associated with Nb5+ and Ta5+ cations.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Monolayer MnBi$_{2}$Te$_{4}$ (MBT) is an intrinsically magnetic topological insulator whose magnetic response is strongly affected by strain and electron correlation. In density functional theory with an on-site Hubbard correction (DFT+$U$), however, predictions vary substantially with the choice of Hubbard $U$, making it difficult to establish a reliable strain-dependent picture of magnetism in this system. Here we use diffusion Monte Carlo (DMC) to benchmark DFT+$U$ for monolayer MBT and to determine an effective $U$ as a function of strain. We find that the predicted magnetic phase diagram depends strongly on $U$, indicating that a single fixed value is not sufficient across the strain range considered. DMC nodal optimization further shows that the optimal $U$ increases with strain magnitude and is well captured by a simple quadratic form. When this DMC-informed strain-dependent $U$ is used in PBE+$U$, the calculated Mn local moments are brought into close agreement with DMC and are improved relative to commonly used fixed-$U$ choices. These results show that, for monolayer MBT, correlation strength itself should be treated as strain dependent, and they provide a practical many-body-guided strategy for improving strain-dependent DFT+$U$ descriptions of magnetic van der Waals materials.

### [16] [Dopability limits in Al-rich AlGaN alloys for far-UVC LEDs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16310)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 向固态紫外（UV）照明转型对降低全球能源消耗以实现净零目标至关重要。基于AlGaN的远紫外LED提供了无汞、高能效的替代方案，但其性能在铝含量超过80%时受到载流子注入效率低的严重制约，而关于AlGaN合金中点缺陷的系统研究仍然缺乏。

Method: 本研究采用显式合金建模方法，并适当处理带隙的温度依赖性，对高铝含量Al₁₋ₓGaₓN合金（x = 1/6、1/4和1/3）中的本征和外来缺陷进行了系统分析。

Result: 研究发现硅掺杂剂优先替代少数镓原子，在富铝环境中形成补偿性负-U DX中心，严重限制了n型导电性。碳被识别为最有害的无意杂质，而在通常用于器件的硅掺杂样品中，氧和氢的影响可以忽略。

Conclusion: 这些发现强调了显式合金建模的重要性，并为基于AlN的合金设计提供了有价值的见解，有助于解决高铝含量AlGaN器件中载流子注入效率低的关键瓶颈问题。

Abstract: Transitioning to solid-state ultraviolet (UV) lighting is critical for reducing global energy utilization to meet net-zero targets. AlGaN-based far-UVC LEDs offer a mercury-free, energy-efficient alternative to conventional mercury lamps, yet their performance is severely bottlenecked by poor carrier injection at Al compositions exceeding 80\%. Point defects are known to significantly affect carrier concentrations and radiative recombination efficiency, however, systematic studies of point defects in AlGaN alloys remain scarce. In this work, we investigate intrinsic and extrinsic defects in high-Al-content Al$_{1-x}$Ga$_x$N alloys ($x$ = 1/6, 1/4, and 1/3). We reveal that explicit alloy modeling and proper treatment of the temperature dependence of the band gap are essential to bring calculated carrier concentrations in line with experimental observations. We uncover that Si dopants preferentially substitute minority Ga atoms, forming compensating negative-\textit{U} \textit{DX} centers in Al-rich environments that severely limit n-type conductivity. We identify carbon as the most detrimental unintentional impurity, while the impact of oxygen and hydrogen is negligible in Si-doped samples typically used for devices. These findings highlight the significance of explicit alloy modeling and provide valuable insights into the design of AlN-based alloys.

### [17] [First-Principles Investigation of the Pressure Dependent Physical Properties of Intermetallic Kagome ZrRe2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16379)

Abstract: We present a density functional theory investigation of the pressure dependent structural, electronic, mechanical, thermophysical, vibrational, and optical properties of the intermetallic Kagome compound ZrRe2. The calculated ground-state structural parameters are in excellent agreement with available experimental results. The estimated structural parameters, elastic constants, and phonon dispersion confirm the structural, chemical, mechanical, and dynamical stability of ZrRe2 up to 25 GPa. The Kagome feature in the material has been identified from the electronic band structure for the first time. ZrRe2 exhibits topological feature at 0 GPa, which vanishes under 25 GPa. Fermi surface (FS) analysis predicts that ZrRe2 could potentially host a charge density wave (CDW) phase. The electronic and optical studies confirmed its metallic nature. The Debye temperature and phonon thermal conductivity are moderate, while the melting point is relatively high. Furthermore, ZrRe2 possesses moderate electron-phonon coupling, which weakens under pressure as the phonon modes harden. Consequently, the superconducting transition temperature decreases with increasing pressure. Most of the properties studied and analyses performed in this paper are novel in nature.

### [18] [Early Prediction of Creep Failure via Bayesian Inference of Evolving Barriers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16419)
*Juan Carlos Verano-Espitia,Tero Mäkinen,Mikko J. Alava,Jérôme Weiss*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种基于贝叶斯推断（Bayesian inference）的蠕变寿命预测方法，通过分析早期声发射（acoustic emission）数据来估计演化中的激活能垒（activation-energy landscape）统计特性，从而提供具有不确定性的寿命预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 蠕变（creep）在持续载荷下可长时间持续，但最终会突然屈服或断裂，这意味着即使材料看似固体也具有有限寿命。现有方法需要将微观能垒演化与宏观蠕变动力学联系起来进行更准确的寿命预测。

Method: 将寿命预测表述为对演化激活能垒景观（evolving activation-energy landscape）的贝叶斯推断（Bayesian inference）。利用早期声发射（acoustic emission）数据估计每个样品中演化能垒的统计特性，并生成失效时间（time-to-failure）的后验预测分布。

Result: 该方法能够提供具有不确定性感知的寿命预测，将微观能垒演化与宏观蠕变动力学联系起来。贝叶斯推断可以估计演化能垒统计特性，并产生失效时间的后验预测分布。

Conclusion: 基于贝叶斯推断的激活能垒景观演化分析为蠕变寿命预测提供了一种有效方法，能够通过早期声发射数据实现不确定性感知的寿命预测，建立了微观能垒演化与宏观蠕变行为之间的联系。

Abstract: Creep under a sustained load can persist for long times yet culminate in abrupt yielding or rupture, implying a finite lifetime even when the material appears solid. Here, we formulate lifetime prediction as Bayesian inference over an evolving activation-energy landscape. A time-dependent distribution of activation barriers controls deformation: stress lowers barriers, while irreversible rearrangements deplete the weakest sites and reshape the low-barrier tail. Using early-time acoustic emission data, Bayesian inference estimates the evolving barrier statistics in each sample and yields posterior predictive distributions for the time-to-failure. This approach provides uncertainty-aware lifetime forecasts that link microscopic barrier evolution to macroscopic creep dynamics.

### [19] [Tritium as an Unambiguous Isotopic Tracer for Nanoscale Hydrogen Analysis by Atom Probe Tomography](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16457)
*Maria Vrellou,Alexander Welle,Stefan Wagner,Marco Weber,Rolf Rolli,Hans-Christian Schneider,Astrid Pundt,Xufei Fang,Christoph Kirchlechner*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 选择钛作为研究平台，因其能容纳氢同位素。采用飞行时间二次离子质谱（ToF-SIMS）和电子背散射衍射（EBSD）在氚充注前表征初始成分和微观结构。在氚充注前后及三个不同时间间隔进行激光模式原子探针层析成像（APT）分析，追踪氚的掺入过程。热脱附分析（TDA）验证氚存在并补充SIMS测量。

Abstract: Accurate nanoscale detection of hydrogen is essential for understanding hydrogen-related phenomena in materials, yet conventional deuterium tracing is often complicated by residual background hydrogen. This study evaluates tritium as an unambiguous isotopic marker for nanoscale hydrogen analysis in metals using atom probe tomography (APT). Titanium was selected for its ability to incorporate hydrogen isotopes, providing a suitable platform for tritium detection. Time-of-flight secondary ion mass spectrometry (ToF-SIMS) and electron backscatter diffraction (EBSD) were performed prior to tritium charging to characterize the initial composition and microstructure. APT analysis in laser-mode before and after tritium charging, at three post-charging intervals, enables tracking of tritium incorporation over time. Thermal desorption analysis (TDA) confirmed the presence of tritium and complemented the SIMS measurements, highlighting the role of the surface oxide layer in modulating tritium release. This work serves as a fundamental benchmarking study for leveraging tritium and APT as a combined tool for understanding the nanoscale location of hydrogen in materials, being relevant for interpreting local processes related to e.g., hydrogen embrittlement.

### [20] [Anharmonicity Driven by Vacancy Ordering Unlocks High-performance Thermoelectric Conversion in Defective Chalcopyrites II-III$_2$-VI$_4$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16477)
*Hui Zhang,Jincheng Yue,Jiongzhi Zheng,Ning Wang,Wenling Ren,Shuyao Lin,Chen Shen,Hao Gao,Yanhui Liu,Yue-Wen Fang,Tian Cui*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过第一性原理计算揭示了缺陷黄铜矿（defective chalcopyrites）中空位有序化（vacancy ordering）作为结构放大器，通过增强晶格非谐性（lattice anharmonicity）和四声子散射（four-phonon scattering）实现超低晶格热导率，同时阴离子取代（anion substitution）可调控电子结构优化电输运，最终在CdGa₂Te₄中获得高热电优值ZT。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 缺陷黄铜矿因其有序本征空位能显著重塑晶格动力学和电子结构而成为有前景的热电材料。研究旨在通过第一性原理系统探究II-III₂-VI₄缺陷黄铜矿的热和载流子输运特性，建立空位有序化与热电性能之间的微观关联。

Method: 采用全面的第一性原理（first-principles）计算方法研究II-III₂-VI₄缺陷黄铜矿的热和载流子输运性质。通过分析空位有序化对晶格非谐性、金属键合特性（metavalent-bonding character）和声子散射的影响，并结合系统性的阴离子取代策略调控电子结构。

Result: 空位有序化作为结构放大器增强了晶格非谐性，结合软低频声子、强负格吕乃森参数（Grüneisen parameters）和显著增大的四声子散射相空间，导致四声子散射主导热输运，实现超低晶格热导率。阴离子电负性降低减弱金属-阴离子杂化，使阴离子p态上移、带隙变窄，优化了电输运。CdGa₂Te₄表现出0.19 W·m⁻¹K⁻¹的超低晶格热导率和0.957的高室温ZT值。

Conclusion: 研究建立了连接空位有序化、高阶声子散射和阴离子依赖能带工程的微观框架，证明缺陷黄铜矿是实现高性能热电材料的有前景平台。空位诱导的声子抑制与阴离子调控的电子优化之间的协同效应为设计高效热电材料提供了新策略。

Abstract: Defective chalcopyrites have recently emerged as promising thermoelectric materials because their ordered intrinsic vacancies can profoundly reshape both lattice dynamics and electronic structure. Here, we present a comprehensive first-principles investigation of the thermal and carrier transport properties of II-III$_2$-VI$_4$ defective chalcopyrites. We show that vacancy ordering serves as a structural amplifier of lattice distortion, giving rise to strong lattice anharmonicity and metavalent-bonding character. In combination with soft low-frequency phonons, strongly negative Grüneisen parameters, and substantially enlarged four-phonon scattering phase space, this leads to four-phonon scattering-dominated heat transport and suppresses the lattice thermal conductivity to ultralow values. Meanwhile, systematic anion substitution at the VI-site provides an effective route to tune the electronic structure: decreasing anion electronegativity weakens metal-anion hybridization, shifts anion $p$ states upward, narrows the band gap, and thereby improves electrical transport. Benefiting from this synergy between vacancy-induced phonon suppression and anion-regulated electronic optimization, CdGa$_2$Te$_4$ exhibits an ultralow lattice thermal conductivity of 0.19 W$\cdot$m$^{-1}$K$^{-1}$ and a high room-temperature $ZT$ of 0.957. These results establish a microscopic framework linking vacancy ordering, higher-order phonon scattering, and anion-dependent band engineering, and highlight defective chalcopyrites as a promising platform for high-performance thermoelectrics.

### [21] [Fully anharmonic calculations of the free energy of migration of point defects in UO2 and PuO2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16602)
*Dillon G. Frost,Johann Bouchet,Mihai-Cosmin Marinica,Clovis Lapointe,Jean-Bernard Maillet,Luca Messina*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究使用平均力势积分（PAFI）方法计算了UO₂和PuO₂中点缺陷迁移的非简谐自由能，揭示了简谐近似（harmonic approximation）的局限性，并发现温度升高显著降低迁移能垒，非简谐效应对扩散系数有重要影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 材料中点缺陷扩散率的计算通常依赖简谐近似来估计迁移自由能，但非简谐效应（anharmonic effects）对扩散性质有显著影响。然而，显式考虑这些效应通常计算成本高昂且难以实现，特别是在核燃料材料如UO₂和PuO₂中。

Method: 采用平均力势积分（PAFI）方法计算了UO₂和PuO₂中多种阳离子和阴离子缺陷类型的完全非简谐迁移自由能。使用了Cooper-Rushton-Grimes（CRG）势和最近开发的机器学习光谱邻域分析势（SNAP）进行UO₂计算，并系统比较了基于尝试频率（attempt frequencies）和德拜近似（Debye approximation）的简谐估计。

Result: 简谐近似的有效性强烈依赖于缺陷类型和基础势能模型，多个案例中观察到显著偏差。缺陷迁移能垒随温度升高而显著降低（0-1200 K之间可达1 eV），非简谐贡献可大幅改变迁移熵，进而影响扩散系数。使用CRG势比较UO₂和PuO₂发现，PuO₂在0 K时所有考虑缺陷的迁移焓较低，但被较高的尝试频率补偿，导致两种材料具有相似的总体跳跃频率。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了常用近似方法的局限性，并强调了非简谐效应对核燃料及其他材料中扩散预测建模的重要性。研究结果为理解缺陷迁移机制提供了新见解，对材料设计具有指导意义。

Abstract: Calculating diffusion rates of point defects in materials typically relies on the harmonic approximation to estimate migration free energies. However, anharmonic effects can have a large impact on diffusion properties, and explicitly accounting for them is usually computationally demanding and difficult to achieve in practice. In this work, we investigate the role of anharmonic effects on defect migration in UO2 and PuO2 using the potential of average force integration (PAFI) method. Fully anharmonic migration free energies are computed for several cation and anion defect types, using the Cooper-Rushton-Grimes (CRG) potential and a recently developed machine learning spectral neighbour analysis potential (SNAP) for UO2. Results are systematically compared to harmonic estimates based on attempt frequencies and the Debye approximation. Our results reveal that the validity of the harmonic approximation strongly depends on the defect type and the underlying potential, with significant deviations observed in several cases. In particular, defect migration barriers are found to decrease strongly with increasing temperature (up to 1 eV between 0 and 1200 K), and anharmonic contributions can substantially modify migration entropies and, consequently, diffusion coefficients. Comparing defect migration in UO2 and PuO2 using the CRG potential reveals that PuO2 has lower migration enthalpies at 0~K for all considered defects, but this is compensated by higher attempt frequencies, resulting in similar overall jump frequencies in UO2 and PuO2. These findings provide insight into the limitations of commonly used approximations and highlight the importance of anharmonic effects for predictive modeling of diffusion in nuclear fuels as well as in other classes of materials.

### [22] [$\mathrm{Cs_3V_9Te_{13}}$: A New Vanadium-Based Material with a Reuleaux-Triangle-Like Lattice and a Possible Phase Transition near 48 K](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16625)
*Zhen Zhao,Jianping Sun,Xin-Wei Yi,Ruwen Wang,Lin Zhu,Tong Liu,Haisen Liu,Hui Guo,Wu Zhou,Jinguang Cheng,Gang Su,Haitao Yang,Hong-Jun Gao*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Exploring and synthesizing materials with new crystal structures provides an important route to discovering exotic quantum phenomena. However, materials with unconventional lattice geometries remain largely unexplored. Here, we report the discovery of a new vanadium-based material, $\mathrm{Cs_3V_9Te_{13}}$, featuring a Reuleaux-triangle-like lattice. Electrical transport and magnetic measurements consistently reveal an anomaly near 48 K, and this feature shows little sensitivity to the applied magnetic field. A corresponding anomaly is also observed in the Hall coefficient near 48 K, indicating a marked change in the carrier response. In addition, temperature-dependent x-ray diffraction results indicate no obvious structural change across 48 K. Taken together, these results suggest that the anomaly is not induced by the structural transition, but associated to a possible electronic and/or magnetic phase transition. High-pressure transport measurements and first-principles calculations further reveal a highly tunable electronic state in $\mathrm{Cs_3V_9Te_{13}}$, with the kagome-like electronic feature and pressure-suppressed antiferromagnetism. These results demonstrate this material, with its structurally novel Reuleaux-triangle-like lattice, as a new platform for exploring the interplay between nontrivial lattice geometry and emergent physical phenomena.

### [23] [Ligand-Controlled Phonon Dynamics in CsPbBr3 Nanocrystals Revealed by Machine-Learned Interatomic Potentials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16631)
*Seungjun Cha,Chen Wang,Victor Fung,Guoxiang Hu*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究开发了一种机器学习原子间势能函数，用于预测卤化物钙钛矿纳米晶中表面配体对声子动力学的调控作用，揭示了阳离子和阴离子配体对关键振动模式的差异化影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 卤化物钙钛矿纳米晶（halide perovskite nanocrystals）是下一代光电子器件的领先候选材料，但表面配体（surface ligands）在调控其声子动力学（phonon dynamics）方面的作用仍不清楚。这些动力学对非辐射弛豫（nonradiative relaxation）、能量上转换（energy up-conversion）和声子辅助反斯托克斯发射（phonon-assisted anti-Stokes emission）至关重要。传统从头算方法（ab initio methods）虽然精确，但计算上无法处理实验相关尺寸的纳米晶，这些体系需要数千个原子来模拟真实的配体壳层和有限温度下的动态无序。

Method: 研究引入了一种机器学习原子间势能函数（machine-learned interatomic potential），该势能函数在小尺寸CsPbBr3纳米晶上进行微调，涵盖了多种配体。这种方法能够准确预测配体诱导的声子性质，其空间和时间尺度远超从头算方法的能力范围。

Result: 研究发现，阳离子和阴离子配体均系统性红移（redshift）Pb-Br-Pb伸缩模式（stretching modes），同时蓝移（blueshift）PbBr6⁴⁻八面体旋转模式（octahedral rotation mode），其中阴离子钝化（anionic passivation）的整体效应更强。值得注意的是，阴离子配体对旋转模式的硬化（stiffen）作用相对于配体结合能（ligand binding energy）呈现非单调性（non-monotonically）。

Conclusion: 研究结果揭示了阳离子和阴离子配体在调控卤化物钙钛矿纳米晶关键动态模式中的重要作用，这些模式与有害的非辐射损耗（nonradiative losses）相关。这为高性能钙钛矿纳米晶光电子器件提供了机理见解和设计原则。

Abstract: Halide perovskite nanocrystals are leading candidates for next-generation optoelectronics, yet the role of surface ligands in controlling their phonon dynamics remains poorly understood. These dynamics critically govern nonradiative relaxation, energy up-conversion, and phonon-assisted anti-Stokes emission. Conventional ab initio methods, while accurate, are computationally infeasible for experimentally relevant nanocrystal sizes that require thousands of atoms to capture realistic ligand shells and dynamic disorder at finite temperatures. Here, we introduce a machine- learned interatomic potential fine-tuned on small CsPbBr3 nanocrystals with diverse ligands, enabling accurate prediction of ligand-induced phonon properties far beyond the spatial and temporal scales of ab initio methods. We find that both cationic and anionic ligands systematically redshift Pb-Br-Pb stretching modes while blueshifting the PbBr64- octahedral rotation mode, with stronger overall effects for anionic passivation. Notably, anionic ligands stiffen the rotation mode non-monotonically with respect to the ligand binding energy. Our findings reveal important roles of cationic and anionic ligands in modulating key dynamic modes of halide perovskite nanocrystals associated with detrimental nonradiative losses, offering mechanistic insights and design principles for high-performance perovskite nanocrystal optoelectronics.

</details>


### [24] [Low bending rigidity and large Young's modulus drive strong flexural phonon renormalization in two-dimensional monolayers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16717)
*Navaneetha K Ravichandran*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过第一性原理计算揭示了二维材料中弯曲刚度（κ）对弯曲声学（ZA）声子非简谐重整化的控制作用，发现低κ材料（如锗烯）的重整化更强，而高κ材料（如二硫化钼）效应较弱。此外，长波长ZA声子经历额外重整化以稳定二维单层材料的平坦相，这一过程受弯曲刚度和面内杨氏模量竞争调节。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前文献缺乏对二维材料中弯曲声学（ZA）声子色散的明确第一性原理描述，特别是未充分考虑晶体非简谐性和大尺寸二维单层材料对热涨落的稳定性。许多有趣现象如波动性流体力学热流、低温下电阻率的对数发散以及微尺度剪纸结构都受ZA声子驱动，因此需要更准确的理论描述。

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）方法，系统研究二维单层材料中弯曲刚度（κ）对ZA声子非简谐重整化的控制作用。通过比较不同κ值的材料（如低κ的锗烯和高κ的二硫化钼），分析弯曲刚度与面内杨氏模量（in-plane Young's modulus）的竞争影响。

Result: 研究发现弯曲刚度控制着整个布里渊区（Brillouin zone）内ZA声子的非简谐重整化，低κ材料表现出更强的重整化效应。长波长ZA声子经历额外重整化以稳定二维单层材料的平坦相，这一过程受弯曲刚度和面内杨氏模量的竞争调节。重整化后的ZA声子色散与第一性原理研究中常用的描述存在质和量的差异。

Conclusion: 该工作为纳米尺度晶体非简谐性和宏观尺度弹性在塑造二维材料振动特性中的作用提供了新见解，将推动对二维及低维系统中ZA声子驱动的非常规热学和电子现象的重新审视。研究结果还将为低维系统特有的新颖工程应用（如剪纸结构）提供材料选择指导，超越石墨烯的限制。

Abstract: Many intriguing phenomena such as the wave-like hydrodynamic heat flow, the logarithmic divergence of electrical resistivity at low temperatures and microscale kirigami are driven by flexural acoustic (ZA) phonons in two-dimensional (2D) materials. Yet, a definitive first-principles description of their dispersion, with explicit consideration of the crystal anharmonicity and the stability of large 2D monolayers against thermal fluctuations, is lacking in the literature. Using first-principles calculations, we show that the bending rigidity ($κ$) controls the anharmonic renormalization of the ZA phonons throughout the Brillouin zone in 2D monolayers, with stronger renormalization in low-$κ$ materials like germanene and weaker effects in high-$κ$ materials like molybdenum disulphide. Furthermore, the ZA phonons at long wavelengths undergo an additional renormalization to stabilize the flat phase of the 2D monolayers against thermal fluctuations, which is modulated by the competing influence of the bending rigidity and the in-plane Young's modulus in all materials. The resulting renormalized ZA phonon dispersions are qualitatively and quantitatively different from those commonly used by the first-principles community, thus motivating a re-examination of the ZA phonon-driven unconventional thermal and electronic phenomena in 2D as well as lower-dimensional systems. Our work provides new insights into the role of nanoscale crystal anharmonicity and macroscale elasticity in shaping the vibrational properties of 2D materials and will inform novel engineering applications that are exclusive to low dimensions such as kirigami, with materials beyond graphene.

</details>


### [25] [Phonon collisional broadening and heat transport beyond the Boltzmann equation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16753)
*Enrico Di Lucente,Nicola Marzari,Michele Simoncelli*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过从Kadanoff-Baym方程（KBE）严格推导时空依赖的玻尔兹曼输运方程（BTE），提出了超越费米黄金定则（FGR）框架的线性化广义BTE（LGBTE），解决了基于FGR的BTE在热导率收敛性和二维系统预测失败等长期问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统基于费米黄金定则（Fermi's Golden Rule, FGR）的玻尔兹曼输运方程（Boltzmann Transport Equation, BTE）存在理论局限性：缺乏基于FGR的碰撞项严格推导，且在多个物理区域失效，特别是当声子色散（phonon dispersion）设定的能量变化尺度接近碰撞展宽（collisional broadening）时。这导致热导率（thermal conductivity）数值收敛性差，而现有自适应方案违反细致平衡（detailed balance）并产生非物理负特征值。

Method: 研究从Kadanoff-Baym方程（Kadanoff-Baym Equations, KBE）严格推导时空依赖的BTE，并引入超越FGR框架的线性化广义BTE（linearized generalized BTE, LGBTE）。该方法包含自洽、物理推导、完全非谐（fully anharmonic）且模式分辨的碰撞展宽和能量非守恒散射。同时建立了格林函数（Green's functions）的层级近似方案，为从半经典BTE向量子KBE精度的扩展提供了可控路径。

Result: 结合第一性原理模拟（first-principles simulations）和解析论证，该方法成功解决了基于FGR的线性化BTE的两个长期问题：1）热导率缺乏收敛性（如金刚石等热导体中常见）；2）在所有二维系统中的普遍失效，其根源在于FGR预测涉及弯曲振动（flexural vibrations）的散射通道存在非物理过阻尼（unphysical overdamping），如绝缘α-GeSe单层所示。

Conclusion: 该研究通过从KBE严格推导并引入LGBTE，克服了传统FGR框架的局限性，建立了包含碰撞展宽和能量非守恒散射的更完备理论框架。提出的格林函数层级近似方案为超越半经典BTE提供了系统化扩展路径，为解决晶体热输运中的长期理论难题提供了新途径。

Abstract: In crystals, macroscopic technological properties such as thermal conductivity originate from the microscopic drift and scattering of phonons, commonly described by the Boltzmann Transport Equation (BTE). Despite its widespread use, the most general space-time nonlocal form of the BTE still lacks a rigorous derivation of its collisional part based on Fermi's Golden Rule (FGR), and becomes inadequate in several regimes, including when the energy-variation scale set by phonon dispersion approaches that of collisional broadening. A hallmark of this issue is the poor numerical convergence of conductivity with respect to the smearing used to evaluate FGR rates. This is often circumvented using adaptive schemes, which however violate detailed balance and allow unphysical negative eigenvalues in the collision operator. Here, we overcome these limitations by rigorously deriving the space-time-dependent BTE from the Kadanoff-Baym Equations (KBE), and introduce a linearized generalized BTE (LGBTE) that goes beyond the FGR framework, incorporating self-consistent, physically derived, fully anharmonic, and mode-resolved collisional broadening and energy-nonconserving scattering. More generally, we establish a hierarchy of ansätze on Green's functions, enabling controlled extensions of the semiclassical BTE and a roadmap toward quantum KBE accuracy. Finally, using first-principles simulations complemented by analytical arguments, we show that this approach addresses two long-standing problems of the FGR-based linearized BTE across crystal dimensionalities: (i) the lack of conductivity convergence, common to heat conductors like diamond; and (ii) its universal failure in all 2D systems, rooted in FGR predicting an unphysical overdamping for scattering channels involving flexural vibrations, as shown in the insulating α-GeSe monolayer.

</details>

### [26] [Fourier transform of irregular connections on $\mathbb P^1$ and classification of Argyres-Douglas theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15942)
*Jean Douçot*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文为A型Argyres-Douglas理论的对偶性提供了数学解释，证明这些对偶性可通过傅里叶变换和莫比乌斯变换的组合实现，并阐明了3d镜像与无负边/环的非阿贝尔霍奇图之间的关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在为Beem等人最近发现的A型Argyres-Douglas理论对偶性提供数学解释。通过利用野生非阿贝尔霍奇对应，这些理论的定义数据可转化为特定形式的不规则连接奇点数据。

Method: 研究证明这些对偶性可通过两种基本操作的组合实现：傅里叶变换（Fourier transform）和交换零与无穷的莫比乌斯变换（Möbius transformation）。证明依赖于平稳相位公式，该公式给出了傅里叶变换奇点数据的显式表达式。

Result: 论文阐明了描述A型Argyres-Douglas理论3d镜像的箭图（quivers）与Boalch-Yamakawa及作者工作中定义的非阿贝尔霍奇图（nonabelian Hodge diagrams）之间的关系。3d镜像对应于在基本操作轨道中唯一没有负边/环的非阿贝尔霍奇图。

Conclusion: A型Argyres-Douglas理论的对偶性可通过傅里叶变换和莫比乌斯变换的组合操作在数学上实现。这一框架将物理对偶性转化为不规则连接奇点数据的变换，并建立了3d镜像与特定非阿贝尔霍奇图之间的对应关系。

Abstract: We give a mathematical interpretation of the dualities between type $A$ Argyres-Douglas theories recently obtained by Beem, Martone, Sacchi, Singh and Stedman, building on work of Xie. Using the fact that, via the wild nonabelian Hodge correspondence, the data defining such a theory amount to singularity data for irregular connections on $\mathbb P^1$ of a specific form, we show that these dualities can all be realized as compositions of two types of more basic operations acting on such irregular connections: the Fourier transform and a Möbius transformation exchanging zero and infinity. The proof relies on the stationary phase formula giving explicit expressions for the singularity data of the Fourier transform. We also clarify the relation between the quivers describing the 3d mirrors of type $A$ Argyres-Douglas theories and the nonabelian Hodge diagrams defined in work of Boalch-Yamakawa and of the author: the 3d mirror corresponds to the unique nonabelian Hodge diagram with no negative edges/loops among those of singularity data in the corresponding orbit under basic operations.

Result: 获得了BC型边界相互作用量子Toda链本征函数的高斯-吉文塔尔积分表示，建立了反射算子与巴克斯特算子的数学框架，证明了相关算子的对易关系。

Abstract: We obtain Gauss-Givental integral representation for the eigenfunctions of quantum Toda chain with boundary interaction of BC type. For this we introduce reflection operator satisfying reflection equation with DST chain Lax matrices. *N. Belousov,S. Derkachov,S. Khoroshkin*

TL;DR: 该论文证明了量子BC Toda链的Baxter算子对易性，构建了具有谱参数对称性的波函数，并建立了其与超八面体Whittaker函数的等价关系。

Abstract: In the previous paper we derived Gauss-Givental integral representation for the wave functions of quantum BC Toda chain and also introduced Baxter operators for this model. Furthermore, we derive Mellin-Barnes integral representation for the wave functions. With its help we show that wave functions satisfy dual system of difference equations with respect to spectral parameters and coincide with hyperoctahedral Whittaker functions. Finally, we give heuristic proofs of orthogonality and completeness of the wave functions.

Abstract: We show that quartic modifications of relativistic dispersion relations arise generically from deformation-quantized phase spaces under minimal kinematical assumptions relevant to quantum gravity. We establish this result through three independent approaches: Fedosov-Berezin quantization, spectral geometry, and a topos-theoretic formulation, all of which yield the same quartic correction and clarify the origin of its apparent universality.

Abstract: In this paper, we propose a soliton gas solution for the focusing Ablowitz-Ladik system. ### [31] [The weakly interacting tenfold way](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16799)
*Lucas C. P. A. M. Müssnich,Renato Vasconcellos Vieira*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文通过不可约自由费米子系统的时间演化算符实现拓扑K理论谱$KU$和$KO$，并证明弱相互作用下的变形收缩保持十重分类的稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于建立拓扑K理论谱与对称性费米子系统之间的具体联系，特别是通过时间演化算符实现$KU$和$KO$谱，并探讨弱相互作用对十重分类稳定性的影响。

Method: 方法包括：1）利用具有对称性的不可约自由费米子系统的时间演化算符实现$KU$和$KO$谱；2）引入弱相互作用时间演化算符的几何定义；3）证明相关谱$KU^{wi}$和$KO^{wi}$可变形收缩到原始谱。

Result: 主要结果为：1）给出了结构悬垂映射（suspension maps）的显式公式；2）证明了$KU^{wi}$和$KO^{wi}$谱可变形收缩到$KU$和$KO$；3）通过稳定同伦理论证明了十重分类（tenfold way）对弱相互作用的稳定性。

Conclusion: 结论表明，拓扑K理论谱可通过对称性费米子系统的时间演化算符具体实现，且十重分类在弱相互作用下保持稳定，这为拓扑物态的分类提供了数学基础。

Abstract: We present implementations of the topological K-theory spectra $KU$ and $KO$ in terms of time evolution operators of irreducible free fermion systems with symmetries, with explicit formulas for the structural suspension maps. We also introduce a geometric definition of weakly interacting time evolution operators, and show how associated spectra $KU^{wi}$ and $KO^{wi}$ deformation retract to $KU$ and $KO$. We thus have a stable homotopy theoretical proof that the tenfold way is stable to weak interactions.

</details>


### [32] [Ergodicity in discrete-time quantum walks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16837)
*Kiran Kumar,Mostafa Sabri*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文对整数格点上的齐次离散时间量子行走（quantum walks）的遍历性（ergodicity）进行了详细分析。在一维情形下，建立了酉算子（unitary operator）的绝对连续谱（absolutely continuous spectrum）与位置空间中动力学均匀分布（equidistribution）的完全等价关系。在高维情形下，提出了基于"无重复图（No Repeating Graphs）"谱性质的遍历性判据，并区分了均匀分布的强弱模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在深入分析整数格点上齐次离散时间量子行走的遍历性，特别是在大体积量子遍历性（large-volume quantum ergodicity）背景下，首次建立谱性质与动力学均匀分布之间的等价关系。研究动机源于理解量子行走的长期动力学行为及其与经典遍历理论的对应关系。

Method: 采用谱分析方法，通过分析编码量子行走的酉算子的谱性质来研究其遍历性。在一维情形下，重点考察绝对连续谱与动力学均匀分布的关系；在高维情形下，引入"无重复图"这一谱的精细性质作为遍历性判据，并区分弱收敛（weak convergence）与全变差收敛（total variation）两种均匀分布模式。

Result: 一维情形下获得了最重要的结果：酉算子的绝对连续谱与位置空间中动力学均匀分布完全等价，这是大体积量子遍历性背景下首次出现的等价关系。高维情形下，基于"无重复图"性质给出了完全和部分遍历性的判据，并区分了均匀分布的强弱程度。论文还提供了丰富的示例，应用这些判据完全刻画了某些量子行走族。

Conclusion: 本文建立了量子行走遍历性的谱理论框架，在一维情形下获得了谱性质与动力学均匀分布的完全等价关系，为量子遍历性研究提供了新的理论工具。高维情形的"无重复图"判据进一步扩展了量子行走遍历性的分析维度，区分了不同强度的均匀分布模式。

Abstract: We undertake a detailed analysis of ergodicity for homogeneous discrete-time quantum walks on the integer lattice. The most significant result of our paper holds in dimension one, and gives a complete equivalence between the absolutely continuous spectrum of the unitary operator encoding the walk, and the equidistribution of its dynamics in position space, which appears for the first time in the context of large-volume quantum ergodicity. In higher dimensions, we give a criterion for full and partial ergodicity in terms of a finer property of the spectrum which we dub ``No Repeating Graphs'', and distinguish how strongly the equidistribution is taking place (weak convergence vs total variation). The paper includes a wealth of examples where we apply our criteria, with certain families of walks fully characterized.

</details>


### [33] [Solving gravitational field equations by Wiener-Hopf matrix factorisation, and beyond](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16847)
*M. Cristina Câmara,Gabriel Lopes Cardoso*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该综述文章探讨了将二维爱因斯坦场方程视为可积系统，通过单值矩阵的Wiener-Hopf分解同时获得场方程及其Lax对的精确解，展示了引力场方程、可积系统、Riemann-Hilbert问题之间的深刻联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在回顾引力场方程、可积系统、Riemann-Hilbert问题和Wiener-Hopf分解理论之间的显著相互作用，特别关注过去十年中由奇异积分方程和Toeplitz算子研究推动的Wiener-Hopf分解技术进展。

Method: 通过将二维爱因斯坦场方程视为可积系统，采用单值矩阵（monodromy matrix）的规范Wiener-Hopf分解，同时获得场方程及其Lax对的精确解。文章利用具体示例说明该方法，并探讨通过τ-不变性（τ-invariance property）的推广作为新的解生成方法。

Result: Wiener-Hopf分解能够为引力理论场方程提供显式精确解，其推广通过τ-不变性性质提供了新的解生成方法。文章通过多个具体示例展示了这一跨学科方法的有效性。

Conclusion: 研究强调了基于广义相对论（General Relativity）、复分析和算子理论的跨学科方法对于引力场方程研究的重要性，展示了数学物理不同领域之间的深刻联系。

Abstract: By viewing Einstein's field equations -- reduced to two dimensions -- as an integrable system, one can simultaneously obtain exact solutions to both the equations themselves and their associated Lax pair via a canonical Wiener-Hopf factorisation of a so-called monodromy matrix. In this article, we review this remarkable interplay between gravitational field equations, integrable systems, Riemann-Hilbert problems, and Wiener-Hopf factorisation theory, with particular emphasis on developments from the past decade enabled by advances in Wiener-Hopf factorisation techniques arising from the study of singular integral equations and Toeplitz operators. Through a variety of concrete examples, we illustrate how Wiener-Hopf factorisation yields explicit, exact solutions to the field equations of gravitational theories, and how its generalisation through a so-called $τ$-invariance property provides a new solution-generating method. Along the way, we aim to demonstrate the importance of an interdisciplinary approach -- grounded in General Relativity, Complex Analysis, and Operator Theory -- for the study of gravitational field equations.

</details>

### [34] [Gravitational-Wave Propagation Through the Axiverse](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15838)
*Leah Jenks,Marc Kamionkowski*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了振荡的超轻标量场和赝标量场对引力波传播的影响，分析了宇称偶的Gauss-Bonnet耦合与宇称奇的Chern-Simons耦合两种机制，发现这些场会在群体和单个引力波事件层面产生由（赝）标量质量控制的振荡特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索超轻标量场和赝标量场与引力相互作用的物理效应，特别是这些场如何影响引力波的传播特性，这对于理解超出标准模型的基本物理具有重要意义。

Method: 研究方法包括理论分析两种（赝）标量与引力的耦合机制：宇称偶的高斯-博内（Gauss-Bonnet）耦合和宇称奇的陈-西蒙斯（Chern-Simons）耦合，并利用GW170817双中子星多信使观测数据对宇称偶标量-引力子耦合施加约束。

Result: 研究发现在宇称偶情况下，振荡特征体现在观测到的引力波红移分布、速度分布以及单个事件的色散关系和相位中；在宇称奇情况下，效应表现为双折射性，但在群体层面出现偏振的整体洗出，振荡特征可见于观测到的引力波振幅和倾角分布。

Conclusion: 研究结论表明连续单色引力波源是观测这些效应的有前景目标，（赝）标量场会在时域中对引力波波形产生调制，这有可能被LISA等空间探测器观测到，为探测超出标准模型的物理提供了新途径。

Abstract: We study the effects of oscillating, ultralight scalar and pseudoscalar fields on the propagation of gravitational waves (GWs). We consider two potential couplings of the (pseudo)scalars to gravity; a parity-even Gauss-Bonnet coupling, and parity-odd Chern-Simons coupling. We find several effects at both the population and individual GW event level, characterized by oscillatory features controlled by the (pseudo)scalar mass. In the parity-even case, this feature can be seen in the observed GW redshift and speed distributions, as well as in the dispersion relation and phase of individual events. We use the observation of the GW170817 multimessenger binary neutron star event to place constraints on the parity-even scalar-graviton coupling. In the parity-odd case, the effects are birefringent, but we find an overall washout of polarization at the population level. Oscillatory features can be seen in the observed GW amplitude and inclination distributions. Finally, we find that continuous, monochromatic GW sources are a promising target to observe these effects. The presence of a (pseudo)scalar field imprints a modulation of the GW waveform in the time domain, which can potentially be observed with space-based detectors such as LISA.

### [35] [Dark Energy with Constant Inertial Mass Density: Updated Constraints and Curvature-Induced Sign Transitions in $ρ_{\rm DE}$ and $ρ_{\rm DE}+p_{\rm DE}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15868)
*Luis A. Escamilla,Berat Karadavut,Nihan Katırcı*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本研究利用最新观测数据（DESI DR2 BAO、Planck CMB、CC和Pantheon+超新星）对simple-gDE模型进行约束分析。该模型以恒定惯性质量密度（IMD）为特征，是ΛCDM的单参数扩展。在平坦宇宙学中，模型与ΛCDM统计不可区分；但引入空间曲率后，simple-gDE模型显示出更丰富的暗能量现象学特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在通过观测数据约束simple-gDE模型，该模型属于graduated暗能量家族，以恒定惯性质量密度（inertial mass density, IMD）为特征。该参数化提供了ΛCDM的单参数物理扩展，为超越传统状态方程（equation-of-state）方法的暗能量动力学研究提供了新视角。

Method: 采用最新发布的DESI DR2 BAO数据，结合Planck 2018的CMB测量或晚期宇宙学探针（包括CC和Pantheon+超新星样本）。分析中考虑了SH0ES校准的有无两种情况，并比较了simple-gDE模型与wCDM和ΛCDM模型的宇宙学含义。

Result: 数据倾向于小的正IMD值，但贝叶斯证据表明在平坦宇宙学场景中，这些模型统计上不可区分。引入空间曲率后，simple-gDE模型展现出更丰富的现象学特征：对于BAO+CC+SN+SH0ES数据集，oSimple-gDE模型给出转变红移z†=1.51^{+0.68}_{-0.34}，零能量条件边界（NECB）交叉发生在z_NECB=2.36^{+1.48}_{-1.48}。该模型在统计上优于oΛCDM和owCDM。

Conclusion: IMD可能作为暗能量现象学的基本参数发挥重要作用。几何效应（如空间曲率）能够揭示暗能量区在平坦ΛCDM框架下隐藏的动力学特征。研究结果表明，在允许空间曲率的情况下，simple-gDE模型能够产生暗能量密度和IMD的符号转变，为理解暗能量动力学提供了新途径。

Abstract: We present updated observational constraints on the simple-gDE model, characterized by a constant inertial mass density (IMD) $ρ_{\rm DE}+p_{\rm DE}$,which belongs to the broader graduated dark energy family, and compare its cosmological implications with those of the $w$CDM and the $Λ$CDM models. This parametrization provides a physically motivated, one-parameter extension of $Λ$CDM, perspective on DE dynamics beyond the usual equation-of-state approach. We use the newly released DESI DR2 BAO data in combination with either CMB measurements from Planck 2018 or late-time probes, CC and the Pantheon+ SNe Ia sample, considered both with and without SH0ES calibration in this analysis. The data favor a small positive IMD, and Bayesian evidence indicates that the models remain statistically indistinguishable within spatially flat scenarios. Consequently, none of these models exhibits a sign transition in the DE energy density, and no improvement in $H_0$ tension. Allowing spatial curvature qualitatively enlarges the phenomenology of the dark sector. In particular, the interplay between spatial curvature and a nonzero IMD permits sign transitions in both the effective dark-energy density and the IMD during cosmic evolution. For the BAO+CC+SN+SH0ES dataset, the $o$Simple-gDE model yields a transition redshift $z^\dagger = 1.51^{+0.68}_{-0.34}$, while the crossing of the Null Energy Condition boundary (NECB), defined by $ρ_{\rm DE}+p_{\rm DE}=0$, occurs at $z_{\rm NECB}=2.36^{+1.48}_{-1.48}$. The model is statistically favored over $oΛ$CDM and $ow$CDM. These results highlight the potential role of IMD as a fundamental parameter in DE phenomenology and demonstrate that geometric effects, such as spatial curvature, can reveal dynamical features of the dark sector that remain hidden within the spatially flat $Λ$CDM framework.

### [36] [Cosmological prospects for multiband detection of intermediate-mass binary black holes with Taiji and ground-based detectors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15999)
*Yue-Yan Dong,Ji-Yu Song,Jing-Fei Zhang,Xin Zhang*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该研究通过模拟中等质量黑洞（IMBHs）双星系统的引力波信号，评估了空间探测器Taiji单独及与第三代地基探测器组成的多波段网络对其的探测能力，发现多波段观测能显著提升探测效果并改善宇宙学参数约束精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 中等质量黑洞（intermediate-mass black holes, IMBHs）填补了恒星级黑洞与超大质量黑洞之间的质量空白，但电磁观测手段难以探测。引力波观测为直接探测中等质量黑洞及其并合事件提供了有效途径。

Method: 研究模拟了不同种群模型下中等质量黑洞双星系统的引力波信号，评估了空间探测器Taiji单独以及Taiji与第三代地基探测器组成的多波段网络（multiband network）对这些信号的探测能力。

Result: Taiji在探测高质量中等质量黑洞双星方面表现良好，而地基探测器弥补了其对低质量系统灵敏度不足的问题。多波段观测将可探测参数空间扩大了约36.5%（相比单独Taiji）和31.0%（相比单独ET2CE），并显著提升了哈勃常数（H₀）的约束精度。

Conclusion: 多波段观测显著增强了中等质量黑洞双星系统的可探测性，并强化了其作为精密宇宙学（precision cosmology）探针的作用。参数精度的改善在样本量较小时最为明显，随着事件数量增加逐渐饱和。

Abstract: Intermediate-mass black holes (IMBHs) bridge the gap between stellar-mass and supermassive black holes, but remain challenging to detect electromagnetically. Gravitational-wave observations provide a direct means of detecting IMBHs and their mergers. We simulate the gravitational-wave signals of IMBH binaries under different population models and assess their detectability with the space-based detector Taiji alone and in a multiband network combining Taiji with third-generation ground-based detectors. Taiji performs well in detecting high-mass IMBH binaries, while ground-based detectors compensate for its reduced sensitivity to lower-mass systems. Their combination expands the accessible parameter space and improves the constraints on cosmological parameters. In particular, multiband observations improve the constraint accuracy on $H_0$ by $36.5\%$ and $31.0\%$ compared with Taiji and ET2CE alone, respectively. We further examine the dependence of parameter accuracy on the number of simulated events, finding that improvements are most pronounced for small samples and gradually saturate as the number of events increases. We conclude that multiband observations enhance the detectability of IMBH binaries and reinforce their role as probes of precision cosmology.

### [37] [Perturbative Effects of Dark Matter Environments on Black Hole Shadows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16402)
*Gabriel Gomez*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种微扰框架来描述暗物质环境中的黑洞形变，计算了光子球半径和黑洞阴影半径的修正，发现这些修正远超出当前观测限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前缺乏系统框架来建模暗物质环境中的黑洞解，现有方法存在方法论上的模糊性。构建此类解对于在强场引力体系中探测暗物质性质至关重要。

Method: 采用微扰框架描述静态球对称黑洞在周围暗物质分布下的形变。假设通用暗物质晕轮廓，计算光子球半径和黑洞阴影半径的领先阶修正，并应用于Hernquist和Navarro-Frenk-White等物理密度轮廓。

Result: 获得了扰动度规函数和Schwarzschild背景中临界撞击参数的封闭形式解析表达式。定量估计显示相应的阴影偏差远超出Keck和VLTI测量的当前观测界限。S2星轨道半径内包含的总暗物质质量远低于GRAVITY合作组报告的0.1%上限。

Conclusion: 该方法为研究暗物质对黑洞现象学的微扰效应提供了系统途径，包括对引力波观测的潜在影响。研究结果与当前观测约束一致，验证了框架的自洽性。

Abstract: Constructing spacetime solutions that describe black holes embedded in dark matter environments is a crucial step toward probing the properties of dark matter in the strong-field regime of gravity. At present, however, there is no unique or systematic framework to model such configurations, and several commonly adopted approaches raise methodological ambiguities. Motivated by these challenges, we build upon a perturbative framework to describe deformations of static, spherically symmetric black holes induced by a surrounding dark matter distribution. Within this framework, we compute the leading-order corrections to both the photon-sphere radius and the radius of the black hole shadow, assuming a generic dark matter halo profile. We then apply the formalism to physically motivated density profiles, including the Hernquist and Navarro-Frenk-White models, obtaining closed-form analytical expressions for the perturbed metric functions and for the critical impact parameter in the Schwarzschild background. Using these results, we obtain quantitative estimates for the corresponding shadow deviations and find that they lie well beyond the current observational bounds set by Keck and VLTI measurements. As a consistency check, we further estimate the total dark matter mass enclosed within the orbital radius of the S2 star and show that it remains well below the $0.1\%$ upper limit reported by the GRAVITY collaboration. Overall, this approach offers a systematic avenue to investigate perturbative effects of dark matter on black hole phenomenology, including potential implications for gravitational wave observations.

### [38] [Testing the Coexistence of Dark Energy and Dark Matter with Late-time Observational Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16533)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用具有哈勃函数解析解的共存模型，利用多种观测数据进行参数约束：包括新发布的宇宙计时器数据（31个旧数据和3个DESI新数据）、DESI DR2重子声学振荡数据、伽马射线暴数据以及多个超新星星表（Pantheon Plus、Union3和DES-Dovekie）。

Conclusion: 相互作用暗物质与暗能量共存模型能够有效描述宇宙晚期加速膨胀现象，在统计上优于标准宇宙学模型，但高红移行为与wCDM模型相似，且提供了更小的哈勃常数估计值。

Abstract: We investigate the viability of a cosmological scenario with interacting dark sector, which can describe the coexistence between dark energy and dark matter. The model possesses an analytical solution for the Hubble function and we constrain the free parameters by applying the newly released cosmic chronometers data (31 old data and 3 new data from DESI), the Baryonic Acoustic Oscillators from the Dark Energy Spectroscopic Instrument Survey (DESI DR2 BAO), along with Gamma-ray bursts (GRBs) and Supernova catalogues (Pantheon Plus, Union3, and DES-Dovekie). We find that the coexistence model fits the data sets in a better way than the reference models - the $Λ$CDM and $w$CDM models. The analysis shows that the coexistence scenario can provide a cosmologically viable model for the description of the late-time acceleration of the universe. Nevertheless, for large redshifts, the model has a similar behaviour to that of the $w$CDM model, as the introduction of the GRB data indicates in the statistical parameters. Finally, it is worth mentioning that the coexistence model provides a statistically smaller value for the $H_{0}$ parameter.

### [39] [Beyond $Λ$CDM with a Logistic RG-like Flow of the Low Redshift Cosmic Evolution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16852)
*Shibendu Gupta Choudhury,Anjan A Sen*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该研究引入了一种基于重整化群流启发的逻辑演化参数化框架，用于描述宇宙总状态方程$w_{\rm T}(z)$的演化，以探测标准$Λ$CDM范式在晚期的可能偏离。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期宇宙学观测显示，在晚期宇宙可能存在偏离标准$Λ$CDM范式的迹象。为研究这种偏离，需要建立一种不依赖于特定暗能量模型的参数化框架。

Method: 引入一个最小化现象学框架，其中宇宙总状态方程$w_{\rm T}(z)$遵循逻辑演化，这种演化受到宇宙学固定点之间重整化群流（renormalization group like flow）的启发。该方法直接重建背景可观测量探测的$w_{\rm T}(z)$，而不假设特定的暗能量模型。

Result: 使用DESI-DR2重子声学振荡测量、DES-Dovekie最新超新星数据和CMB距离先验，发现逻辑参数化相比$Λ$CDM提供了更好的拟合度，且与标准动力学暗能量模型保持竞争力。重建的急动参数（jerk parameter）反映了在低红移处与$Λ$CDM的显著偏离。

Conclusion: 虽然这些偏离的统计显著性依赖于模型，但结果表明流启发的参数化框架作为探测晚期宇宙动力学的补充且物理可解释的工具具有潜力。

Abstract: Recent cosmological observations show hints for possible deviations from the standard $Λ$CDM paradigm at late times. To study such deviation, we introduce a minimal phenomenological framework in which the total equation of state of the Universe, $w_{\rm T}(z)$, follows a logistic evolution motivated by a renormalization group like flow between cosmological fixed points. This approach directly reconstructs $w_{\rm T}(z)$ probed by background observables, without assuming a specific dark energy model. Using DESI-DR2 baryon acoustic oscillation measurements, DES-Dovekie latest supernova data, and CMB distance priors, we find that the logistic parametrization provides an improved fit compared to $Λ$CDM and remains competitive with standard dynamical dark energy models. The inferred expansion history exhibits noticeable deviations from $Λ$CDM at low redshifts, reflected in the reconstructed jerk parameter. While the statistical significance of these deviations is model-dependent, our results highlight the potential of flow-inspired parametrizations as a complementary and physically interpretable framework for probing late-time cosmic dynamics.

</details>

### [40] [Scaled transverse-momentum spectra as a probe of collective dynamics in heavy-ion collisions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15891)
*Thiago S. Domingues,Matthew Luzum*

Main category: nucl-th

TL;DR: 该研究通过移除多重数和平均横动量（mean transverse momentum）的全局尺度，发现超相对论重离子碰撞中横动量谱（transverse-momentum spectra）具有标度性（scaling property）。这种无量纲可观测量揭示了谱的固有形状在不同碰撞中心度、系统和能量间具有近似普适性（approximate universality），为集体动力学提供了新的探针。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索超相对论重离子碰撞中横动量谱的标度特性，以分离谱的固有形状并揭示其在不同碰撞条件下的普适行为。这有助于理解夸克-胶子等离子体（quark-gluon plasma）的集体动力学特性。

Method: 方法包括移除多重数和平均横动量的全局尺度，构建无量纲可观测量来隔离谱的固有形状。使用流体动力学模拟（hydrodynamic simulations）在逐事件（event-by-event）基础上验证标度性，并采用基于JETSCAPE混合模型训练的Gaussian-process emulators进行贝叶斯分析（Bayesian analysis）。

Result: 结果显示标度谱在不同碰撞中心度、系统和能量间表现出近似普适性。谱形状为介质关键性质提供了独立约束，包括平衡前动力学（pre-equilibrium dynamics）和初态颗粒度（initial-state granularity）。横质量谱（transverse-mass spectra）也显示出类似的标度性。

Conclusion: 标度谱为集体动力学提供了强大的新探针，并为重离子碰撞中产生的QCD物质的定量表征提供了互补约束。这些结果揭示了谱形状分析在理解夸克-胶子等离子体性质方面的重要价值。

Abstract: We investigate a scaling property of transverse-momentum spectra in ultrarelativistic heavy-ion collisions obtained by removing the global scales of multiplicity and mean transverse momentum. The resulting dimensionless observable isolates the intrinsic shape of the spectrum and reveals an approximate universality across collision centralities, systems, and energies. Hydrodynamic simulations reproduce this scaling on an event-by-event basis, indicating that it may originate from the collective dynamics of the quark-gluon plasma.
  Using Gaussian-process emulators trained on the JETSCAPE hybrid model, we perform a Bayesian analysis incorporating the scaled spectra as observables. The results demonstrate that the spectral shape provides independent constraints on key properties of the medium, including pre-equilibrium dynamics and initial-state granularity, while exposing tensions with parameter regions preferred by traditional $p_T$-integrated observables.
  We further explore an analogous scaling of transverse-mass spectra and observe a comparable universality across centralities and hadron species. These results suggest that scaled spectra provide a powerful new probe of collective dynamics and offer complementary constraints for the quantitative characterization of QCD matter created in heavy-ion collisions.

### [41] [Sensitivity of neutron star observables to microscopic nuclear parameters of realistic equations of state](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16019)
*Nikolas Cruz-Camacho,Carlos Conde-Ocazionez,Veronica Dexheimer,Jacquelyn Noronha-Hostler,Nicolás Yunes*

Main category: nucl-th

TL;DR: 该研究通过Fisher信息启发式分析，量化了中子星观测参数对Chiral-Mean-Field模型核物理参数的敏感性，识别出影响中子星性质最关键的三个核参数：χ₀、g₁ˣ和k₀。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超核密度下物质的状态方程（equation of state）决定中子星的天文观测特征。Chiral-Mean-Field模型虽能提供真实描述，但依赖众多微观核物理参数，需要系统分析这些参数对中子星观测量的影响。

Method: 采用Fisher信息启发式分析（Fisher-information-inspired analysis），在β平衡条件下使用SLy地壳模型，计算中子星序列并提取质量、半径、致密度和潮汐形变度。通过观测值对核参数的对数导数构建无量纲敏感性矩阵，并进行主成分分析（principal-component analysis）识别关键参数组合。

Result: 尽管参数重要性排序随观测量略有变化，但三个最重要的核参数为：标量势能整体尺度的χ₀（dilaton field真空值）、控制有效质量标量吸引的g₁ˣ（scalar singlet strength），以及决定标量势能曲率的k₀（quadratic scalar term）。

Conclusion: 该框架提供了可重复的数据驱动方法，用于量化致密物质模型中的参数敏感性，并为未来基于多信使天文观测（multi-messenger astrophysical observations）的贝叶斯推断（Bayesian inference）提供指导。

Abstract: The equation of state of matter at supranuclear densities governs the astrophysical observables of neutron stars. A realistic, though complex, description is provided by the Chiral-Mean-Field model, which depends on many microscopic nuclear-physics parameters. We present a Fisher-information-inspired analysis of the sensitivity of neutron-star observables to the parameters of the Chiral-Mean-Field model at $β$-equilibrium using SLy as a crust. We then compute neutron-star sequences and extract masses, radii, compactnesses, and tidal deformabilities. From the logarithmic derivatives of these observables with respect to each nuclear parameter, we construct a dimensionless, Fisher-inspired sensitivity matrix and perform a principal-component analysis to identify the effective combinations of nuclear parameters that most strongly affect neutron-star observables. Although the ranking depends mildly on the observable, the three most important nuclear parameters are the vacuum value of the dilaton field $χ_0$ (which sets the overall scale of the scalar potential and trace-anomaly contribution), the scalar singlet strength $g_{1}^X$ (which controls the overall scalar attraction through the baryon effective masses), and the $k_0$ quadratic scalar term (which governs the curvature of the scalar potential). This framework provides a reproducible, data-driven approach to quantify parameter sensitivities in dense-matter models and to guide future Bayesian inference of nuclear information from multi-messenger astrophysical observations.

### [42] [Exact Path Integral Methods in Supersymmetric $\text{AdS}_2\times \mathbf{S}^2$ Backgrounds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15730)
*Alberto Castellano,Carmine Montella,Matteo Zatti*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于精确计算AdS₂×S²背景中带电粒子的泛函行列式，这一计算是评估量子修正黑洞配分函数（quantum-corrected black hole partition function）的必要中间步骤。该背景可视为解决4维N=2超引力吸引子方程（attractor equations）的BPS黑洞的近地平线几何（near-horizon geometry）。

Method: 采用Schwinger固有时间形式（Schwinger proper-time formalism），在一圈（1-loop）和恒定背景场近似下推导完整的非微扰有效作用量（non-perturbative effective action）。随后将计算专门化到超对称（supersymmetric）设置，获得4维N=2 BPS超多重态（BPS hypermultiplet）的有效作用量。

Result: 精确确定了AdS₂×S²背景中带恒定电磁场的带电自旋0和自旋1/2粒子的泛函行列式，并获得了超对称AdS₂×S²时空中4维N=2 BPS超多重态的有效作用量。这些结果为量子修正的黑洞配分函数评估提供了必要基础。

Conclusion: 研究为量子修正黑洞配分函数的计算提供了关键中间结果，并讨论了与著名的Gopakumar-Vafa积分表示（Gopakumar-Vafa integral representation）的关系。该工作建立了超对称黑洞近地平线几何中量子效应的精确计算方法。

Abstract: We determine the exact functional determinants of charged, massive spin-0 and spin-$\frac12$ particles in $\text{AdS}_2\times \mathbf{S}^2$ backgrounds threaded by constant electric and magnetic fields. This is achieved using Schwinger proper-time formalism, which allows us to derive the full non-perturbative effective action in the 1-loop and constant background field approximations. We then specialize the computation to supersymmetric settings and we obtain the effective action for a 4d $\mathcal{N}=2$ BPS massive hypermultiplet in a supersymmetric $\text{AdS}_2\times \mathbf{S}^2$ spacetime. This setup can be seen to be equivalent to the near-horizon geometry of a BPS black hole which solves the attractor equations of 4d $\mathcal{N}=2$ supergravity. Our results provide a necessary intermediate step for the evaluation of the quantum-corrected black hole partition function. We also comment on the relation with the celebrated Gopakumar-Vafa integral representation.
