  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于揭示产生AdS₄×S²×S²超引力解的具体膜构型，这些解作为三维N=4共形场论（CFT）或四维N=4超对称杨-米尔斯理论（SYM）共形边界和畴壁的全息对偶（holographic dual）。通过分析这些构型，可以更好地理解八超荷理论的几何结构。

Method: 方法基于超对称膜构型分析，展示了AdS₄×S²×S²解与平直空间中正交D3、D5和NS5膜保持相同的Killing旋子。通过追踪从弱耦合参数区（膜不产生反作用）到超引力区的完整演化过程，揭示了AdS₄因子源于五维膜的特定自相似弯曲区域。

Result: 结果表明这些解的奇异源对应于半无限D3-D5和D3-NS5尖峰。AdS₄因子源于五维膜的特定自相似弯曲区域，其陡峭度与弱耦合连接数相同。研究还为Janus界面解提出了相应的膜构型，并为Gaiotto-Witten的"好-坏-丑"分类提供了清晰的几何解释。

Conclusion: 该构造为八超荷理论的Gaiotto-Witten"好-坏-丑"分类提供了清晰的几何解释：只有"好"理论在反作用时不发生五维膜交叉，最终产生AdS₄×S²×S²解。这一分析建立了从弱耦合膜构型到全息超引力解的完整对应关系。

Abstract: We reveal the supersymmetric brane configurations that give rise to AdS$_4\times$S$^2\times$S$^2$ supergravity solutions, which are holographic duals to three-dimensional $N=4$ CFTs or to conformal boundaries and domain walls of four-dimensional $N=4$ SYM. We show that these solutions preserve the same Killing spinors as orthogonal D3, D5 and NS5 branes in flat space, and that the singular sources of these solutions correspond to semi-infinite D3-D5 and D3-NS5 spikes.
  We track these solutions all the way from the weak-coupling regime of parameters, where the branes do not backreact, to the supergravity regime. We explain how the AdS$_4$ factor arises from certain universal self-similar bending regions of the five-branes, whose steepness is the same as the weak-coupling linking numbers. We also propose a brane configuration that gives rise to the Janus interface solutions.
  Our construction gives a clear geometric explanation of the Gaiotto-Witten "good-bad-ugly" classification of eight-supercharge theories: only good theories have five-branes that do not cross when back-reacting, and end up sourcing an AdS$_4\times$S$^2\times$S$^2$ solution.

*Yoav Zigdon*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用世界面（worldsheet）共形场论方法，通过强耦合共形场论描述弦尺度虫洞。具体分析了包含 $\text{SU}(2)_k$ 和 $\big(\text{SU}(2)_k \times \text{U}(1)_{k'}\big)/\text{U}(1)$ CFTs 的共形流形。

Result: 提供了多个共形场论描述弦在虫洞中传播的具体例子，包括欧几里得虫洞（Euclidean wormholes）、双锥（double cones）和爱因斯坦-罗森桥（Einstein-Rosen bridges）。发现强耦合CFTs通常描述这些弦尺度虫洞。

Abstract: I provide multiple examples of conformal field theories (CFTs) on the worldsheet that describe string propagation in target space wormholes connecting two disjoint asymptotic manifolds. The worldsheet approach goes beyond the framework of supergravity by incorporating wormholes for which the size of the throat is comparable to the string scale. Typically, strongly coupled CFTs describe these stringy wormholes, which include Euclidean wormholes, double cones, and Einstein-Rosen bridges. Finally, I interpret a conformal manifold that contains $\text{SU}(2)_k$ and $\big(\text{SU}(2)_k \times \text{U}(1)_{k'}\big)/\text{U}(1)$ CFTs as mediating a transition between a closed Universe and a wormhole.

### [45] [Negative running of gravitational positivity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15755)
*J. Fernandez,M. Ruhdorfer,J. Serra*

Main category: hep-th

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用四维时空中的单圈重整化群（one-loop renormalization group）方法，分析有效场论中具有平移对称性的标量场、光子场和引力子场的算符演化。重点研究非最小三点相互作用（non-minimal three-point interactions）对威尔逊系数跑动的影响。

Result: 研究发现某些非最小三点相互作用会导致相应威尔逊系数的负向跑动，其β函数受到普朗克尺度的抑制。威尔逊系数向红外（infrared）区域的减小促使研究者重新审视其色散界限（dispersive bounds），特别是考虑引力子圈（graviton loops）的贡献。

Conclusion: 引力相互作用会产生正向的红外贡献，在动量转移（momentum transfer）上进行平滑处理后，这些正向贡献被认为会主导负向跑动，前提是非最小耦合粒子（non-minimally coupled particles）的数量根据物种界限（species bound）受到上限约束。

Abstract: We investigate the one-loop renormalization group evolution in four dimensions of the leading operators in the effective field theories of shift-symmetric scalars, photons, and gravitons. We show that certain non-minimal three-point interactions induce a negative running of the corresponding Wilson coefficients, with beta-functions suppressed by the Planck scale. The decrease of the coefficients toward the infrared prompts us to revisit their dispersive bounds, in particular accounting for graviton loops. Gravitational interactions generate positive infrared contributions which, after smearing over the momentum transfer, are argued to dominated over the negative running, provided the number of non-minimally coupled particles is bounded from above according to the species bound.

Abstract: A foundational result in constructive quantum field theory is the construction of the free bosonic quantum field theory in four-dimensional Euclidean spacetime and the proof that it satisfies the Glimm-Jaffe axioms, a variant of the Osterwalder-Schrader axioms. We present a formalization of this result in the Lean 4 interactive theorem prover. The project is intended as a proof of concept that extended arguments in mathematical physics can be translated into machine-checked proofs using existing AI tools. We begin by introducing interactive theorem proving and constructive quantum field theory, then describe our formalization and the design decisions that shaped it. We also explain the methods we used, including coding assistants, and conclude by considering how AI assisted formalization may influence the future of theoretical physics.
  Our original release assumed three results, Minlos' theorem, the nuclear property of Schwartz space, and Goursat's theorem. In subsequent releases from our group and from contributors from the Lean community, these assumptions have been proven (or avoided), so that the OS/GJ axioms are now proven using only Lean and its library Mathlib.

### [47] [Reissner-Nordström Black Holes at second post-Minkowskian order from Scattering Amplitudes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15933)
*Allan Alonzo-Artiles,Manfred Kraus*

Main category: hep-th

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于计算带电致密天体双星系统的经典哈密顿量，该计算对于理解引力与电磁相互作用的耦合效应至关重要，特别是在后闵可夫斯基（post-Minkowskian）近似框架下。

Method: 采用爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦理论中的单圈散射振幅（one-loop scattering amplitudes），通过匹配非相对论经典有效场论（non-relativistic classical effective field theory）提取经典相互作用势。计算达到第二后闵可夫斯基阶（2PM），即$\mathcal{O}(G^2)$阶次。

Result: 获得了适用于所有速度阶次的经典哈密顿量，并提供了第二后闵可夫斯基阶的散射角（scattering angle）。研究结果与文献中现有结果完全一致，并对束缚系统的散射角、结合能和近星点进动（periastron shift）进行了比较分析。

Conclusion: 该研究成功计算了带电致密天体双星系统的经典哈密顿量，验证了与现有文献结果的一致性，为理解引力与电磁相互作用的耦合提供了重要的理论工具，特别是在后闵可夫斯基近似和后牛顿近似框架下的应用。

Abstract: We employ one-loop scattering amplitudes in Einstein-Maxwell theory to compute the classical Hamiltonian of a binary system of two charged, non-spinning compact objects. The Hamiltonian is valid to all orders in velocity and up to second post-Minkowskian order (2PM), i.e. $\mathcal{O}(G^2)$. The classical interaction potential is extracted via matching to a non-relativistic classical effective field theory. We also provide the scattering angle at 2PM order. We perform several cross checks on our results and find full agreement with existing results in the literature. Finally, we also briefly discuss a comparison for the scattering angle, the binding energy and the periastron shift of a bound system up to the second post-Newtonian order.

</details>


### [48] [Two-time physics, Carroll symmetry and Jordan algebras](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16276)
*Alexander Kamenshchik,Alessio Marrani,Federica Muscolino*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文基于Bars等人发展的双时（2T）物理框架，描述了具有非零能量的卡罗尔粒子（Carroll particles），并探索了2T物理的扩展相空间与基于半单三次约当代数构建的Freudenthal三重系统之间的联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于利用双时（2T）物理框架来描述具有非零能量的卡罗尔粒子，这类粒子保持静止状态。通过扩展时空维度（增加一个时间维和一个空间维），可以统一描述表面上不同的单时系统。

Method: 方法包括在具有额外时间维和空间维的时空中，对交换广义坐标与其共轭动量的相空间对称性进行规范（gauge）。本文发展了从2T物理框架中产生的卡罗尔粒子的经典和量子描述。

Result: 研究结果建立了2T物理的扩展相空间与基于半单三次约当代数（Lorentzian spin factor）构建的Freudenthal三重系统（Freudenthal triple systems）之间的联系。

Conclusion: 结论表明双时物理框架为描述卡罗尔粒子提供了统一的理论基础，并揭示了扩展相空间与代数结构之间的深层联系，为理解这类特殊粒子系统提供了新的数学工具。

Abstract: We describe Carroll particles with nonzero energy (i.e., particles that remain at rest) within the framework of two-time (2T) physics developed by Bars and collaborators. In a spacetime with one additional time and one additional space dimension, one can gauge the phase-space symmetry that exchanges generalized coordinates with their conjugate momenta, thereby unifying the description of apparently different one-time systems. We develop both classical and quantum descriptions of the Carroll particle arising from 2T physics, and explore links between the extended phase space of 2T physics and Freudenthal triple systems constructed over a semisimple cubic Jordan algebra (the Lorentzian spin factor).

### [49] [Krylov Complexity in Supersymmetric Large-$N$ Quantum Mechanics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16291)
*Eleonora Alfinito,Matteo Beccaria*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了Krylov复杂度在Veneziano-Wosiek模型中的行为，该模型是具有弱强对偶性的超对称矩阵量子力学模型。研究发现，在临界耦合λ=1处，Krylov复杂度呈二次增长K(t)∼t²，而在λ≠1时则呈现振荡行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Krylov复杂度最近已成为研究多体系统和全息对偶中算子增长和量子动力学的重要探针。本文旨在探究其在具有弱强对偶性和临界相变的Veneziano-Wosiek模型中的行为特征。

Method: 从具有超对称关系的费米子数为0和1的选定态出发，分析数值复杂度的随时间演化。同时研究Veneziano-Wosiek哈密顿量的秩1修正伴生模型，该模型允许显式超荷，从而能够精确计算Krylov复杂度。

Result: 在λ≠1时，Krylov复杂度K(t)呈现振荡行为；在临界耦合λ=1处，它随时间呈二次增长K(t)∼t²，且振幅依赖于费米子数扇区。高阶M度Krylov复杂度在临界点也呈现多项式增长∼t^{2M}。

Conclusion: Krylov复杂度在临界点的二次增长行为类似于一维量子谐振子中局域压缩态的扩散，其中自由极限ω→0对应于临界λ→1极限。伴生模型的精确计算结果与原模型观测行为一致。

Abstract: Krylov complexity has recently emerged as a useful probe of operator growth and quantum dynamics in many-body systems and holographic dualities. In this paper we study its behavior in the Veneziano--Wosiek model, a supersymmetric matrix quantum mechanical model admitting a large-$N$ planar limit with manifest weak-strong duality and a critical transition at the 't Hooft coupling $λ=1$. Starting from selected states in the sectors with fermion number 0 and 1, related by supersymmetry, we analyze the time dependence of the numerical complexity. For $λ\neq1$ the Krylov complexity $K(t)$ exhibits oscillatory behavior, while at the critical coupling $λ=1$ it grows quadratically in time, $K(t)\sim t^2$, with sector-dependent amplitudes. To obtain analytical insight, we study a companion model defined by a rank-1 modification of the Veneziano--Wosiek Hamiltonian, which admits explicit supercharges. In this model the Krylov complexity can be computed exactly and reproduces the behavior observed in the original model. Higher degree-$M$ Krylov complexities, defined as expectation values of powers of Lanczos index, are also computed and grow polynomially in time $\sim t^{2M}$ at the critical point in both models. This behavior is closely analogous to the spreading of a localized squeezed state in a one-dimensional quantum harmonic oscillator of frequency $ω$, with the free limit $ω\to 0$ corresponding to the critical $λ\to 1$ limit.

</details>


### [50] [Gravitational Metric of a Star](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16493)
*Poul H. Damgaard,Hojin Lee,Kanghoon Lee,Tabasum Rahnuma*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文通过递归求解广义相对论中的经典运动方程，研究了空间局域化静止物质源的度规。作者采用de Donder规范，建立了递归方程，将星体外部度规展开为牛顿常数和多极矩的扰动级数。在二阶后闵可夫斯基近似下，结果用动量空间的广义张量泡积分和逆距离展开表示，并在特定多极矩参数下恢复了Kerr黑洞解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于分析一般组成星体的度规特性，通过其无限多极矩集合进行表征。特别关注de Donder规范下的递归求解方法，旨在获得星体外部度规在扰动理论中的任意阶展开。

Method: 方法包括递归求解广义相对论经典运动方程，在de Donder规范下建立递归方程。将度规展开为牛顿常数（Newton's constant）和多极矩（multipoles）的扰动级数，使用后闵可夫斯基（post-Minkowskian）展开方法。

Result: 在二阶后闵可夫斯基近似下，将结果表示为动量空间中的广义张量泡积分（generalized tensor bubble integrals）和相应的逆距离简单展开。在特定多极矩参数空间中恢复了给定阶数的Kerr黑洞解，通过微调多极矩参数可获得类Kerr但非黑洞的星体度规。

Conclusion: 研究表明通过调整多极矩参数可以构造类Kerr但非黑洞的星体度规，同时指出了de Donder规范中关于规范模糊性的微妙问题。该方法为研究一般组成星体的度规特性提供了系统框架。

Abstract: Solving the classical equations of motion in general relativity recursively, we consider the metric of a spatially localized and stationary source of matter. Having in mind a star of general composition, we characterize it by means of its infinite set of mass and current multipoles. Specializing to de Donder gauge we set up the recursive equations that produce the metric outside the star to any desired order in perturbation theory, expanded both in Newton's constant and in the order of multipoles. Up to second post-Minkowskian order we express the result to any order in the multipole expansion in terms of generalized (tensor) bubble integrals in momentum space and a corresponding simple expansion in inverse distances. In a special corner of the space of multipoles we recover the Kerr black hole solution to the given order. By tweaking just slightly the multipoles away from the Kerr limit the metric will describe stars that are Kerr-like and yet are not black holes. A subtlety with respect to the gauge ambiguity of de Donder gauge is also pointed out.

</details>

Method: 研究方法包括将半正交性质（semiorthogonal property）解释为动力学选择规则（dynamical selection rule），并基于此提出理论猜想，将四次立方体的K3 Hodge原子（K3 Hodge atom）与受保护量子相联系起来。

Abstract: We compare algebraic and analytic pictures relevant to the study of birational invariants. Motivated by recent advances in the development of non-commutative Hodge structures, we examine their implication for quiver gauge field theory on the cubic fourfold. ### [52] [Novel cluster-algebraic letters for 5- and 6-point QCD processes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16743)
*Rigers Aliaj,Garbriele Dian,Georgios Papathanasiou*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 通过打破对偶共形不变性，将N=4超杨-米尔斯理论中9点振幅的簇代数字母预测转化为QCD中5点和6点过程的类似预测，首次获得了含一个质量外腿的6点过程候选字母，并发现其中包含嵌套平方根。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究的动机是将N=4超杨-米尔斯理论（N=4 super Yang-Mills theory）中基于簇代数（cluster algebra）的振幅字母预测方法应用于量子色动力学（QCD）过程，以探索更广泛理论框架下的振幅结构。

Method: 通过打破对偶共形不变性（dual conformal invariance），将簇代数预测从N=4超杨-米尔斯理论的9点振幅转换到QCD的5点和6点过程，系统分析不同运动学配置下的字母结构。

Result: 首次获得了含一个质量外腿（one massive external leg）的6点过程候选字母，发现其中包含嵌套平方根（nested square roots）。结果包含了相应运动学的所有单圈积分字母，并在无质量极限下与已知的6点无质量QCD过程平面双圈振幅字母一致，同时发现了162个可能在高圈出现的额外字母。对于5点双质量过程，与文献比较显示出非平凡重叠并包含新字母。

Conclusion: 该方法成功将簇代数框架从N=4超杨-米尔斯理论扩展到QCD过程，揭示了QCD振幅字母结构中的复杂数学特征，包括嵌套平方根和可能的高圈贡献，为理解QCD振幅的代数结构提供了新视角。

Abstract: By breaking dual conformal invariance, we transform cluster-algebraic predictions for the alphabet of 9-point amplitudes in $\mathcal{N}=4$ super Yang-Mills theory to analogous predictions for 5- and 6-point processes in QCD. We start by obtaining, for the first time, candidate letters for 6-point processes with one massive external leg, and discover that they surprisingly also contain nested square roots. We confirm that our results essentially contain the alphabet of all 1-loop integrals with these kinematics, and in their massless limit also the recently computed alphabet of finite, planar 2-loop amplitudes for 6-point massless QCD processes. In the latter case, we additionally find 162 letters that may appear at higher loops. We similarly produce candidate letters for 5-point 2-mass processes, whose comparison with the literature reveals a nontrivial overlap that also includes new letters.

### [53] [Precision $YN$ and $\bar{n}N$ measurements with an LH$_2$/LD$_2$ target in the BESIII detector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16075)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出在束流管（beam pipe）与圆柱形气体电子倍增器内径迹仪（Cylindrical Gas Electron Multiplier Inner Tracker, CGEM）之间安装专用液氢或液氘靶。通过蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte Carlo simulations）验证了增加材料对带电粒子径迹重建的影响可忽略不计。

Result: 模拟结果表明，该升级方案可将Λ、Σ⁺、Ξ和反中子（$\bar{n}$）束在自由质子上的有效亮度（effective luminosity）提高10-30倍，从而显著提升相关散射过程的统计精度。

Abstract: Located at the BEPCII $e^{+}e^{-}$ collider, the BESIII experiment provides a robust platform for investigating (anti)hyperon-nucleon ($YN$) and antineutron-nucleon ($\bar{n}N$) interactions. This is made possible by the high production cross-sections of $J/ψ$ and $ψ(3686)$ resonances and their substantial decay branches into these baryons. Although previous studies using the beam pipe as a target demonstrated feasibility, statistical precision remains constrained by the limited material budget. To address this, we propose installing a dedicated liquid hydrogen or liquid deuterium target between the beam pipe and the Cylindrical Gas Electron Multiplier Inner Tracker. Monte Carlo simulations confirm that the added material has a negligible effect on charged particle tracking. This upgrade is expected to enhance the effective luminosity for scattering on free protons by a factor of 10--30 for $Λ$, $Σ^{+}$, $Ξ$, and $\bar{n}$ beams, enabling high-precision measurements of $YN$ and $\bar{n}N$ interactions that will significantly advance our knowledge of non-perturbative strong interactions.

### [54] [Search for direct pair production of top squarks in $pp$ collisions at $\sqrt{s}= 13$ TeV and $13.6$ TeV in events with two oppositely charged leptons using the ATLAS detector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16191)

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 该论文在ATLAS探测器收集的质子-质子对撞数据中，搜索顶标量夸克（top squark）直接成对产生并衰变为两个在壳顶夸克和两个中性微子（neutralino）的信号，未发现显著超出标准模型预期的迹象，并设置了95%置信水平的质量上限。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在通过搜索顶标量夸克（top squark）的直接成对产生过程，来探索超对称理论（supersymmetry）中的参数空间。顶标量夸克是超对称理论中顶夸克（top quark）的超对称伙伴，其衰变到顶夸克和中性微子（neutralino）的通道是寻找超对称粒子的重要途径。

Method: 研究使用ATLAS探测器收集的完整Run 2数据集（质心能量13 TeV，积分亮度140 fb⁻¹）和早期Run 3数据集（质心能量13.6 TeV，积分亮度53 fb⁻¹）。分析针对包含两个带相反电荷轻子（电子或μ子）、b-喷注（b-jet）和大横向动量丢失（missing transverse momentum）的末态。采用基于机器学习（machine-learning）的分类器在广泛的运动学相空间（kinematic phase space）中区分信号和标准模型背景。

Result: 未观察到相对于标准模型预测的显著超出。研究设置了95%置信水平（confidence level）下顶标量夸克和中性微子质量组合的上限，顶标量夸克质量上限可达1060 GeV，中性微子质量上限可达560 GeV。与同一通道中先前的ATLAS分析相比，质量限制提高了约10%。

Conclusion: 该搜索未发现顶标量夸克直接成对产生的证据，但显著提升了质量排除限制，为超对称理论参数空间提供了更严格的约束。

Abstract: This paper presents the search for direct pair production of top squarks decaying into two on-shell top quarks and two neutralinos in final states with two oppositely charged leptons (electrons or muons), $b$-jets and large missing transverse momentum. The search uses the full Run 2 dataset, corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 140 fb$^{-1}$ of proton-proton collisions at a centre-of-mass energy of $\sqrt{s} = 13$ TeV collected by the ATLAS detector from 2015 to 2018, and the early Run 3 dataset, corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 53 fb$^{-1}$ of proton-proton collisions at $\sqrt{s} = 13.6$ TeV collected in 2022 and 2023. Machine-learning-based classifiers are used to distinguish the signal from Standard Model backgrounds, to enhance signal discrimination across a wide kinematic phase space. No significant excess is observed with respect to the Standard Model prediction and 95% confidence level limits are set on top squark and neutralino mass combinations reaching up to 1060 GeV for the former and 560 GeV for the latter, improving mass limits by about 10% compared to previous ATLAS analyses in the same channel.

### [56] [Measurement of the $|V_{cb}|$ element of the CKM matrix in $t\bar{t}$ decays with the ATLAS detector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16414)
*ATLAS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文首次通过在线W玻色子衰变测量CKM夸克混合矩阵元$|V_{cb}|$的大小，在ATLAS实验13 TeV质子-质子对撞数据中获得$|V_{cb}| = (50^{+11}_{-14})\times10^{-3}$的测量值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在开发一种新颖的测量方法，通过高动量转移下的稀有强子衰变$t\rightarrow b\bar{b} c$来测量CKM矩阵元$|V_{cb}|$，这与传统基于低动量转移半轻子B介子衰变的测量方法形成对比。

Method: 利用ATLAS实验在大型强子对撞机（Large Hadron Collider）收集的13 TeV质子-质子对撞数据，对应积分亮度为140 fb$^{-1}$，通过分析$t\bar{t}$事件中的在线W玻色子衰变进行测量。

Result: 测得$|V_{cb}| = (50^{+11}_{-14})\times10^{-3}$，其中不确定度大致均等地来自数据样本的有限大小和系统效应，该结果与在低能标B强子衰变中的现有测量结果一致。

Conclusion: 虽然当前灵敏度尚未超越先前测定方法，但这种新颖方法探测了完全不同的物理情境，为CKM矩阵元测量提供了新的实验途径。

Abstract: The first measurement of the magnitude of the CKM quark mixing matrix element $|V_{cb}|$ using on-shell $W$-boson decays is presented. The measurement is made with $t\bar{t}$ events from $pp$ collision data corresponding to an integrated luminosity of $140$ fb$^{-1}$ at a centre-of-mass energy of 13 TeV collected by the ATLAS experiment at the Large Hadron Collider. A value of: $$|V_{cb}| = (50^{+11}_{-14})\times10^{-3}$$ is measured, where the uncertainties have roughly equal contributions from the limited size of the data sample and from systematic effects. This is consistent with existing measurements made at much lower energy scales in $B$ hadron decays. While the sensitivity does not yet rival that of previous determinations, this novel approach probes a very different physical situation, namely the rare hadronic $t\rightarrow b\bar{b} c$ decay at high momentum-transfer, rather than semileptonic $B$ decays at low momentum-transfer.

</details>

Abstract: The study of the phase transition in planar FK-percolation on the square lattice has seen significant recent breakthroughs. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究方法基于对关联单点函数（associated one-point functions）精确渐近行为的分析。通过推导这些单点函数的渐近公式，为特征值出现在椭圆律支撑集外指定区域的概率计算提供关键工具，从而统一处理谱半径和最右特征值的大偏差问题。

Result: 研究获得了谱半径和最右特征值的上尾大偏差概率（upper tail large deviation probabilities）的渐近公式。更一般地，推导了特征值出现在椭圆律支撑集外指定区域的概率渐近表达式，建立了统一框架，其中谱半径和最右特征值的结果作为特例出现。

Conclusion: 本文为椭圆Ginibre系综在三种对称类中的大偏差概率提供了系统分析框架，其中关联单点函数的精确渐近行为分析具有独立的理论价值。研究结果将谱半径和最右特征值的大偏差问题统一处理，扩展了对随机矩阵特征值分布极限行为的理解。

Abstract: We consider the elliptic Ginibre ensembles in the real, complex and symplectic symmetry classes. As the matrix size tends to infinity, we derive the asymptotic behaviour of the upper tail large deviation probabilities for both the spectral radius and the rightmost eigenvalue. More generally, we obtain asymptotic formulas for the probability that an eigenvalue is found in a prescribed region outside the support of the elliptic law, thereby providing a unified framework in which the results for the spectral radius and the rightmost eigenvalue appear as special cases. The key ingredient of our analysis is the precise asymptotic behaviour of the associated one-point functions, which is of independent interest.

### [60] [AC Fingerprints of 2D Electron Hydrodynamics: Superdiffusion and Drude Weight Suppression](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15737)
*Davis Thuillier,Thomas Scaffidi*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究发现二维费米液体（Fermi liquids）在低频非局域电导中存在一个具有动力学指数z=4/3和超扩散粘度η_⋆的单流体动力学极点，其残差随波矢q以α=1/3的指数衰减，表明动力学性质由两个独立指数描述而非一个。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前研究发现清洁二维费米液体在弹道输运和纳维-斯托克斯（Navier-Stokes）输运之间存在由费米面（Fermi surface）宇称奇多极形变弛豫异常缓慢引起的中介层析（tomographic）区域。本研究旨在探索这一异常是否延伸到动力学领域。

Method: 从微观数值评估线性化电子-电子碰撞算符（electron-electron collision operator）出发，分析有限频率非局域电导（finite-frequency nonlocal conductivity）的低频行为。采用Krylov链（Krylov-chain）描述电流弛豫来解释残差抑制现象。

Result: 发现低频非局域电导由单流体动力学极点控制：σ(q,ω)=𝒟(q)/(iω+η_⋆q^z)，其中动力学指数z=4/3，超扩散粘度η_⋆。极点残差具有尺度依赖性：𝒟(q)∼q^{-α}，α=1/3。这表明动力学性质由两个独立指数而非一个描述。

Conclusion: 随着波矢q增加，最长寿命的准正规模（quasinormal mode）不再是近乎纯电流激发，而是扩展到更高的奇角谐波（odd angular harmonics）。窄通道中的交流输运（AC transport）为分别测量指数z和α提供了直接途径。

Abstract: Clean two-dimensional Fermi liquids are now known to exhibit an intermediate tomographic regime, between ballistic and Navier--Stokes transport, caused by the anomalously slow relaxation of parity-odd multipolar deformations of the Fermi surface. Here we show that this anomaly extends to the dynamical realm. Starting from a microscopic numerical evaluation of the linearized electron--electron collision operator, we find that the finite-frequency nonlocal conductivity is controlled at low frequency by a single hydrodynamic pole, $σ(q,ω)=\mathcal{D}(q)/(iω+η_\star q^z)$, with dynamical exponent $z=4/3$ and superdiffusive viscosity $η_\star$. Remarkably, the pole residue itself is scale dependent and obeys $\mathcal{D}(q)\sim q^{-α}$ with $α=1/3$, so the dynamical properties are described by two separate exponents rather than one. We interpret the residue suppression using a Krylov-chain description of current relaxation: as $q$ increases, the longest-lived quasinormal mode ceases to be a nearly pure current excitation and spreads over higher odd angular harmonics. Finally, we show that AC transport in narrow channels provides a direct route to measuring the exponents $z$ and $α$ separately.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 使用在合成、材料无关数据上训练的神经网络，学习从杂化函数和局域相互作用到格林函数的映射关系。该方法适用于单轨道和多轨道模型，并与数值可控的量子蒙特卡罗（quantum Monte Carlo）方法进行基准测试。

Result: 神经网络求解器能够准确再现莫特相变（Mott transition）、Hubbard-Kanamori模型的多轨道相图，以及SrVO₃和SrMnO₃的电子性质。与量子蒙特卡罗相比，该方法实现了数量级的加速，同时保持了计算精度。

Conclusion: 学习的求解器实现了数量级的加速，能够初始化受控计算，在保持精度的同时显著加速动力学平均场理论计算，为关联材料研究提供了高效的量子杂质求解方案。

Abstract: Quantum impurity solvers are the computational bottleneck of quantum embedding approaches to correlated materials, such as dynamical mean-field theory (DMFT). We show that neural networks trained on synthetic, material-agnostic data learn the impurity mapping from hybridization functions and local interactions to Green's functions with quantitative accuracy for both model systems and real materials, providing fast solvers for single- and multi-orbital models. Benchmarks against numerically controlled quantum Monte Carlo show that the method reproduces the Mott transition, multi-orbital phase diagrams of Hubbard-Kanamori models, and the electronic properties of SrVO$_3$ and SrMnO$_3$. The learned solvers achieve orders-of-magnitude speedup and can initialize controlled calculations, dramatically accelerating DMFT while preserving accuracy.

### [62] [Unified gauge-theory description of quantum spin liquids on square-based frustrated lattices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15745)
*Atanu Maity,Andreas Feuerpfeil,Ronny Thomale,Subir Sachdev,Yasir Iqbal*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该论文提出一个统一框架，将看似不同的量子自旋液体（quantum spin liquids）相联系起来，认为方晶格、Shastry-Sutherland晶格和棋盘晶格上的自旋-1/2海森堡反铁磁体（Heisenberg antiferromagnets）可实现同一类无能隙Z₂狄拉克量子自旋液体相，尽管它们具有显著不同的晶格对称性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子自旋液体通常被认为对晶格几何、对称性和微观交换模式高度敏感，导致在受挫磁体（frustrated magnets）中出现大量看似不同的相。本文旨在提供一个统一框架，将这些从直觉视角看似不同的相联系起来。

Method: 采用系统的投影对称群分析（projective symmetry group analysis），识别出一个棋盘自旋液体态，该态完成了一组封闭的绝热连接相，连接了已确立的方晶格和Shastry-Sutherland自旋液体。研究显示这种晶格层面的统一在连续描述中得到精确反映。

Result: 所有三种情况下的自旋液体都源自共同的SU(2) π-通量母态（π-flux parent state），并由相同的规范理论——具有两个狄拉克费米子味（Dirac fermion flavors）耦合到两个伴随希格斯场（adjoint Higgs fields）的QED₃——所支配。周围的奈尔相（Néel phases）和价键固体相（valence-bond-solid phases）及其禁闭转变（confinement transitions）可在去禁闭量子临界性（deconfined quantum criticality）框架内获得统一解释。

Conclusion: 量子自旋液体最根本的分类依据不是晶格几何或微观耦合，而是涌现的规范理论（emergent gauge theory）及其希格斯结构（Higgs structure）。因此，不同的受挫晶格可以承载相同的量子相并表现出相同的禁闭机制，尽管它们的微观对称性存在显著差异。

Abstract: Quantum spin liquids are commonly thought to be highly sensitive to lattice geometry, symmetry, and microscopic exchange patterns, leading to a proliferation of seemingly distinct phases across frustrated magnets. Here, we provide a framework that unifies phases that appear distinct from the viewpoint of this intuition. We postulate that the spin-$\tfrac{1}{2}$ Heisenberg antiferromagnets on the square, Shastry-Sutherland, and checkerboard lattices can realize a single unified quantum phase: a gapless $\mathbb{Z}_2$ Dirac quantum spin liquid, despite their markedly different lattice symmetries. Using a systematic projective symmetry group analysis, we identify a checkerboard spin-liquid state that completes a closed set of adiabatically connected phases linking the well-established square-lattice and Shastry-Sutherland spin liquids. Crucially, we show that this lattice-level unification is mirrored exactly in the continuum description. In all three cases, the spin liquids descend from a common SU(2) $π$-flux parent state and are governed by the same gauge theory, QED$_3$ with two Dirac fermion flavors coupled to two adjoint Higgs fields. As a result, we postulate that the surrounding Néel and valence-bond-solid phases and their confinement transitions admit a unified interpretation within the framework of deconfined quantum criticality. More broadly, our results suggest that quantum spin liquids are most fundamentally classified not by lattice geometry or microscopic couplings, but by the emergent gauge theory and its Higgs structure. Distinct frustrated lattices can thus host the same quantum phase and exhibit the same confinement mechanisms, despite substantial differences in their microscopic symmetries.

Conclusion: 该半解析框架成功描述了强关联电子系统的关键特征，包括自生局域涨落、扩散阻尼模式和线性温度依赖的电阻行为，为理解极端关联条件下的电子输运提供了理论见解。

Abstract: We have developed a semi-analytical framework formulated in the canonical fermion representation to investigate strongly correlated electron systems. We consider the U=$\infty$ Hubbard model and used the equation of motion method to calculate the fermion self-energy which has two parts: single and two-boson exchange processes. The emergent bosons here are self-generated local charge and spin-density fluctuations which become strongly time-dependent due to extreme correlations. The computed boson spectral density is a diffusive damped mode with a long tail. The electron self-energy at $d=\infty$ is computed self-consistently. The corresponding fermionic spectral density displays a pronounced coherence peak at $ω=0$, while its frequency derivative develops a two-peak structure at finite $ω$. The resistivity shows a linear temperature dependence over a broad range, crossing over to coherent Fermi-liquid behavior at extremely low temperatures.

Abstract: Chirality is a fundamental organizing principle of correlated and topological states. In quantum magnets, chirality arises from the geometric twisting of spins and serves as an emergent source of Berry curvature and quantum metrics. Although external fields can reversibly tune the spin chirality, understanding how spontaneous reversal occurs on macroscopic length scale remains an unresolved challenge. In this letter, we use resonant magnetic x-ray scattering with 2.5-micron spatial resolution to image intertwined spin, charge, and lattice orders of the correlated topological magnet EuAl4. We uncover a macroscopic chirality flipping transition and a remarkable chiral memory effect. The chiral magnetic domain tracks the landscape of the underlying charge density wave, implicating emergent chiral magnetic interactions arising from competing chiral and nematic lattice fields. Our results reveal the fundamental significance of magnetoelastic coupling in stabilizing homochiral and topological magnetic states.

### [65] [Anomalous Thermal Transport Reveals Weak First-Order Melting of Charge Density Waves in 2H-TaSe2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15915)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 低维量子材料中有序相的熔解机制难以解析，因为相关涨落是动态且电中性的。本研究旨在通过热输运测量探测这些隐藏涨落，以理解层状过渡金属二硫化物2H-TaSe2中的电荷密度波（CDW）熔解过程。

Method: 采用热输运测量作为主要探测手段，结合电子衍射（electron diffraction）观察短程周期性晶格畸变，以及X射线衍射（X-ray diffraction）分析CDW波矢的热滞现象。同时建立了将热输运与空间CDW涨落关联的唯象模型。

Result: 观察到热导率呈现显著的V形温度依赖性，无法用传统声子-声子散射解释。电子衍射显示短程周期性晶格畸变持续至至少300K，X射线衍射揭示了CDW波矢的热滞现象。这些结果表明热导率异常源于持续的局域CDW关联散射。

Conclusion: 综合结果表明，2H-TaSe2中的CDW态经历了一种位错和涨落驱动的弱一级熔解（weak first-order melting）。热输运测量为探测低维量子材料中隐藏的动态涨落提供了灵敏探针。

Abstract: How ordered phases melt in low-dimensional quantum materials remain difficult to resolve because the relevant fluctuations are dynamic and charge neutral. In this work, we show that thermal transport provides a sensitive probe of these hidden fluctuations in the layered transition metal dichalcogenide 2H-TaSe2. We observe a striking V-shaped temperature dependence of the thermal conductivity that cannot be explained by conventional phonon-phonon scattering. Instead, it originates from scattering by persistent local charge-density-wave (CDW) correlations, consistent with our phenomenological model linking thermal transport to spatial CDW fluctuation. Electron diffraction reveals short-range periodic lattice distortions persisting to at least 300 K, while X-ray diffraction shows thermal hysteresis of the CDW wavevector. Together, these results reveal a dislocation- and fluctuation-driven weak first-order melting of the CDW state.

</details>


### [66] [Theory of Magnetoacoustic Resonance to Probe Multipole Effects Due to a Crystal Field Quartet](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16087)
*Mikito Koga,Masashige Matsumoto*

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种声学驱动共振新方法，用于探测八极矩自由度以及通常被晶体场四重态磁性性质隐藏的四极矩。该方法通过表面声波传播方向依赖的各向异性共振跃迁速率来表征四极矩特性，并利用八极矩相关的各向异性塞曼分裂进行调制。

Method: 该方法基于声学驱动共振（acoustically driven resonance），利用表面声波（surface acoustic wave）在平行于典型晶轴的外部磁场中的传播方向依赖性。通过分析各向异性共振跃迁速率（anisotropic resonance transition rate），并结合八极矩相关的各向异性塞曼分裂（anisotropic Zeeman splitting）进行调制。对于强磁场下的大激发能隙，提出了基于弗洛凯理论（Floquet theory）的光子辅助磁声共振（photon-assisted magnetoacoustic resonance）。

Result: 该方法能够获取四重态四极矩-应变耦合（quartet quadrupole-strain coupling）的信息，并定量评估各向异性八极矩效应（anisotropic octupole effect）。同时证明了该方法可用于识别多极矩-多极矩相互作用模型（multipole-multipole interaction model）中的四极矩序参量（quadrupole order parameter）。

Conclusion: 本文提出的声学驱动共振方法为探测高阶多极矩自由度提供了有效途径，特别是在强磁场环境下通过光子辅助磁声共振方案扩展了应用范围。该方法能够定量表征四极矩-应变耦合和八极矩效应，并为识别多极矩序参量提供了新工具。

Abstract: We present a new method of acoustically driven resonance that probes octupole degrees of freedom as well as a quadrupole usually hidden by the magnetic properties of a crystal field quartet. A characteristic of the quadrupole is reflected in the anisotropic resonance transition rate, which depends on the propagation direction of a surface acoustic wave under an external magnetic field parallel to a typical crystallographic axis. The transition rate is modulated by the anisotropic Zeeman splitting associated with octupoles. We demonstrate how to obtain information about the quartet quadrupole-strain coupling and evaluate the anisotropic octupole effect quantitatively. We also discuss the applicability of our method to identifying a quadrupole order parameter using a multipole-multipole interaction model. For large excitation energy gaps under strong magnetic fields, we propose a photon-assisted magnetoacoustic resonance formulated on the basis of the Floquet theory.

### [67] [SU($N$) Quantum Spin Model with Weak and Strong First-Order Néel to Valence-Bond Solid Transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16106)
*Ryan Flynn,Anders W. Sandvik*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文引入了一种SU(N)对称的二维量子自旋模型——X-Q模型，该模型在Néel反铁磁态和自发二聚化态之间表现出基态相变。量子蒙特卡洛模拟显示，对于N=2，该模型接近去禁闭量子临界点（deconfined quantum critical point），但对于N>2，相变变为强一级相变，这与传统预期相悖。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在研究SU(N)对称量子自旋模型中基态相变的性质，特别是探索微观相互作用如何影响去禁闭临界性（deconfined criticality）。通过引入X-Q模型，研究者希望理解不同相互作用项对相变行为的影响。

Method: 研究者引入了SU(N)对称的二维X-Q量子自旋模型，其中Q项是两个最近邻单重态投影算符的乘积（类似于J-Q模型），而X项是两个次近邻置换算符的乘积。采用量子蒙特卡洛（quantum Monte Carlo）模拟方法研究该模型的相变行为。

Result: 量子蒙特卡洛模拟显示，对于N=2，X-Q模型接近去禁闭量子临界点，类似于J-Q模型的行为。然而，对于N>2，相变变为强一级相变，这与传统预期（即增加N应减弱不连续性）相反。研究者将此归因于在大N极限下主导相变的X项无法诱导二聚化模式的U(1)涨落。

Conclusion: X-Q模型的研究结果表明，微观相互作用的具体形式对去禁闭临界性的存在至关重要。X项无法诱导二聚化模式的U(1)涨落，这解释了为什么在大N极限下相变变为一级相变，为理解支持去禁闭临界性的微观机制提供了新见解。

Abstract: We introduce an SU($N$) symmetric two-dimensional quantum spin model, the $X$-$Q$ model, which hosts a ground state transition between Néel antiferromagnetic and spontaneously dimerized states. The $Q$ terms are products of two adjacent singlet projectors on nearest-neighbor sites, as in the often studied $J$-$Q$ model (where $J$ is the Heisenberg exchange), while the $X$ terms are products of two permutation operators on second-neighbor sites. Quantum Monte Carlo simulations reveal close proximity to a deconfined quantum critical point for $N=2$, as in the $J$-$Q$ model. However, for $N>2$ the transition becomes strongly first-order, contrary to conventional expectations that increasing $N$ should weaken discontinuities. We attribute this behavior to the inability of the $X$ term, which dominates at the transition for large $N$, to induce U(1) fluctuations of the dimer pattern. These results provide insights into the microscopic interactions that support deconfined criticality.

Conclusion: 该理论揭示了多组分逆流态中Laughlin准粒子分数化的新机制，展示了分数涡旋在不同相中的禁闭与非禁闭行为，为理解拓扑序的多样性和量子相变提供了新视角。

Abstract: A key property of topologically ordered systems, such as Quantum Hall states, is the existence of excitations obeying fractional quantum statistics - anyons. There are two phases, separated by a quantum phase transition, where in the first, although observable, the fractionalized charges are asymptotically confined. In the second phase, they are unconfined anyons and the topological order is different from that of the Laughlin state.

Abstract: Order parameter analysis of the t/U series reveals a uniform altermagnet endemic to the doped Mott insulator, driven by kinetic interactions, occupying a position between the antiferromagnet and hole-doped d-wave superconductor that is normally reserved for the pseudogap. The metastable boundary of the altermagnet punctures and divides the superconductor into underdoped and overdoped regions, reminiscent of the $T^\ast$ crossover or transition in the cuprates. Similarly, the $T_{pair}$ boundary of the superconductor divides the altermagnet, leading to a low temperature phase susceptible to Cooper fluctuations. ### [70] [A Correlated Route to Antiferromagnetic Spintronics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16552)
*Joel Bobadilla,Alberto Camjayi*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 反铁磁体因其无净磁化和超快自旋动力学而成为自旋电子学（spintronics）的有前景平台，但其固有的自旋补偿电子结构限制了其在自旋输运中的主动作用。研究旨在探索反铁磁体中实现自旋极化电荷输运的机制。

Method: 采用掺杂反铁磁哈伯德模型（doped antiferromagnetic Hubbard model），在动力学平均场理论（dynamical mean-field theory）框架下进行研究。通过掺杂打破粒子-空穴对称性（particle-hole symmetry），并施加均匀磁场破坏反铁磁亚晶格等效性。

Result: 电子关联在掺杂远离半填充时产生强烈的自旋依赖散射，而磁场则消除了强制自旋简并输运的剩余对称性。只有当掺杂打破粒子-空穴对称性和外加磁场破坏反铁磁亚晶格等效性相结合时，这些动力学不对称性才会转化为电荷电流的有限自旋极化。

Conclusion: 研究确立了电子关联作为反铁磁自旋电子学的活性成分，并揭示了在结构常规的共线反铁磁体中，与交变磁性（altermagnetic）自旋极化输运的对称性破缺机制相关的关联类比机制。

Abstract: Antiferromagnets offer an attractive platform for spintronics due to their absence of net magnetization and ultrafast spin dynamics, yet their intrinsically spin-compensated electronic structure has traditionally limited their active role in spin transport. Here we identify a minimal, correlation-driven route to spin-polarized charge transport in collinear antiferromagnets. Using the doped antiferromagnetic Hubbard model within dynamical mean-field theory, we show that electronic correlations generate strong spin-dependent scattering upon doping away from half filling, while a uniform magnetic field lifts the residual symmetries that enforce spin-degenerate transport. Only the combined breaking of particle--hole symmetry by doping and of the antiferromagnetic sublattice equivalence by the applied magnetic field converts these dynamical asymmetries into a finite spin polarization of the charge current. Our results establish electronic correlations as an active ingredient for antiferromagnetic spintronics and reveal a correlated analogue of the symmetry-breaking mechanism underlying altermagnetic spin-polarized transport in structurally conventional, collinear antiferromagnets.

Abstract: Mesoscopic transport measurements are underexplored as probes of quasiparticles and their properties in correlated metals. The mixed valence compound YbAl$_3$ exhibits a single-ion Kondo temperature of 670 K, while thermodynamic and transport properties (probed with specific heat, magnetic susceptibility, Hall effect, and resistivity) imply the onset of coherence of heavy fermion quasiparticles at T$* \approx$ 37 K. ### [72] [Quantum Algorithms to Determine Spin-Resolved Exchange-Correlation Potential for Strongly Correlated Materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16605)

Using the Hubbard model as a prototypical strongly correlated lattice system, we prepare ground states in fixed spin sectors through a Hamiltonian variational ansatz combined with a continuation strategy that gradually increases the interaction strength. From the resulting many-body ground states, we extract the XC energy and compute the corresponding spin-resolved XC potentials via finite differences. The accuracy of the approach is benchmarked against exact diagonalization for one- and two-dimensional Hubbard systems of various lattice sizes. We demonstrate that the variational ansatz reproduces the ground-state energies and densities with high fidelity, enabling accurate construction of both magnetic and non-magnetic XC potentials. We analyzed the dependence of the XC potentials on the interaction strength, charge, spin densities, and magnetization. We also present an empirical complexity scaling relation for the computational cost of the method at a fixed fidelity. These results illustrate how quantum simulations can be used to construct spin-resolved XC functionals for correlated lattice models, providing a potential pathway for improving density functional approximations in strongly correlated materials.

Motivation: 交变磁体（altermagnets）作为具有高阶分波型序参量的非常规补偿磁性相，在正常条件下的稳定性引起了从自旋电子学到拓扑和相关量子材料等多个领域的广泛研究兴趣。自旋和角度分辨光电子能谱（SARPES）有望解析与交变磁体实空间自旋序交织的动量依赖自旋织构。

Method: 以α-MnTe交变磁体能带结构中一个节面上的相对论性d波型自旋极化为例，结合第一性原理能带计算和一步光电子发射计算，研究光电子能谱实验中的挑战和数据解释。特别关注光电子发射诱导的电子极化以及光与磁畴奈尔矢量（Néel vector）之间的耦合。

Result: 研究揭示了使用线偏振光时光电子选择规则的异常行为。实验观察并区分了两种不同来源的光电子极化：一种来自样品基态自旋织构，另一种来自光电子发射过程本身。这些实验结果得到了第一性原理能带计算和一步光电子发射计算的支持。

Conclusion: 本研究识别并解决了交变磁体（SARPES）研究中的关键挑战，为数据解释提供了重要见解。通过区分不同来源的光电子极化效应，深化了对交变磁体光电子能谱特征的理解，为这类非常规磁性材料的研究提供了实验和理论框架。

Abstract: Recently discovered altermagnets provide a physical realization of an unconventional compensated magnetic phases with a higher partial-wave type of ordering, reminiscent of unconventional superfluid phases. Their stability under normal conditions has sparked significant research interest, spanning fields from spintronics to topological and correlated quantum materials. Spin- and angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy (SARPES) has great promise to resolve the momentum-dependent spin textures intricately interweaved with the altermagnetic real space spin order. Using the relativistic $d$-wave-like spin polarization on one of the nodal surfaces of the altermagnetic band structure of $α$-MnTe as an example, we here identify and resolve the challenges associated with (S)ARPES studies on altermagnets and offer insights into data interpretation. We focus particularly on the role of photoemission-induced electron polarization and the coupling between light and the Néel vector of a magnetic domain. Our findings reveal an extraordinary behaviour of photoemission selection rules while using linearly-polarized light. We observe, and distinguish, polarization of photoelectrons originating from the sample's ground state spin texture, on one hand, and from the photoemission process, on the other hand. Our experimental results are supported by a combination of ab initio band-structure and 1-step photoemission calculations.

</details>


### [74] [Machine Learning Reconstruction of High-Dimensional Electronic Structure from Angle-Resolved Photoemission Spectroscopy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16725)
*Yu Zhang,Yong Zhong,Nhat Huy Tran,Shuyi Li,Kyuho Lee,Yonghun Lee,Tiffany C. Wang,Harold Y. Hwang,Zhi-Xun Shen,Chunjing Jia*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究开发了一种基于隐式神经表示（implicit neural representations）的深度学习框架，用于从光电子能谱（photoemission spectroscopy）数据中高效提取过渡金属氧化物（transition-metal oxides）的哈密顿量参数（Hamiltonian parameters），相比传统分析方法具有显著优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子材料（quantum materials）的涌现行为由其电子结构决定，可通过光电子能谱技术（photoemission spectroscopy）生成能量-动量四维数据集进行实验探测。然而，从这些高维谱中定量提取哈密顿量参数仍面临重大挑战，目前依赖于劳动密集型、专家依赖的分析而非标准化工作流程。

Method: 研究引入了一种基于隐式神经表示（implicit neural representations）的深度学习框架，用于加速从两类过渡金属氧化物（transition-metal oxides）——钙钛矿镍酸盐（perovskite nickelates）和锰酸盐（manganites）——中提取哈密顿量参数（Hamiltonian parameters）。

Result: 该方法优于传统的分析拟合程序（analytical fitting procedures），在实验费米面拓扑结构（Fermi surface topologies）和能量-动量色散关系（energy-momentum dispersions）方面获得了更优的一致性。

Conclusion: 这项工作突显了深度学习工具在弥合理论与实验之间差距方面的潜力，为量子材料（quantum materials）领域的高通量、自主发现流程（high-throughput, autonomous discovery pipelines）铺平了道路。

Abstract: The emergent behavior of quantum materials is governed by their electronic structure, which can be experimentally probed by photoemission spectroscopy techniques that generate a four-dimensional dataset of energy and momentum. However, the quantitative extraction of Hamiltonian parameters from these high-dimensional spectra remains a significant challenge, currently relying on labor-intensive, expert-dependent analysis rather than standardized workflows. Here, we introduce a deep learning framework based on implicit neural representations to accelerate the retrieval of Hamiltonian parameters in two types of transition-metal oxides: perovskite nickelates and manganites. Our approach outperforms traditional analytical fitting procedures, yielding superior agreement with experimental Fermi surface topologies and energy-momentum dispersions. This work highlights the potential of deep learning tools to bridge the gap between theory and experiment, paving the way for high-throughput, autonomous discovery pipelines in quantum materials.

### [75] [Schrödinger-picture formulation of a scalar quantum field driven by white noise](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15704)
*Pei Wang*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文为受洛伦兹不变白噪声场驱动的标量量子场开发了薛定谔绘景表述，通过随机波泛函描述量子态演化，并获得了精确解以分析量子场的统计特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在为受洛伦兹不变白噪声场（Lorentz-invariant white-noise field）驱动的标量量子场建立薛定谔绘景（Schrödinger-picture）理论框架，研究随机演化下的量子态动力学。

Method: 采用随机波泛函（stochastic wave functional）描述系统量子态，其演化遵循随机薛定谔方程（stochastic Schrödinger equation）。证明高斯结构在随机演化下保持不变，将动力学简化为相应核函数（kernel functions）的方程组。

Result: 精确求解核方程，获得了波泛函的显式时间依赖表达式。场算符期望值满足与经典场相同的随机方程，且从随机波泛函计算的能量密度（energy density）的系综平均与相应林德布拉德方程（Lindblad equation）结果一致。

Conclusion: 尽管某些导出可观测量因白噪声理想化而呈现紫外发散（ultraviolet divergences），随机量子态仍保持良好定义，且能量产生率与林德布拉德方程结果相符，验证了理论框架的自洽性。

Abstract: We develop a Schrödinger-picture formulation for a scalar quantum field driven by a Lorentz-invariant white-noise field. The quantum state of the system is described by a stochastic wave functional that evolves according to a stochastic Schrödinger equation. We show that the Gaussian structure of the wave functional is preserved under the stochastic evolution, allowing the dynamics to be reduced to a set of equations for the corresponding kernel functions. These kernel equations are derived and solved exactly, yielding an explicit time-dependent expression for the wave functional. The exact solution enables a direct analysis of the statistical properties of the quantum field in the space of field configurations. In particular, we show that the expectation value of the field operator obeys the same stochastic equation as the classical field obtained from the Euler-Lagrange equation of the action. We further compute the energy density from the stochastic wave functional and evaluate its ensemble average over noise realizations. The resulting energy production rate coincides with that obtained from the corresponding Lindblad equation. This result indicates that the stochastic quantum state remains well defined even though certain derived observables exhibit ultraviolet divergences associated with the white-noise idealization.

</details>


### [76] [CSS codes from the Bruhat order of Coxeter groups](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16036)
*Kamil Bradler*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于Coxeter群和Bruhat偏序（Bruhat order）生成CSS量子纠错码（CSS codes）家族的方法，能够控制稳定子权重（stabilizer weights）或产生高度不规则的权重分布。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究的动机是利用Coxeter群（包括有限和无限、可约或不可约）及其特有的Bruhat偏序结构来设计量子纠错码。Bruhat偏序作为面偏序集（face poset）能够捕捉正则CW复形（regular CW complex）的p维胞腔包含关系，这一特性使其在量子纠错码设计中具有重要价值。

Method: 方法基于Coxeter群特有的Bruhat面偏序区间结构，将相应的链复形（chain complexes）转化为多种CSS码。针对不同需求，作者开发了控制稳定子权重的编码方法，并为处理罕见重稳定子（heavy stabilizers）开发了权重约减方法（weight-reduction method）。

Result: 研究获得了多种CSS码及其家族，包括具有受控稳定子权重的编码如[6006, 924, {≤14,≤7}]（稳定子权重14和9）和[22880,3432,{≤8,≤16}]（权重16和10），以及具有高度不规则稳定子权重分布的编码如[571,199,{5,5}]。此外，还展示了如何提取四元（长度三）链复形，这些可解释为带有元校验（metacheck）的CSS码。

Conclusion: 该研究证明Coxeter群和Bruhat偏序结构为生成具有有趣编码参数的CSS码家族提供了系统方法，能够实现稳定子权重的控制或产生特定的不规则分布，并扩展至包含元校验的更复杂编码结构。

Abstract: I introduce a method to generate families of CSS codes with interesting code parameters. The object of study is Coxeter groups, both finite and infinite (reducible or not), and a geometrically motivated partial order of Coxeter group elements named after Bruhat. The Bruhat order is known to provide a link to algebraic topology -- it doubles as a face poset capturing the inclusion relations of the $p$-dimensional cells of a regular CW~complex and that is what makes it interesting for QEC code design. Assisted by the Bruhat face poset interval structure unique to Coxeter groups I show that the corresponding chain complexes can be turned into multitudes of CSS codes. Depending on the approach, I obtain CSS codes (and their families) with controlled stabilizer weights, for example $[6006, 924, \{{\leq14},{\leq7}\}]$ (stabilizer weights~14 and 9) and $[22880,3432,\{{\leq8},{\leq16}\}]$ (weights 16 and 10), and CSS codes with highly irregular stabilizer weight distributions such as $[571,199,\{5,5\}]$. For the latter, I develop a weight-reduction method to deal with rare heavy stabilizers. Finally, I show how to extract four-term (length three) chain complexes that can be interpreted as CSS codes with a metacheck.

</details>


### [77] [Quantum classification and search algorithms using spinorial representations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16564)
*Lauro Mascarenhas,Vinicius N. A. Lula-Rocha,Marco A. S. Trindade*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于克利福德代数（Clifford algebra）和旋量表示（spinorial representation）的代数框架，统一描述了量子分类算法和非均匀初始分布的量子搜索算法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在为两种不同的量子算法提供统一的代数描述框架：量子分类算法和具有非均匀初始分布的量子搜索算法。通过克利福德代数及其旋量表示，为这两种算法建立共同的数学基础。

Method: 利用克利福德代数的旋量表示性质，在分类算法中构造与不同类别关联的正交量子态，通过评估从克利福德代数生成元导出的算符期望值来识别项目类别。在搜索算法中，直接使用克利福德代数的生成元实现预言机（oracle），简化了具有先验信息数据库的实现。

Result: 提出的方法为两种算法提供了统一的代数描述，在量子态和算符的构造中都使用了旋量表示。论文还展示了计算实现的具体方案。

Conclusion: 基于克利福德代数和旋量表示的代数框架成功统一了量子分类和量子搜索算法，为这两种量子算法的实现提供了简化的数学描述和实现途径。

Abstract: We propose an algebraic formulation for two distinct quantum algorithms: a quantum classification algorithm and a quantum search algorithm with a non-uniform initial distribution, both based on Clifford algebras and spinorial representations. In the classification algorithm, we exploit properties of spinorial representations to construct orthogonal quantum states associated with different classes, allowing the identification of an item's class through the evaluation of expectation values of operators derived from the generators of the Clifford algebra. In the quantum search algorithm, we consider a database with prior information in which the oracle is implemented directly using generators of the Clifford algebra, simplifying its realization. The proposed approach provides a unified algebraic description for both algorithms, employing spinorial representations in the construction of quantum states and operators. Computational implementations are presented.

### [78] [An asymmetry lower bound on fermionic non-Gaussianity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16762)
*Filiberto Ares,Michele Mazzoni,Sara Murciano,Dávid Szász-Schagrin,Pasquale Calabrese,Lorenzo Piroli*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文建立了费米子高斯态（fermionic Gaussian states）的非高斯性（non-Gaussianity）度量与粒子数分布香农熵（Shannon entropy）之间的理论联系，并推导出基于该熵的指数形式的非高斯性相对熵下界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 费米子高斯态是多体物理中的基本工具，能精确描述非相互作用量子系统并支持高效数值模拟。因此，量化任意多体波函数与高斯态之间的差异（即非高斯性）具有重要意义。

Method: 通过理论推导，将非高斯性度量与粒子数分布的香农熵联系起来，该熵对于纯态等同于粒子数不对称性（particle-number asymmetry）。基于（混合）费米子高斯态的粒子数分布集中性质，推导出非高斯性相对熵的下界。

Result: 获得了以香农熵指数形式表示的非高斯性相对熵下界，并在大系统尺寸下数值研究了该边界的紧致性。该下界在不对称性较大时非平凡，且依赖于粒子数分布的集中特性。

Conclusion: 由于粒子数分布的香农熵通常易于计算或实验测量，该结果为非高斯性提供了实用的下界估计方法，揭示了非高斯性与粒子数不对称性之间的非平凡相互作用。

Abstract: Fermionic Gaussian states are a fundamental tool in many-body physics, faithfully representing non-interacting quantum systems and allowing for efficient numerical simulations. Given a many-body wave function, it is therefore interesting to ask how much it differs from that of a Gaussian state, as quantified by the notion of non-Gaussianity. In this work, we relate measures of non-Gaussianity with the Shannon entropy of the particle-number distribution, coinciding with the particle-number asymmetry for pure states. We derive a lower bound on the relative entropy of non-Gaussianity in terms of the exponential of the Shannon entropy, and study numerically its tightness for large system sizes. Our bound is non-trivial for large values of the asymmetry and relies on the concentration of the particle-number distribution of (mixed) fermionic Gaussian states. Since the Shannon entropy of the particle-number distribution is often efficient to compute or experimentally measure, our results can be viewed as a practical way to lower bound non-Gaussianity, highlighting a non-trivial interplay with particle-number asymmetry.

### [79] [Geometric phase for an accelerated two-level atom in AdS spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16084)
*Linghui Qiu,Jialin Zhang,Hongwei Yu*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了在反德西特（Anti-de Sitter）时空中，匀加速两能级原子与无质量共形标量场真空涨落耦合时获得的几何相位（geometric phase）。研究揭示了亚临界和超临界加速度之间的显著差异，并发现边界条件对相位修正有重要影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机是探究在反德西特（AdS）时空中，匀加速两能级原子与无质量共形标量场真空涨落耦合时获得的几何相位。特别关注不同边界条件（Dirichlet、透明和Neumann）对相位的影响，以及加速度临界值对系统行为的区分。

Method: 采用开放量子系统（open-quantum-system）形式体系，计算了在反德西特时空边界施加三种不同边界条件（Dirichlet、透明和Neumann）下的几何相位。研究对比了亚临界和超临界加速度情况下的相位行为。

Result: 研究结果揭示了亚临界和超临界加速度之间的显著差异：亚临界时原子近似孤立演化，几何相位与AdS半径和加速度均无关；超临界时出现拓扑-加速度诱导的相位修正，且强烈依赖于边界条件。当AdS半径小于原子固有波长时，大加速度下的修正幅度遵循Neumann>透明>Dirichlet的排序。在原子权重参数有限区间内，Dirichlet和Neumann边界条件比透明情况产生更丰富的峰值结构，具体模式由加速度与原子能隙（energy gap）的竞争决定。对于超临界区的透明边界条件，AdS相位修正与德西特（dS）对应情况非常相似。

Conclusion: 研究表明，在反德西特时空中，匀加速原子的几何相位行为存在临界加速度的区分。边界条件对超临界加速度下的相位修正具有决定性影响，且AdS与dS时空在透明边界条件下的相位修正表现出相似性。这些发现揭示了时空几何、边界条件和加速度之间的复杂相互作用。

Abstract: We have investigated the geometric phase acquired by a uniformly accelerated two-level atom coupled to vacuum fluctuations of a massless conformal scalar field in Anti-de Sitter (AdS) spacetime. Using the open-quantum-system formalism, we calculate the phase under three boundary conditions (Dirichlet, transparent and Neumann) imposed on the field at the AdS boundary. Our findings reveal a sharp distinction between subcritical and supercritical accelerations. For subcritical accelerations, the atom evolves effectively as an isolated system, and the geometric phase is independent of both the AdS radius and the acceleration. For supercritical accelerations, however, topology-acceleration-induced phase corrections emerge and display pronounced boundary-condition dependence. When the AdS radius is smaller than the atomic proper wavelength, the magnitude of the correction at large accelerations follows the ordering Neumann$>$transparent$>$Dirichlet. Moreover, over a finite interval of the atomic weight parameter, both Dirichlet and Neumann boundary conditions produce a richer peak structure in the phase correction than the transparent case, with the detailed pattern governed by the competition between the acceleration and the atomic energy gap. Finally, for transparent boundary conditions in the supercritical regime, the AdS phase correction closely resembles its de Sitter (dS) counterpart.

</details>


### [80] [Decoherence and the Reemergence of Coherence From a Superconducting "Horizon"](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16765)
*Eric J. Sung,Charles A. Stafford*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究在超导类比黑洞事件视界的系统中，分析了安德烈夫反射（Andreev reflection）引起的退相干现象，发现弱耦合时存在类似DSW退相干的效应，但强耦合时通过安德烈夫束缚态（Andreev bound states）的共振隧穿会重新出现相干性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Danielson等人近期研究表明黑洞存在会导致量子叠加态的普遍退相干（DSW退相干），这一结果对量子力学与引力的相互作用具有深远意义。本研究旨在通过超导类比系统分析类似现象，为在地球上研究黑洞量子物理开辟新途径。

Method: 研究分析了arXiv:1709.06154中描述的黑洞事件视界超导类比系统，其中安德烈夫反射扮演霍金辐射（Hawking radiation）的角色。考虑了一个由阿哈罗诺夫-玻姆（Aharonov-Bohm）磁通穿过的正常金属干涉仪，其中干涉仪的一条臂通过可变强度的隧道耦合与超导体连接。

Result: 在绝对零度和弱耦合条件下，干涉仪的散射态因安德烈夫反射而退相干，这是类似黑洞事件视界DSW退相干的邻近效应（proximity effect）的非平凡表现。然而，随着与超导体耦合强度的增加，通过安德烈夫束缚态的共振隧穿（resonant tunneling）会重新出现相干性。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明可能存在一种类比引力现象：在黑洞事件视界几个康普顿波长（Compton wavelengths）范围内的干涉仪中，通过虚拟霍金辐射介导的传输会导致相干性的重新出现。这些结果为通过类比研究在地球上探索黑洞量子物理开辟了新路径。

Abstract: In a recent paper arXiv:2205.06279, Danielson et al. demonstrated that the mere presence of a black hole causes universal decoherence of quantum superpositions (dubbed the DSW decoherence). This result has profound implications for the interplay of quantum mechanics and gravity. We analyze decoherence in a superconducting analogue arXiv:1709.06154 of the event horizon of a black hole, where Andreev reflection plays the role of Hawking radiation. We consider a normal metal interferometer threaded by an Aharonov-Bohm flux, where one of the arms of the interferometer is coupled to a superconductor by a tunnel coupling of varying strength. At absolute zero and for weak coupling, we find that the scattering states of the interferometer are decohered by Andreev reflection, a nontrivial manifestation of the proximity effect analogous to DSW decoherence from the event horizon of a black hole. However, for increasing coupling strength to the superconductor, we find a reemergence of coherence via resonant tunneling through Andreev bound states. This suggests the existence of an analogue gravitational phenomenon wherein transmission mediated by virtual Hawking radiation leads to a reemergence of coherence in an interferometer placed within a few Compton wavelengths of a black hole's event horizon. Our results open a new path to study black hole quantum physics on earth via analogue studies.

</details>


### [81] [Measurement-Based Estimation of Causal Conditional Variances and Its Application to Macroscopic quantum phenomenon](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16821)
*Kosei Hatakeyama,Ryotaro Fukuzumi,Akira Matsumura,Daisuke Miki,Kazuhiro Yamamoto*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种基于零差测量记录的机械振子量子估计方法，通过构建相对估计算子并分析其方差，证明了在典型量子态制备的实验相关参数范围内，重构偏差可忽略不计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 仅基于测量记录进行估计的重要性在于，它能够在无需假设真实系统状态知识的情况下实现态验证。该方法建立在C.Meng等人（Science Advances 8, 7585 (2022)）开发的框架基础上。

Method: 从因果和反因果量子维纳滤波器（quantum Wiener filters）构建相对估计算子（relative estimate operator），并计算其方差。将偏离因果条件方差（causal conditional variance）的部分定义为重构偏差（reconstruction bias），并对其大小进行解析评估。

Result: 研究表明，在典型量子态制备的实验相关参数范围内，重构偏差足够小，可以忽略不计。该方法被应用于电磁相互作用介导的宏观量子纠缠（macroscopic quantum entanglement）和零差检测生成的条件动量压缩态（conditional momentum-squeezed states）的提案验证。

Conclusion: 该方法阐明了重构偏差保持可忽略的条件，以及偏差变得显著的情况，为基于测量记录的量子态验证提供了理论依据和实用指导。

Abstract: We analytically investigate a quantum estimation method for a mechanical oscillator in a detuned cavity system based solely on homodyne measurement records, building on the framework developed by C.Meng et al. (Science Advances 8, 7585 (2022)). Estimation based only on measurement records is important because it enables state verification without assuming knowledge of the true system state. We construct a relative estimate operator from causal and anti-causal quantum Wiener filters and calculate its variance. The deviation from the causal conditional variance is defined as a reconstruction bias, whose magnitude is evaluated analytically. We show that, within experimentally relevant parameter regimes for typical quantum-state preparation, the reconstruction bias is sufficiently small to be neglected. As applications to state verification, we apply the method to proposals for macroscopic quantum entanglement mediated by electromagnetic interactions and for conditional momentum-squeezed states generated by homodyne detection, and clarify the conditions under which the bias remains negligible and when the reconstruction bias becomes significant.

</details>


### [82] [Entanglement advantage in sensing power-law spatiotemporal noise correlations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15742)
*Yu-Xin Wang,Anthony J. Brady,Federico Belliardo,Alexey V. Gorshkov*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了量子传感器在探测时空相关噪声时的基本灵敏度极限，证明了在特定条件下纠缠传感器相对于非纠缠传感器的可扩展优势，并揭示了非马尔可夫性如何改变纠缠优势的本质。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究计算了量子传感器探测时空相关噪声（spatiotemporally correlated noise）的基本灵敏度极限。首先分别证明了使用纠缠和非纠缠传感器探测空间相关马尔可夫噪声（spatially correlated Markovian noise）的基本量子极限。特别关注幂律空间噪声关联（power-law spatial noise correlations），这在具有长程相互作用和/或接近临界点的凝聚态系统中自然出现。

Result: 当幂律衰减缓慢时，研究推导出了可扩展的纠缠优势（scalable entanglement advantage）。对于具有1/f^p型频谱的目标信号，研究证明非马尔可夫性（non-Markovianity）可能完全改变估计空间噪声关联时纠缠优势的本质。

Conclusion: 所提出的协议可在固态缺陷、超导电路和中性原子等前沿量子传感平台上实现，为利用量子资源增强相关噪声探测提供了理论基础和实验指导。

Abstract: Noise sensing underlies many physical applications including tests of non-classicality, thermometry, verification of correlated phases of quantum matter, and characterization of criticality. While previous works have shown that quantum resources such as entanglement and squeezing can enhance the sensitivity in estimating deterministic signals, less is known about the entanglement advantage in sensing correlated stochastic signals (noise). In this work, we compute the fundamental sensitivity limits of quantum sensors in probing spatiotemporally correlated noise. We first prove the fundamental quantum limits in sensing spatially correlated Markovian noise using entangled and unentangled sensors, respectively. Focusing on power-law spatial noise correlations, which naturally arise in condensed matter systems with long-range interactions and/or near criticality, we further derive a scalable entanglement advantage when the power-law decays slowly. Then, considering a target signal with a $1/f^{p}$-type spectrum, we demonstrate that non-Markovianity may entirely modify the nature of entanglement advantage in estimating spatial noise correlations. Our protocols can be implemented using state-of-the-art quantum sensing platforms including solid-state defects, superconducting circuits, and neutral atoms.

### [84] [Post-selected Criticality in Measurement-induced Phase Transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15744)
*Dolly Nambi,Kabir Khanna,Andrew Allocca,Thomas Iadecola,Ciarán Hickey,Romain Vasseur,Justin H. Wilson*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 测量诱导相变（MIPT）通常基于典型测量结果的条件轨迹进行研究，但这些轨迹通常只能通过后选择（post-selection）访问。本文旨在探究显式后选择如何改变相变的本质。

Method: 采用强制测量（forced measurements）来研究后选择对相变的影响，通过重新加权原本稀有的轨迹来分析相变性质的变化。同时将后选择的MIPT与随机张量网络（Random Tensor Networks, RTN）的纠缠相变进行比较。

Result: 后选择通过重新加权稀有轨迹，从根本上改变了相变的普适类：获得相关长度指数ν≈2.1（大于标准MIPT）和负的有效中心电荷c_eff≈-0.4。后选择的MIPT与RTN的纠缠相变属于同一普适类。此外发现，在时间周期、平移不变的电路中，至少需要三维（qutrits）而非二维（qubits）的局部维度才能诱导相变。

Abstract: Information-theoretic phase transitions, such as the measurement-induced phase transition (MIPT), characterize the robustness of quantum dynamics to local monitoring and are naturally formulated in terms of trajectories conditioned on typical measurement outcomes, which are naively accessible only through post-selection. Here we implement forced measurements to investigate how explicit post-selection alters the nature of the transition. We find that post-selection fundamentally alters the universality class by reweighting trajectories that are otherwise rare. In particular, we obtain a correlation-length exponent $ν\approx 2.1$ larger than that of the standard MIPT and a negative effective central charge $c_\mathrm{eff}\approx -0.4$. We also compare the post-selected MIPT to the entanglement transition of Random Tensor Networks (RTN), and demonstrate that their universality class is the same. This setup further allows time-periodic, translationally-invariant circuits with post-selected weak measurements. In both models, we find that an onsite dimension of at least 3 (qutrits but not qubits) is necessary to induce a transition.

Exceptions include fluctuations at infinite temperature, at critical points, and in semiclassical systems. ### [86] [Role of spectral structure in adiabatic ground-state preparation of the XXZ model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15794)
*Francisco Albarrán-Arriagada,Juan Carlos Retamal*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了各向异性海森堡（XXZ）模型中绝热基态制备的效率限制，发现性能主要受基态与激发态之间的谱简并（spectral degeneracies）制约，并提出通过初始哈密顿量优化或位点依赖的塞曼场（site-dependent Zeeman fields）来抑制临界交叉（critical crossings）的简单策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 绝热基态制备（adiabatic ground-state preparation）的效率受限于含时哈密顿量的谱结构，特别是能隙减小和简并性（degeneracies）引发的非绝热跃迁（nonadiabatic transitions）。研究旨在通过各向异性海森堡（XXZ）模型这一严格基准，探索克服这些限制的策略。

Method: 在八位点环（eight-site ring）上的各向异性海森堡（XXZ）模型中，比较了三种策略：初始哈密顿量优化（optimization of the initial Hamiltonian）、添加辅助项（addition of auxiliary terms）以及近似反绝热驱动（approximate counterdiabatic driving）。该模型因低能态间的各向异性依赖能级交叉（anisotropy-dependent level crossings）而成为严格基准。

Result: 研究发现性能主要受基态与激发态之间的谱简并（spectral degeneracies）约束。初始哈密顿量优化或位点依赖的塞曼场（site-dependent Zeeman fields）等简单策略能抑制临界交叉（critical crossings），显著提升基态制备效率。相比之下，当谱结构仍存在能级交叉时，反绝热项（counterdiabatic terms）单独使用无法改善协议，仅在简并被移除后才有效。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，谱工程（spectral engineering）是实现相互作用自旋系统中高效绝热基态制备的先决条件。通过操控哈密顿量的谱结构来消除简并性，是提升绝热量子计算协议性能的关键途径。

Abstract: Adiabatic ground-state preparation is fundamentally limited by the spectral structure of the time-dependent Hamiltonian, particularly by gap reductions and degeneracies that induce nonadiabatic transitions. We examine this dependence in the anisotropic Heisenberg (XXZ) model on an eight-site ring by comparing three strategies: optimization of the initial Hamiltonian, addition of auxiliary terms, and considering approximate counterdiabatic driving. Owing to anisotropy-dependent level crossings among low-energy states, the XXZ model provides a stringent benchmark. We find that performance is mainly constrained by spectral degeneracies between the ground and excited states. Simple strategies such as initial-Hamiltonian optimization or site-dependent Zeeman fields, suppresses critical crossings and drastically enhance ground-state preparation. In contrast, counterdiabatic terms alone do not improve the protocol when the spectral structure remains level-crossings, becoming effective only after degeneracies are removed. These results identify spectral engineering as a prerequisite for efficient adiabatic ground-state preparation in interacting spin systems.

### [88] [Qudit Implementation of the Rodeo Algorithm for Quantum Spectral Filtering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16049)

Abstract: Qudits, the multi-level generalization of qubits, provide a natural extension of the binary paradigm in quantum computation and offer new opportunities to enhance algorithmic performance. Beyond their direct applicability to the simulation of multi-level quantum systems, higher-dimensional ancillae can improve sampling efficiency in quantum algorithms by enabling the simultaneous implementation of multiple control operations, thereby reducing circuit complexity. In this work, we pursue three main objectives. First, we present a formulation of the Rodeo algorithm employing a general $d$-level ancilla qudit. Second, we introduce the concept of the \emph{Rodeo kernel}, defined as a two-frequency interferometer, which acts as a spectral filter in the energy domain. Finally, we propose a microcanonical protocol for the Rodeo algorithm. Our results show that the qudits provide a framework for spectral analysis and thermodynamic characterization of multi-level quantum systems.

### [89] [Uncertainty Relation for Entropy and Temperature of Gibbs States](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16456)
*Francis J. Headley*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文推导了吉布斯态中熵估计的量子费希尔信息（quantum Fisher information），发现熵与温度的费希尔信息互为对偶关系，并建立了与勒让德共轭（Legendre conjugacy）相关的普适不确定性关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索熵估计的量子计量学基础，揭示熵与温度在费希尔信息层面的对偶关系，并建立与热力学勒让德共轭相关的普适不确定性原理。

Method: 通过推导吉布斯态（Gibbs state）中熵估计的量子费希尔信息，分析其与温度费希尔信息的对偶关系，并利用勒让德共轭原理建立普适的不确定性关系。

Result: 发现熵费希尔信息 $F_s = 1/C_v$ 与温度费希尔信息 $F_S = C_v/T^2$ 互为对偶，其乘积 $F_S·F_T = 1/T^2$ 与哈密顿量无关，导出了普适的不确定性关系 $Δ^2 S\,Δ^2 T ≥ T^2/n^2$。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了熵与温度估计的普适不确定性关系，验证了能量测量是熵估计的最优协议，并将结果推广到正则系综（grand canonical ensemble）和广义吉布斯系综（generalised Gibbs ensembles）。

Abstract: We derive the quantum Fisher information for entropy estimation in a Gibbs state and show that $F_s = 1/C_v$, dual to the temperature Fisher information $F_S = C_v/T^2$. Their product $F_S\cdot F_T = 1/T^2$ is independent of the Hamiltonian, yielding the universal uncertainty relation $Δ^2 S\,Δ^2 T \geq T^2/n^2$ in which all system-specific quantities such as heat capacity, the Hamiltonian, and the number of degrees of freedom cancel identically. This is the metrological expression of the Legendre conjugacy between $S$ and $T$. We identify energy measurement as the optimal protocol for entropy estimation, analyse critical-point scaling where $F_S \sim |t|^α\to 0$, and connect $F_S$ to the Ruppeiner metric in entropy coordinates. The uncertainty relation is shown to hold for all standard thermodynamic conjugate pairs, and we examine the distinguished role of the von~Neumann entropy within the Rényi family. Generalisations to the grand canonical and generalised Gibbs ensembles are given.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于模拟量子退火系统在量子相变过程中的动力学行为，特别关注从顺磁相到自旋玻璃相的转变，以及Kibble-Zurek幂律在残余能量预测中的适用性。

Method: 采用三维张量网络方法，将系统表示为张量积态（tensor product state），即二维情况下的投影纠缠对态（PEPS）。针对无限周期边界晶格使用确定性方法，而对有限开放边界晶格则引入更高效的蒙特卡洛采样方法。

Result: 研究结果显示，随着退火时间的增加，残余能量作为退火时间的函数逐渐趋近于Kibble-Zurek幂律预测，验证了该理论在量子退火动力学中的适用性。

Conclusion: 通过三维张量网络模拟证实，在立方晶格随机伊辛模型的量子退火过程中，残余能量随退火时间的变化遵循Kibble-Zurek幂律，为量子退火系统的动力学行为提供了理论验证。

Abstract: Quantum annealing with the D-Wave Advantage system in the random Ising model on a cubic lattice is simulated using a three-dimensional (3D) tensor network. The Hamiltonian is driven across a quantum phase transition from a paramagnetic phase to a spin-glass phase. The network is represented as a tensor product state, also known-particularly in two dimensions-as a projected entangled-pair state (PEPS). The annealing procedure is repeated for a range of annealing times in order to test the Kibble-Zurek (KZ) power law governing the residual energy at the end of the annealing ramp. For an infinite lattice with periodic nearest-neighbor random Ising couplings, the final energy is evaluated using a deterministic method. For a finite lattice with open boundaries, we introduce a more efficient Monte Carlo sampling approach. In both cases, the residual energy as a function of annealing time approaches the KZ power law as the annealing time increases.

### [91] [Dark state role in time-reversal symmetry breaking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16512)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于理解全局驱动相位Φ在相干控制原子、分子和固态平台中的核心作用，特别是在具有闭环耦合的系统中，外部驱动场会引发强烈影响种群转移和时间演化对称性的干涉效应。

Method: 研究方法聚焦于相位反转（或哈密顿量复共轭）这一限制较少的变换，分析了三能级和四能级系统，并推导了适用于一般n能级配置（n为偶数）的种群相位对称性（PΦS）的普遍条件。

Result: 研究结果表明，暗态（旁观态）的存在是种群相位对称性的充分条件，因为它将动力学约束到以SU(2)或开环SU(3)演化为特征的简化子空间，这些发现为量子信息处理和量子计算中的鲁棒控制提供了实用指南。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了在存在暗态时种群动力学对全局驱动相位的对称性，为量子系统的鲁棒控制提供了理论基础和实用指导，具有在量子信息处理和量子计算中的潜在应用价值。

Abstract: We investigate the role of the global driving phase $Φ$ in the dynamics of driven few-level quantum systems, a central setting in coherent control of atomic, molecular, and solid-state platforms. In particular, we focus on systems with closed-loop couplings, where external driving fields induce interference effects that strongly influence population transfer and symmetry properties of time-evolution. While full time-reversal symmetry requires $Φ=0,π$, leading to a real Hamiltonian, we focus on a less restrictive transformation, the phase inversion (or complex conjugation of the Hamiltonian), under which population dynamics can remain symmetric even though coherences generally do not. We show that the presence of a dark (spectator) state is a sufficient condition for this population phase symmetry (P$Φ$S), as it constrains the dynamics to reduced subspaces characterized by SU(2) or open-loop SU(3) evolution. We analyze this mechanism in three- and four-level systems and derive general conditions for P$Φ$S that extend to generic $n$-level configurations, with $n$ even. These findings provide practical guidelines for achieving robust control in quantum systems, with potential applications in quantum information processing and quantum computing.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在解决在单光子水平检测巡游微波辐射（itinerant microwave radiation）的挑战，现有技术需要更高效、低噪声的检测方案。

Method: 利用现有的约瑟夫森光子学器件（Josephson-photonics devices），其中两个微波腔通过直流电压偏置的超导结耦合，理论展示了如何实现频闪重复的近投影测量。通过结的磁通控制优化测量速率、持续时间和强度，并开发阈值协议从另一个腔的辐射输出的零差测量中检测光子。

Abstract: We present a novel scheme to detect itinerant microwave radiation at the single photon level. Using existing Josephson-photonics devices, where two microwave cavities are coupled by a dc-voltage biased superconducting junction, we theoretically show how to implement a stroboscopically repeated, near-projective measurement of a photon impinging on one of the cavities. Optimizing rate, duration, and strength of the measurement by flux control of the junction and developing a threshold protocol to detect the photon from a homodyne measurement of the radiation output of the other cavity, we achieve highly efficient detection with low dark counts. By cascading the detector with a preamplifier, where a similar two-cavity Josephson-photonics device acts as a photon multiplier, we can further improve the device to reach a detection efficiency of $88.5 \%$ with a dark count rate of $\sim10^{-4} γ_a$, set by the resonance width $γ_a$ of the absorbing cavity. These results for a multiplication factor of two suggest that near-unity efficiencies may be reached for higher multiplication factors.

### [93] [FAlCon: A unified framework for algorithmic control of quantum dot devices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16650)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: FAlCon提供三个核心组件：(1) 用于以硬件无关形式表达基于状态的调谐逻辑的轻量级领域特定语言；(2) 包含物理信息量子点数据结构的可传输专用库（"调谐方言"）；(3) 支持可互操作实验室无关测量堆栈的可扩展共享测量协议库。

Result: 通过将算法意图与仪器实现分离，同时保持可追溯性并支持类型化脚本，FAlCon使研究人员和工程师能够在异构量子点设置间交换、适配和部署表征与自动调谐例程。该框架支持从使用预构建算法的终端用户到扩展仪器支持和贡献新调谐策略的开发者的所有用户。

Conclusion: 虽然当前版本针对量子点实验，但其他量子比特（qubit）模式和其他科学实验可以通过提供新的调谐数据类型和仪器控制模板来重用FAlCon的模块化抽象，展示了该框架的广泛适用性。

Abstract: As spin-based quantum systems scale, their setup and control complexity increase sharply. In semiconductor quantum dot (QD) experiments, device-to-device variability, heterogeneous control-electronics stacks, and differing operational modalities make it difficult to reuse characterization, calibration, and control logic across laboratories. We present FAlCon, an open-source software ecosystem for portable, automated characterization and tuning measurement workflows. FAlCon provides (i) a lightweight domain-specific language for expressing state-based tuning logic in a hardware-agnostic form; (ii) specialized transmittable libraries of physics-informed QD data structures (``tuning vernacula''); and (iii) extensible libraries of shared measurement protocols enabling an interoperable lab-agnostic measurement stack. By separating algorithm intent from instrument realization, while preserving traceability and supporting typed scripting, FAlCon enables researchers and engineers to exchange, adapt, and deploy characterization and autotuning routines across heterogeneous QD setups. The framework supports all users, ranging from end users running prebuilt algorithms with custom initial conditions to developers extending instrumentation support and contributing new tuning strategies. Although the present release targets QD experiments, other qubit modalities and scientific experiments could reuse FAlCon's modular abstractions by providing new tuning data types and instrument control templates.

### [94] [Kibble-Zurek Mechanism in the Open Quantum Rabi Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16709)
*T. Pirozzi,G. Di Bello,V. Cataudella,C. A. Perroni,G. De Filippis*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了非马尔可夫（non-Markovian）记忆效应能够保持基布尔-祖雷克机制（Kibble-Zurek mechanism）在开放量子系统中的普适标度律，与马尔可夫耗散破坏标度律的行为形成鲜明对比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基布尔-祖雷克机制为非平衡相变中的缺陷形成提供了普适框架，但马尔可夫耗散通常会破坏普适标度律，而非马尔可夫记忆效应的影响尚未得到充分探索。

Method: 研究采用基于矩阵乘积态（Matrix Product States）的模拟方法，在开放量子拉比模型（open quantum Rabi model）中分析欧姆浴（Ohmic bath）诱导的别列津斯基-科斯特利茨-索利斯相变（Berezinskii-Kosterlitz-Thouless transition）。

Result: 研究发现激发能在冻结时间（freeze-out time）处严格遵循普适的基布尔-祖雷克幂律标度（Kibble-Zurek power-law scaling），且由于环境定义了普适类（universality class），耗散并不固有地与绝热动力学竞争。

Conclusion: 该研究确立了基布尔-祖雷克机制作为开放量子系统中普适性的鲁棒见证者，揭示了非马尔可夫记忆能够保持非平衡标度律的完整性，这与马尔可夫体系形成鲜明对比。

Abstract: The Kibble-Zurek mechanism provides a universal framework for predicting defect formation in non-equilibrium phase transitions. While Markovian dissipation typically degrades universal scaling, the impact of non-Markovian memory remains largely unexplored. We demonstrate that an Ohmic bath induces a Berezinskii-Kosterlitz-Thouless transition in the open quantum Rabi model. Using simulations based on Matrix Product States, we show that the excitation energy strictly follows universal Kibble-Zurek power-law scaling when evaluated at the freeze-out time. Crucially, we find that since the environment defines the universality class, dissipation does not inherently compete with adiabatic dynamics, in stark contrast to Markovian regimes. Our results establish the Kibble- Zurek mechanism as a robust witness of universality in open quantum systems, revealing that non-Markovian memory preserves the integrity of non-equilibrium scaling.
