### [95] [How compactness curbs entanglement growth in bosonic systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16775)
*Stefan Aimet,Philipp Schmoll,Jens Eisert,Jörg Schmiedmayer,Spyros Sotiriadis*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了零模（zero modes）在玻色系统非平衡动力学中的核心作用，揭示了非紧致零模导致纠缠熵对数发散，而紧致零模则限制纠缠熵于有限值，这一机制在从最小模型到多体系统的对比中得到验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 零模（zero modes）作为具有消失约束频率的自由度，在玻色系统的非平衡动力学中扮演关键角色。然而在高斯模型中，零模会导致纠缠熵的无界对数增长，本文旨在探究这种发散是否为零模的固有属性。

Method: 通过对比紧致与非紧致零模的理论分析，首先在最小设置中比较两个耦合谐振子与两个耦合量子转子。随后将分析扩展到多体系统，对比N点紧致转子链与非紧致谐振链。最后将这些见解与超冷原子实现的紧致量子场论联系起来。

Result: 研究显示纠缠熵发散并非零模的固有属性，而是非紧致零模的特有现象。非紧致构型空间允许位置空间的无界扩散，连续谱则使动量空间发生无限退相干。相比之下，紧致玻色系统中的紧致零模行为根本不同：扩散和退相干最终停止，紧致性将纠缠熵限制在有限值内。

Conclusion: 即使初始状态可由非紧致高斯描述准确捕捉，紧致性最终支配了晚时淬火动力学，抑制纠缠增长而非允许动力学发散。这些发现阐明了何时需要紧致自由玻色子描述，以及常用的非紧致无质量克莱因-戈登模型何时失效。

Abstract: Zero modes, understood here as degrees of freedom with vanishing confining frequency, play a central role in the nonequilibrium dynamics of bosonic systems. In Gaussian models, however, they lead to an unbounded, logarithmic growth of entanglement entropy. We show that this divergence is not an intrinsic property of zero modes themselves, but arises specifically for non-compact zero modes. Their non-compact configuration space allows unbounded spreading in position space, while their continuous spectra enable indefinite dephasing in momentum space. By contrast, compact zero modes in compact bosonic systems behave fundamentally differently: Spreading and dephasing are eventually halted, so that compactness caps the entanglement entropy at a finite value, making its dynamical role most transparent in the presence of a zero mode. We demonstrate this mechanism in a minimal setting by comparing two coupled harmonic oscillators with two coupled quantum rotors. We then show that the same physics persists in many-body systems by contrasting an N-site compact rotor chain with the non-compact harmonic chain. Finally, we relate these insights to ultra-cold-atom realizations of compact quantum field theories. In particular, we clarify when a compact free-boson (Tomonaga-Luttinger liquid) description is required and when the commonly used non-compact massless Klein-Gordon model breaks down. Even when the initial state is accurately captured by a non-compact Gaussian description, compactness ultimately governs the late-time quench dynamics, curbing entanglement growth rather than allowing a dynamical divergence.

</details>


### [96] [Quantum signal processing in Hilbert space fragmented systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16784)
*Naoya Egawa,Kaoru Mizuta,Joji Nasu*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种利用希尔伯特空间碎片化（Hilbert space fragmentation, HSF）将量子信号处理（quantum signal processing, QSP）扩展到非可积系统的协议，实现了在单个系统中对可积与非可积扇区的并行量子动力学控制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子信号处理（QSP）作为量子算法的统一框架，在可积多体系统的非平衡控制中已展现出优势，但其向非可积系统的扩展面临守恒量有限和热化（thermalization）的根本性障碍。本研究旨在克服这一障碍，扩展QSP的应用范围。

Method: 研究提出了一种协议，利用展现希尔伯特空间碎片化（HSF）结构的系统——具体为一个具有四重周期势（four-fold periodic potentials）的对跳模型（pair-hopping model）。该系统在同一模型内同时包含可积扇区（integrable sectors）和非可积扇区（nonintegrable sectors）。

Result: 分析表明，通过由周期势设计的QSP，可以在可积扇区内灵活设计非平衡动力学（nonequilibrium dynamics）。数值计算则在非可积扇区识别出了热化特征。引人注目的是，通过插入畴壁（domain walls），实现了在单个系统内对多个量子动力学的并行控制。

Conclusion: 该工作通过将QSP的范围扩展到非可积系统，从量子计算（quantum computation）的视角为控制非平衡动力学提供了新思路。利用HSF结构，实现了在同一物理系统中对可积与非可积行为的区分与操控。

Abstract: Quantum signal processing (QSP), originally developed for composite pulse sequences in nuclear magnetic resonance systems, has recently attracted attention as a unified framework for quantum algorithms. A pioneering study applied QSP to nonequilibrium control in integrable many-body systems, enabling the realization of nonequilibrium dynamics with greater flexibility than Floquet engineering. However, extending QSP to nonintegrable systems faces fundamental obstacles arising from the limited number of conserved quantities and thermalization. In this work, we propose a protocol that leverages QSP in systems exhibiting Hilbert space fragmentation (HSF). Specifically, we consider a pair-hopping model with four-fold periodic potentials that exhibits an HSF structure, thereby providing integrable and nonintegrable sectors within a single system. We analytically show that nonequilibrium dynamics can be flexibly designed through QSP engineered by these potentials in the integrable sectors. In contrast, we numerically identify signatures of thermalization in the nonintegrable sectors. Remarkably, by inserting domain walls, we achieve parallel control of multiple quantum dynamics within a single system. This approach sheds light on the control of nonequilibrium dynamics from the perspective of quantum computation by extending the scope of QSP to nonintegrable systems.

</details>

### [97] [Taming the expressiveness of neural-network wave functions for robust convergence to quantum many-body states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15853)
*Dezhe Z. Jin*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种改进的神经网络方法，通过最小化局部能量的对数压缩方差（logarithmically compressed variance）来更有效地确定相互作用多体费米子系统的量子态，相比传统的最小化平均局部能量方法，能显著提高收敛速度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 神经网络已成为确定相互作用多体费米子系统量子态的有力工具，但标准方法通过最小化蒙特卡洛样本估计的平均局部能量进行训练，通常会导致估计平均能量的样本间波动较大，从而减缓能量最小化的收敛速度。

Method: 提出最小化局部能量的对数压缩方差（logarithmically compressed variance）作为损失函数，该方法可显著改善收敛性。此外，该损失函数可适应性地通过多次运行系统性地获取能谱（energy spectrum）。

Result: 在具有吸引性Poschl-Teller相互作用的二维谐振子陷阱中，对自旋-1/2粒子系统演示了该方法，验证了其有效性。

Conclusion: 最小化局部能量的对数压缩方差相比传统的最小化平均局部能量方法，能显著提高神经网络确定多体费米子系统量子态的收敛速度，并可扩展用于获取系统的能谱。

Abstract: Neural networks are emerging as a powerful tool for determining the quantum states of interacting many-body fermionic systems. The standard approach trains a neural-network ansatz by minimizing the mean local energy estimated from Monte Carlo samples. However, this typically results in large sample-to-sample fluctuations in the estimated mean energy and thus slow convergence of the energy minimization. We propose that minimizing a logarithmically compressed variance of the local energies can dramatically improve convergence. Moreover, this loss function can be adapted to systematically obtain the energy spectrum across multiple runs. We demonstrate these ideas for spin-1/2 particles in a 2D harmonic trap with attractive Poschl-Teller interactions between opposite spins.

### [98] [Stoichiometric FeTe is a Superconductor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16115)
*Zi-Jie Yan,Zihao Wang,Bing Xia,Stephen Paolini,Ying-Ting Chan,Nikalabh Dihingia,Hongtao Rong,Pu Xiao,Kalana D. Halanayake,Jiatao Song,Veer Gowda,Danielle Reifsnyder Hickey,Weida Wu,Jiabin Yu,Peter J. Hirschfeld,Cui-Zu Chang*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 通过Te退火去除间隙Fe原子，使FeTe薄膜达到理想化学计量比，从而抑制反铁磁序并诱导出~13.5K的超导转变，证明化学计量比FeTe本质上是超导体而非反铁磁金属。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 铁基超导体中多电子带和强反铁磁关联导致多种竞争基态。FeTe长期以来被认为是反铁磁金属而非超导体，但其超导异质结构中存在超导性，需要澄清其超导起源及化学计量比的作用。

Method: 采用分子束外延生长FeTe薄膜，并在Te气氛下进行后生长退火。使用自旋极化扫描隧道显微镜和谱学技术表征薄膜的磁性和电子结构。

Result: 间隙Fe原子破坏1:1化学计量比并诱导反铁磁序；Te退火去除间隙Fe原子后，获得化学计量比FeTe薄膜，反铁磁序消失并出现~13.5K的超导转变。观察到库珀对隧穿、零电阻和迈斯纳效应证实超导态。

Conclusion: 化学计量比FeTe本质上是超导体，而非传统认为的反铁磁金属。该研究阐明了FeTe基异质结构中超导性的起源，并证明化学计量比控制在理解铁基超导体中反铁磁与超导竞争中的重要性。

Abstract: Iron-based superconductors are a fascinating family of materials in which multiple electronic bands and strong antiferromagnetic (AFM) correlations are key ingredients for competing ground states, including antiferromagnetism, electronic nematicity, and unconventional superconductivity. FeTe, unlike its superconducting isostructural counterpart FeSe, has long been regarded as an AFM metal sans superconductivity. In this work, we employ molecular beam epitaxy to grow FeTe films and perform post-growth annealing under a Te flux. By performing spin-polarized scanning tunneling microscopy and spectroscopy, we demonstrate that the AFM order in as-grown FeTe films is induced by interstitial Fe atoms that disrupt the ideal 1:1 stoichiometry. Remarkably, the removal of these interstitial Fe atoms through Te annealing yields stoichiometric FeTe films that show no AFM order and instead exhibit robust superconductivity with a critical temperature of ~13.5K. This superconducting state is further confirmed by the observation of Cooper pair tunneling, zero electrical resistance, and the Meissner effect. Therefore, our results demonstrate that stoichiometric FeTe is inherently a superconductor, overturning a long-held view that it is an AFM metal. This work clarifies the origin of superconductivity in FeTe-based heterostructures and demonstrates the importance of stoichiometry control in understanding the competition between AFM and superconductivity in iron-based superconductors.

</details>

### [99] [Survival probability of random networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15682)
*Kevin Peralta-Martinez,J. A. Méndez-Bermúdez*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究详细分析了Erdös-Renyi随机网络中δ型激发的生存概率（survival probability）随时间演化的所有阶段，包括初始快速衰减、幂律衰减、关联孔（correlation hole）区域及饱和行为，揭示了与网络结构参数和本征态多重分形特性的定量关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于深入理解Erdös-Renyi随机网络中δ型激发的时间演化全过程，特别是通过生存概率分析来揭示网络动力学行为与结构参数之间的定量关系。

Method: 采用生存概率（survival probability）作为主要分析工具，研究Erdös-Renyi随机网络中随机加权邻接矩阵的本征态特性，重点关注时间演化的各个阶段：初始快速衰减、幂律衰减、关联孔区域和饱和行为。

Result: 研究发现：（1）生存概率的幂律衰减和时间平均生存概率分别与t^{-D_2}和t^{-\widetilde{D}_2}成正比，其中D_2和\widetilde{D}_2分别对应随机加权邻接矩阵本征态和初始状态的相关维数（correlation dimension）；（2）关联孔的相对深度与平均度⟨k⟩≈np成比例缩放；（3）ER网络随机加权邻接矩阵的本征态表现出明显的多重分形（multifractal）特性。

Conclusion: 该研究系统揭示了Erdös-Renyi随机网络中δ型激发时间演化的完整动力学图像，建立了生存概率衰减行为与网络结构参数（平均度）及本征态分形特性之间的定量关系，为理解复杂网络中的量子输运和局域化现象提供了新视角。

Abstract: In this work we study in detail all phases of the time evolution of a delta-like excitation in Erdös-Renyi (ER) random networks by means of the survival probability (SP): The initial decay of the SP (both, the fast decay followed by the power-law decay), the correlation hole regime (the regime between the minimum value of the SP and its saturation value), and the saturation of the SP. Specifically, we found that (i) the power-law decay of the SP and the time-averaged SP are proportional to $t^{-D_{2}}$ and $t^{-\widetilde{D}_{2}}$, respectively (where $D_2$ and $\widetilde{D}_2$ are the correlation dimension of the eigenstates of the randomly weighted adjacency matrices of the ER random networks and the correlation dimension associated with the initial state, respectively) and (ii) the relative depth of the correlation hole of the SP scales with the average degree $\langle k\rangle\approx np$ (here, $n$ and $p$ are the size and the connection probability of the ER random networks). In addition, we show that the eigenstates of the randomly weighted adjacency matrices of ER networks display clear multifractal properties.

</details>


### [100] [Non-Thermal Aging of Supercooled Liquids in Optical Cavities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15693)
*Muhammad R. Hasyim,Arianna Damiani,Norah M. Hoffmann*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种利用光学腔（optical cavity）中的光作为精确选择性工具来引导无序材料老化（aging）动力学的新方法。通过光腔耦合实现非热老化（non-thermal aging），并引入腔构型反馈冷却（C²F cooling）技术，为光学控制老化、玻璃形成和非平衡材料动力学开辟了新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 老化（aging）是玻璃、塑料和药物等无序材料的普遍特征，通常限制了其长期稳定性和性能。传统上通过温度或压力等全局参数控制老化，但这些参数对整个系统产生均匀作用，缺乏选择性。

Method: 研究引入了一种根本不同的方法：利用光学腔（optical cavity）中的光作为精确选择性工具来引导老化动力学。通过将过冷液体（supercooled liquid）与光学腔耦合，实现非热老化（non-thermal aging），其中老化由光诱导而非热淬火（thermal quench）。

Result: 光选择性泵浦快速振动模式（fast vibrational modes）而浴温度保持不变，重塑了液体的慢结构动力学（slow structural dynamics）。腔耦合液体在结构上表现得比其周围环境更冷，利用这种有效结构冷却（effective structural cooling）和时间尺度分离（timescale separation），研究者引入了腔构型反馈冷却（cavity configurational feedback cooling, C²F cooling）。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了玻璃物理学与强光-物质相互作用（strong light-matter interactions）之间的联系，为光学控制老化、玻璃形成和非平衡材料动力学（nonequilibrium materials dynamics）开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Aging is a hallmark of disordered materials such as glasses, plastics, and pharmaceuticals, where it often limits long-term stability and performance. In practice, aging is controlled through global parameters like temperature or pressure, which act uniformly on the entire system. Here we introduce a fundamentally different approach, using light confined in optical cavities as a precise and selective tool to guide aging dynamics. We show that a supercooled liquid coupled to an optical cavity undergoes non-thermal aging, where aging is induced by light without a thermal quench. Light selectively pumps fast vibrational modes while the bath temperature remains unchanged, reshaping the slow structural dynamics of the liquid. The cavity-coupled liquid thereby behaves as if it were structurally colder than its surroundings. Exploiting this effective structural cooling together with the timescale separation, we introduce cavity configurational feedback ($\mathrm{C^2F}$) cooling, which uses cavity coupling to reach progressively lower structural temperatures. Our results establish a connection between glass physics and strong light-matter interactions and open a new route toward optical control of aging, glass formation, and nonequilibrium materials dynamics.

</details>


### [101] [Casimir versus Helmholtz forces in the Gaussian model: exact results for Dirichlet--Dirichlet, Neumann--Dirichlet, Neumann--Neumann, and periodic boundary conditions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16030)
*Daniel Dantchev,Joseph Rudnick*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文比较了三维高斯模型中两种涨落诱导力：大正则系综（固定外场h）下的临界卡西米尔力（critical Casimir force）与正则系综（固定序参量平均值m）下的临界亥姆霍兹力（critical Helmholtz force）。研究发现，在狄利克雷-狄利克雷和诺伊曼-狄利克雷边界条件下两力行为不同，而在周期性和诺伊曼-诺伊曼边界条件下两力一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于比较两种涨落诱导力在不同系综中的行为：大正则系综（固定外场h）下的临界卡西米尔力与正则系综（固定序参量平均值m）下的临界亥姆霍兹力。通过分析这两种力在不同边界条件下的表现，可以深入理解系综选择对临界现象中涨落诱导力的影响。

Method: 研究方法基于三维高斯模型，在体临界点T=Tc附近推导了两种力的精确结果。考虑了四种边界条件：狄利克雷-狄利克雷（Dirichlet-Dirichlet）、诺伊曼-狄利克雷（Neumann-Dirichlet）、诺伊曼-诺伊曼（Neumann-Neumann）和周期性边界条件（periodic boundary conditions）。

Result: 对于所有考察的边界条件，两种力都遵循有限尺寸标度（finite-size scaling）。在狄利克雷-狄利克雷边界条件下，卡西米尔力总是吸引的，而亥姆霍兹力随T和m的变化既可以是吸引的也可以是排斥的。在诺伊曼-狄利克雷边界条件下，卡西米尔力随h增加从排斥变为吸引，而亥姆霍兹力总是排斥的。在周期性和诺伊曼-诺伊曼边界条件下，两力完全一致：卡西米尔力不依赖于h，亥姆霍兹力不依赖于m，且总是吸引的。

Conclusion: 研究结论表明，临界卡西米尔力和临界亥姆霍兹力的行为强烈依赖于边界条件。在某些边界条件下两力表现不同，这反映了系综选择对涨落诱导力的重要影响；而在其他边界条件下两力一致，表明系综差异的影响消失。

Abstract: We present results and compare the behavior of two fluctuation-induced forces pertinent for their corresponding ensembles: the critical Casimir force in the grand canonical (fixed external field $h$) one and the critical Helmholtz force in the canonical (fixed average value of the order parameter $m$) one. We do so by deriving exact results for their behavior near the bulk critical point at $T=T_c$ in the three-dimensional Gaussian model. We consider Dirichlet-Dirichlet, Neumann-Dirichlet, Neumann-Neumann, and periodic boundary conditions. For every boundary condition examined, we confirm that both forces follow a finite-size scaling. We find that for Dirichlet-Dirichlet and Neumann-Dirichlet boundary conditions the Casimir and the Helmholtz force differ from each other. For Dirichlet-Dirichlet boundary conditions the Casimir force is always attractive, while the Helmholtz force can be both attractive and repulsive as a function of $T$ and $m$. For Neumann-Dirichlet boundary conditions the Casimir force changes sign from repulsive to attractive with increase of $h$, while the Helmholtz force stays always repulsive. Under periodic and Neumann-Neumann boundary conditions the Casimir force and the Helmholtz force coincide - the first does not depend on $h$, while the latter does not depend on $m$; they are always attractive.

</details>


### [102] [Population Annealing as a Discrete-Time Schrödinger Bridge](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16056)
*Masayuki Ohzeki*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该论文提出一个理论框架，将群体退火（Population Annealing）重新解释为离散时间薛定谔桥（Schrödinger Bridge）问题，揭示了PA中的启发式重加权步骤可通过瞬时投影解析求解薛定谔系统得到，并将热力学功识别为路径空间全局变分问题的最优控制势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在建立群体退火（Population Annealing, PA）与薛定谔桥（Schrödinger Bridge, SB）问题之间的理论联系，为PA算法提供更坚实的数学基础，并统一非平衡热力学与最优传输的几何框架。

Method: 通过将PA重新解释为离散时间薛定谔桥问题，采用瞬时投影（instantaneous projection）方法解析求解薛定谔系统，避免了迭代计算，并将热力学功识别为路径空间全局变分问题的最优控制势。

Result: 证明了PA中的启发式重加权步骤（heuristic reweighting step）可通过解析求解薛定谔系统得到，阐明了Jarzynski等式作为Donsker-Varadhan变分原理中的一致性条件，并揭示了PA的热力学最优性。

Conclusion: 该框架统一了非平衡热力学与最优传输的几何框架，为PA算法提供了理论基础，将Jarzynski等式解释为变分原理的一致性条件，并阐明了PA的热力学最优性特征。

Abstract: We present a theoretical framework that reinterprets Population Annealing (PA) through the lens of the discrete-time Schrödinger Bridge (SB) problem. We demonstrate that the heuristic reweighting step in PA is derived by analytically solving the Schrödinger system without iterative computation via instantaneous projection. In addition, we identify the thermodynamic work as the optimal control potential that solves the global variational problem on path space. This perspective unifies non-equilibrium thermodynamics with the geometric framework of optimal transport, interpreting the Jarzynski equality as a consistency condition within the Donsker-Varadhan variational principle, and elucidates the thermodynamic optimality of PA.

</details>


### [103] [Conditional Ergodicity and Universal Fluctuations in Weak Ergodicity Breaking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16121)
*Dan Shafir,Stanislav Burov*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该论文揭示了在弱遍历破缺系统中，基于内部时钟条件化可以恢复时间平均观测量的自平均性，并推导出时间平均输运系数遵循米塔格-莱弗勒分布的普适定律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在复杂介质中，单粒子轨迹的时间平均表现出强烈的轨迹间差异，这种持续的轨迹间散射在反常扩散中常见，表明由无标度捕获驱动的弱遍历破缺。研究旨在理解这种非遍历行为的统计特性。

Method: 提出条件遍历性概念：基于自然内部时钟进行条件化，恢复时间平均观测量的自平均性。结合内部时钟与物理时间之间的随机映射关系，推导出普适分布规律。

Result: 证明了一个普适定律：在弱遍历破缺系统中，经过均值归一化后，时间平均输运系数遵循米塔格-莱弗勒分布。该普适性在多个显示反常扩散的无序介质模型中得到验证。

Conclusion: 条件遍历性为理解弱遍历破缺系统的统计行为提供了新框架，揭示了时间平均输运系数的普适分布规律，这一发现适用于多种反常扩散模型。

Abstract: Time averages extracted from single-particle trajectories in complex media often vary strongly from one trajectory to another, even for long measurement times. Such persistent trajectory-to trajectory scatter is commonly observed in anomalous diffusion and signals weak ergodicity breaking driven by scale-free trapping. Here we identify conditional ergodicity: conditioning on a natural internal clock restores self-averaging of time-averaged observables. Combining conditional ergodicity with the stochastic mapping between the internal clock and physical time implies a universal law: once rescaled by their mean, time-averaged transport coefficients in systems exhibiting weak ergodicity breaking follow the Mittag-Leffler distribution. We demonstrate this universality across multiple models of disordered media displaying anomalous diffusion.

</details>


### [104] [Percolation and Criticality in Hyperuniform Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16167)
*Yongyi Wang,Jaeuk Kim,Yang Jiao,Izabella Stuhl,Salvatore Torquato,Reka Albert*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了无序隐身超均匀（stealthy hyperuniform）系统的渗流行为，发现其渗流阈值低于泊松网络，且随隐身参数χ增加而降低。高χ系统与晶格属于同一普适类，而低χ系统则表现出偏离。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超均匀（hyperuniform）多粒子系统在宏观尺度上表现出异常密度涨落抑制，但其网络渗流行为尚未充分研究。本研究旨在探索无序隐身超均匀（SHU）系统的渗流特性，特别是其与泊松点配置的对比。

Method: 基于不同χ值的SHU配置和泊松点配置构建Delaunay三角化网络。研究非均匀键渗流过程，其中键占据概率随连接顶点间欧氏距离增加而降低。通过有限尺寸标度（finite-size scaling）和Newman-Ziff算法估计渗流阈值zc和临界指数。

Result: SHU网络的渗流阈值低于泊松网络，且随隐身参数χ增加而降低，表明短程有序增强时全局连通性更易形成。高χ系统与晶格属于同一普适类（universality class），而泊松和低χ系统则表现出偏离。

Conclusion: 该研究将SHU系统的输运性质研究从连续两相介质扩展到网络领域，揭示了密度涨落抑制程度与临界指数变化的相关性，为优化统计均匀无序网络的鲁棒性开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Hyperuniform many-particle systems, which encompass crystals, quasicrystals and certain exotic disordered systems, exhibit an anomalous suppression of density fluctuations on macroscopic length scales relative to those of conventional disordered systems. Here we investigate the percolation behaviors of disordered stealthy hyperuniform systems (SHU), a subclass of hyperuniform configurations for which the structure factor vanishes for a finite range of wavevectors near the origin, with the degree of stealthiness controlled via a parameter $χ$. We construct Delaunay triangulation networks derived from SHU configurations with varying $χ$ as well as Poisson point configurations for the purpose of comparison. We investigate a non-uniform bond percolation process, in which bond occupation probabilities decrease with the Euclidean distance between the connected vertices. In this setting, percolation is induced by varying a tuning parameter $z$. We estimate the percolation thresholds $z_c$ and critical exponents of the networks via finite-size scaling and the Newman-Ziff algorithm. We find that SHU networks exhibit lower percolation thresholds than Poisson networks. Notably, the percolation threshold of SHU networks decreases with the stealthiness parameter $χ$, indicating that global connectivity emerges more readily as short-range order increases. Moreover, we show that SHU networks with large $χ$ belong to the same universality class as lattices, while Poisson and low-$χ$ systems show deviations. We relate the shift in critical exponents to the degree of suppression of density fluctuations in the point configurations. Our work extends previous studies on transport properties of SHU systems from continuum two-phase media to networks. These results open new avenues for optimizing the resilience of statistically homogeneous disordered networks.

</details>


### [105] [Quantum Brownian Motion: proving that the Schmid transition belongs to the Berezinskii-Kosterlitz-Thouless universality class](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16227)
*Francesco G. Capone,Antonio de Candia,Vittorio Cataudella,Rosario Fazio,Naoto Nagaosa,Carmine Antonio Perroni,Giulio De Filippis*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究通过世界线蒙特卡洛方法证明，在欧姆耗散（Ohmic dissipation）区域，量子布朗粒子在周期势中的耗散驱动施密特转变（Schmid transition）属于Berezinskii-Kosterlitz-Thouless普适类（universality class）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探究量子布朗粒子在周期势中的平衡性质，特别关注欧姆耗散区域中耗散驱动施密特转变的本质特性。

Method: 采用路径积分形式中的世界线蒙特卡洛方法（World-Line Monte Carlo），并引入特定的二元序参量（binary order parameter）进行分析。

Result: 通过有限尺寸标度分析（finite-size scaling analysis）证实，该转变属于BKT普适类，表现为序参量关联函数在临界点呈现特征性对数衰减。量子相变极为脆弱，在超欧姆和亚欧姆耗散区域均消失。

Conclusion: 临界行为的出现严格受环境谱函数（environmental spectral function）低频形式支配，该函数决定了耗散核的长程时间衰减。周期势在亚欧姆和超欧姆区域不改变系统的局域化特性。

Abstract: We investigate the equilibrium properties of a quantum Brownian particle moving in a periodic potential, specifically addressing the nature of the dissipation-driven Schmid transition in the Ohmic regime. By employing World-Line Monte Carlo in the path-integral formalism and introducing a specific binary order parameter, we demonstrate that the transition belongs to the Berezinskii-Kosterlitz-Thouless universality class. This classification is substantiated through finite-size scaling analysis that reveals the characteristic logarithmic decay of the correlation functions associated with the order parameter at the critical point. Quantum phase transition turns out to be extremely fragile: it disappears in both over- and sub-Ohmic dissipation regimes. Crucially, we find that the presence of the periodic potential does not alter the localization properties in the sub-Ohmic and super-Ohmic regimes, where the system exhibits the same qualitative behavior as the free quantum Brownian particle. These findings highlight that the emergence of critical behavior is strictly governed by the low-frequency form of the environmental spectral function, which determines the long-range temporal decay of the dissipative kernel.

</details>


### [106] [Fractal and Spectral Dimensions as Determinants of Thermal Ablation Outcomes in Cancer Tissues](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16499)
*Mario Olmo-Fajardo,Alexander López,Malte Henkel,Sébastien Fumeron*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本研究通过建立分形-分数生物热模型，揭示了组织分形结构是临床热消融疗效变异性的关键因素，成功解释了肝转移瘤相比原发癌消融效果降低的现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 临床热消融结果存在显著变异性，经典生物热模型无法完全解释。一个重要原因在于生物组织的分形结构，这种结构异质性结合记忆效应导致活体组织中的热传递偏离傅里叶扩散，形成异常生物传输。

Method: 本研究实现了真实的分形-分数生物热模型，包含非线性灌注和PI控制的功率输送，用于量化组织分形性在消融结果中的作用。

Result: 研究结果表明，凝固区的扩展由分形几何及其相关的拓扑连通性共同控制。谱维度被识别为临床变异性的关键驱动因素，成功再现了肝转移瘤相比原发癌消融效果降低的现象。

Conclusion: 这些发现强调了谱维度作为临床变异性的关键驱动因素，为恶性肿瘤热消融的拓扑知情治疗策略提供了证据支持。

Abstract: Clinical thermal ablation outcomes display significant variability that classical bio-heat models cannot fully explain. One reason may lie in the fractal architecture of biological tissues, which has been identified as a robust biomarker directly correlated with cancer grades. This structural heterogeneity, together with memory effects (e.g., thermotolerance), causes heat transfer in living tissues to differ from Fourier diffusion, resulting in anomalous biological transport.
  In this work, we implemented a realistic fractal-fractional bio-heat model, with non-linear perfusion and PI-controlled power delivery, to quantify the role of tissue fractality in ablation outcomes. Our results reveal that the expansion of coagulation zones is jointly controlled by fractal geometry and its associated topological connectivity. These findings highlight spectral dimension as a key driver of clinical variability, successfully reproducing the reduced ablative efficacy in liver metastases compared to primary carcinomas, and provide evidence for topologically informed treatment strategies for the thermal ablation of malignant neoplasms.

</details>


### [107] [Lifting the fog - a case for non-reversible "lifted" Markov chains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16855)
*Gabriele Tartero,Sora Shiratani,Werner Krauth*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该论文研究非可逆"提升"（lifting）蒙特卡洛算法在相分离Lennard-Jones系统中的粗化动力学，发现相比传统可逆Metropolis算法，非可逆算法能显著加速相变动力学，提高粗化增长指数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 相变动力学在科学和日常生活中普遍存在，但通常非常缓慢。在计算算法中，Metropolis蒙特卡洛算法（Metropolis Monte Carlo algorithm）的混合动力学同样受可逆性和细致平衡（detailed-balance）原理支配，导致收敛缓慢。研究旨在探索非可逆算法是否能加速相变动力学过程。

Method: 研究采用非可逆"提升"（lifting）变体的Metropolis算法，特别是事件链蒙特卡洛（event-chain Monte Carlo）方法。通过实现长程Metropolis算法及其非可逆提升版本，分析Lennard-Jones系统的相分离粗化动力学。

Result: 非可逆"提升"算法在相分离Lennard-Jones系统中表现出更快的粗化时间尺度。微观非可逆性转化为液滴间的大尺度相对运动，通过密度-位移耦合（density-displacement coupling）产生透镜效应（lensing effect）。粗化增长指数（coarsening growth exponent）在提升算法下更大，对于大系统尺寸，计算问题解决速度无限快于传统方法。

Conclusion: 非可逆"提升"算法能显著加速相变动力学，且严格保持与Metropolis算法相同的结果。这一发现具有更广泛的应用前景，因为"提升"非可逆算法可应用于通用的可逆采样方法，适用范围远超文中研究的"提升雾"（lifting fog）示例。

Abstract: Phase transitions appear all over science, and are familiar from everyday life, as water boiling, sugar melting into caramel or as nematic molecules turning smectic in liquid-crystal displays. The dynamics of phase transitions can be extremely slow, as for example when fog in winter does not lift, that is when the coarsening takes much time from many tiny water droplets to fewer but larger rain drops that feel the pull of gravity. The dynamics of phase transitions is relevant also for the performance of computer algorithms. In the ubiquitous Metropolis Monte Carlo algorithm, the mixing dynamics towards equilibrium leads towards the solution of a sampling problem. It is governed by the same reversibility and detailed-balance principles as the overdamped physical dynamics of fog. For the phase-separated Lennard-Jones system, we describe here how the coarsening dynamics of non-reversible "lifted" variants of the Metropolis algorithm proceeds on much faster time scales, with the microscopic non-reversibility translating into large-scale relative motion of droplets that is impossible under the Ostwald-ripening condition of reversibility. A density-displacement coupling moves droplets relative to each other through a lensing effect. Efficient implementations of the long-range Metropolis algorithm and its non-reversible lifting (event-chain Monte Carlo) allow us to show that, in consequence, the coarsening growth exponent is larger under lifting. For large system sizes, the computing problem is thus solved infinitely faster than before, with the outcome strictly unchanged with respect to the Metropolis algorithm. We also discuss the larger setting of our findings, namely that "lifted" non-reversible algorithms can be set up for generic reversible sampling methods, with applications going much beyond our example of lifting fog.

</details>

Abstract: Inspired by the Bohlin transformation relating the planar harmonic oscillator to the Kepler problem, a variant of the Eisenhart lift is studied, in which a Lagrangian conservative dynamical system with d degrees of freedom is embedded into timelike geodesics of a conformally flat metric on a (d+2)-dimensional space-time of the Lorentzian signature. ### [110] [Ising criticality can drive vortex deconfinement in a spin-orbit coupled Bose gas](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15747)
*Stuart Yi-Thomas,David M. Long,Jay D. Sau*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该研究通过蒙特卡洛模拟发现，在具有自旋轨道耦合的二维玻色气体中，伊辛相变附近的临界涨落可以驱动超流体的Berezinskii-Kosterlitz-Thouless相变，同时伊辛相变本身变为一级相变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于二维自旋轨道耦合玻色气体中，超流序参量与伊辛序参量之间的非平凡相互作用。具体而言，伊辛畴壁允许涡旋-反涡旋对自由分离，这暗示伊辛相变附近的临界涨落可能驱动超流体的BKT相变。

Method: 采用蒙特卡洛模拟方法研究该现象，同时使用变分近似来支持数值发现。模拟重点考察了超流刚度在伊辛相变附近的行为变化。

Result: 数值证据显示：1）在伊辛相变附近，超流刚度消失，表明发生了Berezinskii-Kosterlitz-Thouless相变；2）伊辛相变本身变为一级相变，这一发现通过变分近似得到了理论支持。

Conclusion: 研究证实了二维自旋轨道耦合玻色气体中，伊辛相变与超流体BKT相变之间存在耦合机制，伊辛临界涨落能够驱动超流相变，同时伊辛相变性质也发生改变为一级相变。

Abstract: Spin-orbit coupling in Bose gases is known to lead to an Ising-symmetry-broken phase where the bosons condense at one of two nonzero momenta. In two dimensions, the finite momentum of the order parameter allows vortex-antivortex pairs that are typically bound in the superfluid phase to freely separate along Ising domain walls. This non-trivial interaction between the superfluid and the Ising order suggests that the critical fluctuations near an Ising transition could drive a Berezinskii-Kosterlitz-Thouless transition of the superfluid. We present numerical evidence of this phenomenon using a Monte Carlo simulation that shows the disappearance of superfluid stiffness near an Ising transition. Additionally, we find numerical evidence that the Ising phase transition becomes first order and we justify this claim with a variational approximation.

### [111] [Anomalous dynamical scaling in interacting anyonic chains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15972)
*Xu-Chen Yang,Botao Wang,Jianpeng Liu,Bing Yang,Jianmin Yuan,Yongqiang Li*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该研究通过大规模数值模拟发现，一维晶格中任意子（anyons）的远平衡弛豫表现出非常规但普适的标度行为：密度关联超扩散传播，而纠缠熵呈弹道增长，揭示了分数统计（fractional statistics）作为超越玻色-费米范式的非平衡动力学新普适性来源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 粒子统计（particle statistics）对非平衡量子动力学施加基本约束，但分数统计（fractional statistics）能否导致超越传统玻色-费米范式（Bose-Fermi paradigm）的涌现普适动力学标度行为，仍是一个开放问题。

Method: 基于大规模数值模拟（large-scale numerical simulations）和标度分析（scaling analysis），研究一维晶格中任意子的远平衡多体弛豫（far-from-equilibrium many-body relaxation）。

Result: 发现粒子输运与信息传播的明显分离：密度关联（density correlations）超扩散（superdiffusively）传播，而纠缠熵（entanglement entropy）呈弹道（ballistically）增长。异常粒子动力学可归因于统计相位诱导的量子干涉（statistical-phase-induced quantum interference）抑制了相干holon-doublon传播。

Conclusion: 任意子统计（anyonic statistics）被确立为超越玻色子和费米子的独特普适非平衡动力学来源，对当前量子模拟实验具有直接相关性。

Abstract: Particle statistics impose fundamental constraints on nonequilibrium quantum dynamics, yet it remains an open question whether fractional statistics can lead to emergent universal dynamical scaling beyond the conventional Bose-Fermi paradigm. Here we investigate the far-from-equilibrium many-body relaxation of anyons in a one-dimensional lattice and uncover an unconventional yet universal scaling behavior governed by fractional statistics. Based on large-scale numerical simulations and scaling analysis, we identify a distinct separation between particle transport and information spreading: density correlations spread superdiffusively, whereas entanglement entropy grows ballistically. The anomalous particle dynamics can be interpreted intuitively from the statistical-phase-induced quantum interference, which suppresses coherent holon-doublon propagation. In contrast, the entanglement growth turns out to be dominated by its configurational component, which propagates ballistically. Our results establish anyonic statistics as a distinct source of universal nonequilibrium dynamics beyond bosons and fermions, with direct relevance to current quantum simulation experiments.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用超冷自旋-1系综构建三能级系统，利用可调自旋张量耦合（spin-tensor coupling）引入场各向异性。通过拓扑不变量第一陈数（first Chern number）量化磁单极子电荷，并用贝里曲率（Berry curvature）量化合成磁场。

Result: 直接测量了陈数并观测到拓扑相变，验证了磁单极子拓扑电荷在形变下的鲁棒性。通过自旋织构（spin-texture）和马约拉纳星（Majorana-star）测量观测到拓扑相的特征。

Conclusion: 该工作证明自旋张量耦合可作为调节参数，用于工程化几何各向异性和丰富的拓扑相空间，为量子模拟中的拓扑现象研究提供了新途径。

Abstract: Higher-dimensional Hilbert spaces in quantum simulation, as in all quantum science, expand the range of accessible phenomena. In this work, we experimentally realize a synthetic monopole using an ultracold spin-1 ensemble, where the monopole charge is quantified by the topologically invariant first Chern number and sources a synthetic magnetic field quantified by the Berry curvature. By using a three-level system with tunable spin-tensor coupling, we introduce anisotropy to the field, directly measure the Chern number, and observe a topological phase transition. We verify the robustness of the monopole's topological charge under deformation, and observe signatures of the topological phases using spin-texture and Majorana-star measurements. This work demonstrates spin-tensor coupling as a tuning parameter for engineering both geometric anisotropy and a rich topological phase space.

### [113] [Efimovian Phonon Production for an Analog Coasting Universe in Bose-Einstein Condensates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16095)
*Yunfei Xue,Jiabin Wang,Li Chen,Chenwei Lv,Ren Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该论文预测了在模拟线性膨胀宇宙中实现的时间性埃菲莫夫效应（temporal Efimov effect），通过准二维玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（Bose-Einstein condensate）平台，展示了声子模式（phonon mode）在时间重标度下的不变性导致粒子产生（particle production）的两种动力学特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 空间埃菲莫夫效应（spatial Efimov effect）已被广泛研究，但其时间对应物（temporal counterpart）的实现仍具挑战性，需要破坏时间平移对称性（time-translation symmetry）同时保持时间标度对称性（time-scaling symmetry）的动力学系统。类比宇宙学（analog cosmology）为此提供了解决这一挑战的强大平台。

Method: 采用准二维玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（quasi-two-dimensional Bose-Einstein condensate）实现模拟线性膨胀宇宙（analog linearly expanding universe），利用声子模式方程（phonon mode equations）在时间重标度（time rescaling）下的不变性来研究时间性埃菲莫夫效应。

Result: 预测了粒子产生（particle production）具有两种不同的动力学：幂律增长（power-law growth）和对数周期振荡（log-periodic oscillations），后者是埃菲莫夫效应的标志性特征。这些动力学直接映射到亚视界和超视界宇宙学模式（sub- and super-horizon cosmological modes）。

Conclusion: 研究预测可以通过当前实验中对密度涨落谱（density-fluctuation spectrum）$S_{k}(t)$的时间平均测量直接验证，为连接埃菲莫夫物理和宇宙学领域提供了具体实现方案。

Abstract: Efimov effects arise from scale invariance, a fundamental symmetry with universal implications. While spatial Efimov physics has been extensively studied, realizing its temporal counterpart remains challenging, as it requires a dynamical system that breaks time-translation symmetry yet preserves the essential time-scaling symmetry. Analog cosmology offers a powerful platform to address this challenge, bridging the domains of Efimov physics and cosmology. Here, we predict a temporal Efimov effect in an analog linearly expanding universe realized with a quasi-two-dimensional Bose-Einstein condensate. The invariance of phonon mode equations under time rescaling leads to particle production with two distinct dynamics: power-law growth and log-periodic oscillations, with the latter being the hallmark signature of the Efimov effect. Furthermore, these dynamics map directly onto sub- and super-horizon cosmological modes. Our predictions can be directly verified through time-averaged measurements of the density-fluctuation spectrum $S_{k}(t)$ in current experiments.

### [114] [Quantized transport of solitons in Bose-Einstein condensates driven by spin-orbit coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16433)
*Yaroslav V. Kartashov,Vladimir V. Konotop,Dmitry A. Zezyulin*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该论文展示了在具有滑动螺旋自旋轨道耦合（helicoidal spin-orbit coupling）的双组分玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体中实现线性和非线性Thouless泵浦（Thouless pumping），并研究了孤子（solitons）在半无限和有限能隙中的稳定量子化输运（quantized transport）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用具有滑动螺旋自旋轨道耦合的双组分玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体系统，该系统具有对两个自旋分量相同的静态光学晶格（static optical lattice），研究孤子在半无限和有限能隙中的输运特性。

Result: 在特定化学势和原子数区间内，孤子在半无限和有限能隙中表现出稳定的量子化输运。在半无限能隙中，原子数足够大的孤子输运会被抑制。Zeeman分裂（Zeeman splitting）在控制量子化输运中起重要作用，当移除Zeeman场的纵向分量时输运消失。

Conclusion: 研究表明通过滑动螺旋自旋轨道耦合可以在双组分玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体中实现线性和非线性Thouless泵浦，Zeeman场对量子化输运的控制至关重要，为操控拓扑输运提供了新途径。

Abstract: We demonstrate that linear and nonlinear Thouless pumping can be realized in two-component elongated Bose-Einstein condensates using helicoidal spin-orbit coupling that slides with respect to a static optical lattice, identical for both spinor components. Stable quantized transport is found for solitons in semi-infinite and finite gaps, within certain intervals of chemical potentials and numbers of atoms. In the semi-infinite gap, the transport is arrested for solitons with sufficiently large number of atoms. We elucidate the important role of Zeeman splitting in the control of quantized transport, which disappears when the longitudinal component of the Zeeman field is removed.

### [115] [Fate of a Fractional Chern Insulator under Nonlocal Interactions in Synthetic Dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16724)
*Patrick Liam Geraghty,Alberto Nardin,Leonardo Mazza,Matteo Rizzi*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该研究通过引入无限长程柱状相互作用模拟合成维度中的非局域性，展示了从玻色分数量子陈绝缘体到电荷有序态的绝热演化，揭示了拓扑标记在非局域相互作用下的局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 合成维度（synthetic dimensions）为超冷原子系统中拓扑晶格模型的工程提供了强大途径，但其中包含沿合成方向的内在非局域相互作用。研究旨在探索这种非局域性对拓扑相的影响。

Method: 研究扩展的Harper-Hofstadter模型，引入无限长程柱状相互作用（infinite-range column interactions）来模拟合成维度中的非局域性，并通过调节相互作用强度实现绝热演化。

Result: 通过调节相互作用强度，实现了从Laughlin型玻色分数量子陈绝缘体（bosonic fractional Chern insulator）到类Tao-Thouless电荷有序态的绝热演化，过程中多体能隙保持开放。尽管纠缠谱发生显著重构且对局域扰动的鲁棒性丧失，但多体陈数（many-body Chern number）和拓扑纠缠熵（topological entanglement entropy）保持不变。

Conclusion: 该绝热连通性在拓扑有序态和有效一维电荷有序态之间建立了可控桥梁，为态制备开辟了新途径。同时表明传统拓扑标记可能无法诊断合成维度中局域性保护的拓扑序的破坏，并确认非局域相互作用可作为在不同多体态之间相干插值的有效调控手段。

Abstract: Synthetic dimensions provide a powerful route to engineer topological lattice models in ultracold atomic systems, but they contain intrinsic nonlocal interactions along the synthetic direction. We investigate an extended Harper-Hofstadter model subject to infinite-range column interactions that mimic this synthetic nonlocality. By tuning this interaction strength, we demonstrate an adiabatic evolution from a Laughlin-type bosonic fractional Chern insulator to a charge-ordered Tao-Thouless-like state without closing the many-body gap. Along this path, the many-body Chern number and the topological entanglement entropy remain unchanged, despite a pronounced restructuring of the entanglement spectrum and the loss of robustness against local perturbations. This adiabatic connectivity establishes a controlled bridge between topologically ordered and effect- ively one-dimensional charge-ordered regimes, opening potential new avenues for state preparation. Our results also show that conventional topological markers may fail to diagnose the breakdown of locality-protected topological order in synthetic dimensions, and identify nonlocal interactions as a powerful knob to coherently interpolate between distinct many-body regimes.

</details>

### [116] [Biomedical active matter: Emergence and breakdown of collective functionalities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15778)
*Arnold Mathijssen,Hamed Almohammadi,Lauren Altman,Talia Calazans,M. J. Ferencz,Michelle Fung,Ian J. Lee,Maciej Lisicki,Ivy Liu,Maggie Liu,Tianyi Liu,Ernest Park,Ran Tao,Albane Thery,Zeyuan Wang,Margot Young*

TL;DR: 该综述论文探讨了生物医学活性物质（biomedical active matter）领域的最新进展，重点分析了生命系统中集体功能的自组织机制及其在疾病治疗中的应用潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生命系统由活性材料（active materials）构成，其微观组件协同工作以执行宏观生物功能。这些集体功能的破坏会导致疾病，而利用自组织（self-organization）原理则可能为医疗技术提供新的治疗途径。

Method: 论文采用综述方法，围绕四个主要主题展开分析：(1)集体自组装（collective self-assembly）与时空协调；(2)集体运动、运输与导航；(3)集体感知、信号传导与通信；(4)集体适应、进化与学习。

Result: 作者讨论了从蛋白质折叠到心血管流动网络等多种系统中的新兴过程，包括生物分子凝聚物（biomolecular condensates）、细胞骨架动力学（cytoskeleton dynamics）、细菌生物膜（bacterial biofilms）、群体感应（quorum sensing）等具体案例。

Conclusion: 论文强调了集体功能减弱相关的医疗状况，并探讨了如何利用微机器人集群（microrobotic swarms）、仿生超材料（bioinspired metamaterials）、芯片实验室（lab-on-chip devices）、类器官（organoids）等活性与适应性物质创新进行治疗。

Abstract: Living systems are made of active materials with microscopic components that work together to perform macroscopic biological tasks. The breakdown of these collective functionalities leads to diseases, which, conversely, could be treated by exploiting self-organization in healthcare technologies. Here, we review recent advances in this rapidly growing field of biomedical active matter. The main themes are (1) collective self-assembly and spatiotemporal coordination; (2) collective motion, transport, and navigation; (3) collective sensing, signaling, and communication; and (4) collective adaptation, evolution, and learning. We discuss these emerging processes in a wide range of systems, including protein folding, biomolecular condensates, cytoskeleton dynamics, intracellular flows, bacterial biofilms, quorum sensing, cilia synchronization, wound healing, biolocomotion, neurons, endocrine signalling, and cardiovascular flow networks. For each, we highlight medical conditions associated with reduced collective functionality and how they may be treated using microrobotic swarms, bioinspired metamaterials, diagnostics, lab-on-chip devices, organoids, and other active and adaptive matter innovations.

### [117] [Novelty-Driven Target-Space Discovery in Automated Electron and Scanning Probe Microscopy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16715)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代自动化显微镜面临根本性发现挑战：许多系统中最重要的科学信息并不存在于立即可见的图像特征中，而是存在于顺序获取的光谱或功能响应的目标空间。因此需要开发能够主动搜索新行为而非仅优化已知目标的策略。

Method: 开发了深度核学习（deep-kernel-learning）的BEACON框架，通过在实验中学习结构-性质关系（structure-property relationships），并利用该演化模型寻找多样化的响应机制。首先基于预采集的真实数据集建立演示工作流程，实现与经典采集策略的直接基准测试。

Result: 建立了包含探索质量、目标空间覆盖度和代理模型行为比较的监控函数集，为评估发现驱动算法提供了实用基准框架。该方法成功从离线验证过渡到扫描透射电子显微镜（STEM）的实际实验实施。

Conclusion: BEACON框架能够有效指导目标空间的科学发现，相关笔记本资源可供社区使用，支持用户复现工作流程、测试基准，并将方法适配到各自的仪器和数据集。

Abstract: Modern automated microscopy faces a fundamental discovery challenge: in many systems, the most important scientific information does not reside in the immediately visible image features, but in the target space of sequentially acquired spectra or functional responses, making it essential to develop strategies that can actively search for new behaviors rather than simply optimize known objectives. Here, we developed a deep-kernel-learning BEACON framework that is explicitly designed to guide discovery in the target space by learning structure-property relationships during the experiment and using that evolving model to seek diverse response regimes. We first established the method through demonstration workflows built on pre-acquired ground-truth datasets, which enabled direct benchmarking against classical acquisition strategies and allowed us to define a set of monitoring functions for comparing exploration quality, target-space coverage, and surrogate-model behavior in a transparent and reproducible manner. This benchmarking framework provides a practical basis for evaluating discovery-driven algorithms, not just optimization performance. We then operationalized and deployed the workflow on STEM, showing that the approach can transition from offline validation to real experimental implementation. To support adoption and extension by the broader community, the associated notebooks are available, allowing users to reproduce the workflows, test the benchmarks, and adapt the method to their own instruments and datasets.

### [118] [Stochastic Resetting Accelerates Policy Convergence in Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16842)
*Jello Zhou,Vudtiwat Ngampruetikorn,David J. Schwab*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 随机重置（stochastic resetting）与强化学习（reinforcement learning）结合，可加速策略收敛，特别是在探索困难、奖励稀疏的环境中，提供了一种超越经典首次通过优化的新机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有随机重置理论主要处理静态、非学习过程，本文旨在探索随机重置如何与强化学习相互作用，研究底层动态通过经验适应时的优化效果。

Method: 在表格网格环境中分析重置对策略收敛的影响，并在基于神经网络值近似的连续控制任务中，研究随机重置对深度强化学习（deep reinforcement learning）的改进效果。

Result: 重置在网格环境中加速策略收敛，即使不减少纯扩散代理的搜索时间；在连续控制任务中，随机重置在探索困难、奖励稀疏时改善深度强化学习性能，通过截断长轨迹增强值传播。

Conclusion: 随机重置作为一种简单可调的机制，可加速学习过程，将统计力学（statistical mechanics）的典型现象转化为强化学习的优化原则，同时保持最优策略不变。

Abstract: Stochastic resetting, where a dynamical process is intermittently returned to a fixed reference state, has emerged as a powerful mechanism for optimizing first-passage properties. Existing theory largely treats static, non-learning processes. Here we ask how stochastic resetting interacts with reinforcement learning, where the underlying dynamics adapt through experience. In tabular grid environments, we find that resetting accelerates policy convergence even when it does not reduce the search time of a purely diffusive agent, indicating a novel mechanism beyond classical first-passage optimization. In a continuous control task with neural-network-based value approximation, we show that random resetting improves deep reinforcement learning when exploration is difficult and rewards are sparse. Unlike temporal discounting, resetting preserves the optimal policy while accelerating convergence by truncating long, uninformative trajectories to enhance value propagation. Our results establish stochastic resetting as a simple, tunable mechanism for accelerating learning, translating a canonical phenomenon of statistical mechanics into an optimization principle for reinforcement learning.

</details>

### [119] [\texttt{py5vec}: a modular Python package for the 5-vector method to search for continuous gravitational waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15703)
*Luca D'Onofrio,Federico Muciaccia,Lorenzo Mirasola,Matthew Pitkin,Cristiano Palomba,Paola Leaci,Francesco Safai Tehrani,Francesco Amicucci,Lorenzo Silvestri,Lorenzo Pierini*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文介绍了py5vec——一个用于实现和扩展5-向量方法（5-vector method）的Python软件包，该方法用于搜索连续引力波（continuous gravitational wave, CW）信号。该软件包提供了模块化架构，支持多种数据格式，并首次在5-向量形式中实现了贝叶斯参数估计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在提供一个灵活的平台来实施和扩展5-向量方法，该方法用于搜索连续引力波信号。通过开发py5vec软件包，研究者可以更有效地进行目标搜索，并与其他现有软件进行精确比较。

Method: py5vec采用模块化架构，将数据表示、信号解调和统计推断分离为独立的抽象阶段。该方法扩展了相对似然形式，通过对噪声方差进行边缘化得到更稳健的Student's t-似然，并对初始相位进行边缘化以处理脉冲星闪烁（pulsar glitches）。软件包支持多种输入数据格式，并与现有Python软件互操作。

Result: py5vec首次在5-向量形式中实现了贝叶斯参数估计，通过基于bilby的接口完成。该软件包实现了多探测器目标搜索（multidetector targeted search），使用LIGO O4a运行数据和硬件注入（hardware injections）进行验证，证明能够一致地重建信号参数。

Conclusion: py5vec为当前的目标搜索提供了一个灵活平台，并为未来扩展到其他连续引力波搜索策略奠定了基础。其模块化设计允许在不同软件（如cwinpy和SNAG）之间进行精确的多层次和直接比较。

Abstract: We present \texttt{py5vec}, a Python package for implementing and extending the 5-vector method, used to search for continuous gravitational wave (CW) signals. We also provide a comprehensive theoretical review of the 5-vector method and extend the relative likelihood formalism by marginalizing over the noise variance, resulting in a more robust Student's t-likelihood, and over the initial phase to account for pulsar glitches. \texttt{py5vec} provides a modular architecture that separates data representation, signal demodulation, and statistical inference into independent abstract stages. It supports multiple input data formats and interoperates with existing Python software, providing a bridge between different approaches. For example, using a \texttt{bilby}-based interface, \texttt{py5vec} implements Bayesian parameter estimation within the 5-vector formalism for the first time. The modular design also allows for making exact multi-level and direct comparisons between other software, such as \texttt{cwinpy} and \texttt{SNAG} in MATLAB. In \texttt{py5vec}, we implement a multidetector targeted search for known pulsars, validated using LIGO data from the O4a run and hardware injections, demonstrating consistent reconstruction of signal parameters. This package therefore provides a flexible platform for current targeted searches and for future extensions to other CW search strategies.

</details>

Conclusion: 量子力学百年发展历程展现了从原子现象理论模型到现代信息科学应用的演变轨迹。当前量子理论面临量子-经典边界（quantum-classical boundary）、量子引力（quantum gravity）以及暗物质（dark matter）和暗能量（dark energy）等关键挑战，这些问题的解决将推动量子理论的进一步发展。

Abstract: This paper commemorates the 100th anniversary of quantum mechanics as a theoretical model of atomic phenomena. We discuss briefly the foundational contributions of Werner Heisenberg, Wolfgang Pauli, Erwin Shrodinger, and Paul Dirac to the development of quantum theory. Special attention is given to the often-overlooked contributions of Charles Galton Darwin and Hendrik Anthony Kramers. We examine the three periods of quantum theory development: foundation, development, and the modern era connected with information science. The paper also highlights current challenges facing quantum theory, including the quantum-classical boundary, quantum gravity, and the mysteries of dark matter and dark energy. One of the goals of this article is to extend the recent review in J. Phys. A: Math. Theor. 58 (2025) 053001 primarily by a a more detailed consideration of the period of formation of quantum mechanics.

I also discuss selected advances in lattice methods and in QCD thermodynamics under external conditions, in particular strong magnetic fields, isospin chemical potential, rotation, acceleration, and quark spin polarization.

### [122] [Tailoring spontaneous symmetry breaking in engineered van der Waals superlattices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15787)
*Keda Jin,Lennart Klebl,Zachary A. H. Goodwin,Junting Zhao,Felix Lüpke,Dante M. Kennes,Jose Martinez-Castro,Markus Ternes*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种基于本征衬底电子序调控超晶格势的新方法，利用1T-NbSe₂的电荷密度波在石墨烯中构建了两种不同的近公度超晶格，实现了对Dirac锥能带折叠的精确控制，并揭示了自发对称性破缺的结构起源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 范德华异质结中的超晶格工程（如莫尔工程）为设计电子能带和实现关联拓扑量子现象提供了强大平台。本研究旨在开发一种基于本征衬底电子序调控超势能的新方案，以建立更稳健、自对准且高度通用的能带结构控制途径。

Method: 研究采用扫描隧道显微镜（scanning tunnelling microscopy, STM）观测石墨烯/1T-NbSe₂异质结中的超晶格结构。结合密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）与层间相互作用模型，分析能带折叠和对称性破缺的物理机制。

Result: 利用1T-NbSe₂的电荷密度波（charge density waves, CDWs）成功构建了两种不同的近公度超晶格，分别将石墨烯的Dirac锥折叠到迷你布里渊区的Γ点或K点。Γ折叠系统保持了C₃对称性，而K折叠系统表现出自发对称性破缺（spontaneous symmetry breaking）。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了基于本征衬底电子序的超晶格工程新范式，为设计量子态提供了新途径。研究揭示了对称性破缺并非电子驱动，而是源于结构不稳定性，为控制涌现对称性破缺提供了结构机制。

Abstract: Superlattice engineering in van der Waals heterostructures (e.\,g.\ by moiré engineering) provides a powerful platform for designing electronic bands and realising correlated and topological quantum phenomena. Here, we pioneer a scheme to tailor superpotentials based on intrinsic substrate electronic orders. We show that this establishes a robust, self-aligned, and highly versatile route to band-structure control as we demonstrate in graphene by engineering two distinct, nearly commensurate superlattices using the charge density waves of 1T-NbSe$_2$. In these superlattices the graphene's Dirac cones are folded either to the $Γ$-point or to the K-points of the mini-Brillouin zone. Using scanning tunnelling microscopy, we observe that the $Γ$-folded system preserves C$_3$ symmetry, while the K-folded system exhibits spontaneous symmetry breaking. Combining density functional theory with an interlayer interaction model, we reveal that this difference is not electronically driven but originates from a structural instability. Our work establishes superlattice engineering for designer quantum states and unveils a structural mechanism for controlled emergent symmetry breaking.

</details>


### [123] [Dissipation effects in the Su-Schrieffer-Heeger model coupled to a metallic environment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15835)
*Leandro M. Arancibia,Cristián G. Sánchez,Alejandro M. Lobos*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究通过改进的SSH模型，理论分析了沉积在金属基底上的反式聚乙炔分子的电子和晶格性质。研究发现，在均匀金属基底中，系统会在临界耦合参数下发生零温绝缘体-金属转变；在非均匀基底中，同一分子内会出现金属化或Peierls二聚化相的局域成核现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解沉积在金属基底上的反式聚乙炔（tPA）分子的电子和晶格性质，特别是金属环境对Peierls二聚化的影响。这一研究对于正确解释现有tPA/Cu(110)实验以及设计新型有机纳米电子器件具有重要意义。

Method: 采用改进的Su-Schrieffer-Heeger（SSH）模型，该模型通过将每个SSH链位点与独立的一维半无限链耦合（即"局域浴近似"）来纳入金属环境效应。在零温条件下，通过最小化N位点tPA链的总基态能量（包括电子和晶格自由度）作为晶格位点位置的函数，获得其物理性质。

Result: 在均匀金属基底情况下，当耦合参数γ_0达到临界值时，SSH链经历零温绝缘体-金属转变，Peierls二聚化被完全抑制，系统变为金属性。在非均匀基底情况下，同一tPA分子内会出现金属化或Peierls二聚化相的局域成核现象，具体取决于分子下方表面是金属性还是绝缘性。

Conclusion: 该理论模型能够描述金属基底对tPA分子电子和晶格性质的显著影响，包括绝缘体-金属转变和相分离现象。这些发现对于正确解释现有实验数据以及设计基于有机分子的纳米电子器件具有重要价值。

Abstract: We theoretically study the electronic and lattice properties of a trans-polyacetylene (tPA) molecule deposited on top of a metallic substrate at equilibrium. We describe the system using a modified Su-Schrieffer-Heeger (SSH) model generalized to incorporate the effects of a metallic environment, represented by independent one-dimensional semi-infinite chains coupled to each site of the SSH chain (i.e., ``local bath approximation"). We focus on the zero-temperature case and obtain the physical properties of an $N$-site tPA chain deposited on a metallic surface by minimizing its total ground-state energy (i.e., electronic plus lattice degrees of freedom) as a function of the $N$ lattice-site positions. Interestingly, in the case of a homogeneous metallic substrate, where all coupling parameters are assumed identical, the SSH chain undergoes a zero-temperature insulator-to-metal transition as the coupling parameter $γ_0$ reaches a critical value where the Peierls dimerization is fully suppressed and the system becomes metallic. In addition, our model can be generalized to describe inhomogeneous situations where the substrate contains metallic and insulating regions, as usually occurs in realistic experiments containing accidentally oxidized decoupling layers. In this case, our results predict the occurrence of local nucleation of the metalized or the Peierls-dimerized phase within the same tPA molecule, depending on whether the surface directly beneath the molecule is metallic or insulating, respectively. We finally discuss the relevance of our findings for both the correct interpretation of existing tPA/Cu(110) experiments, as well as for their possible utility in the design of novel organic nanoelectronic devices.

</details>


### [124] [Flexural Cavity Mechanics in Electrostatically Driven 1D Phononic Crystal](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15893)
*Vishnu Kumar,Bhargavi B. A.,Saurabh A. Chandorkar*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该论文展示了一种基于静电换能的一维声子晶体传输系统，通过在声子晶体中嵌入双端音叉谐振器，实现了具有高Q值的机械振荡器。研究发现，位于声子带隙内的同相模式（in-phase mode）的Q值比锚定谐振器提高约两倍，而带隙外的反相模式（out-phase mode）则无此增强效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 声子晶体（phononic crystals）为控制声子（phonons）提供了多功能平台，可用于波导、滤波和传感等应用。为了最小化耗散，通常将腔体谐振器嵌入声子晶体的带隙中，并与合适的换能技术集成。

Method: 采用静电换能（electrostatic transduction）实现一维声子传输，构建了嵌入一维声子晶体中的双端音叉谐振器（double-ended tuning fork resonator）。通过该装置研究简并弯曲模式（degenerate flexural modes）——同相和反相模式在相同器件中的质量因子表现。

Result: 观察到简并弯曲模式在相同器件中表现出增强且可比的质量因子。位于声子带隙内的同相模式（in-phase mode）的质量因子比锚定谐振器（anchored resonator）提高约两倍；而在热弹性耗散（thermoelastic dissipation）可忽略的温度下，位于带隙外的反相模式（out-phase mode）的增强效应消失。

Conclusion: 该方法为实现低损耗、封装式声子器件（low-loss, encapsulated phononic devices）提供了一条有前景的技术路径，适用于传感和信号处理应用。

Abstract: Phononic Crystals provide a versatile platform for controlling phonons in applications such as waveguiding, filtering, and sensing. To minimize dissipation, cavity resonators are often embedded within the bandgap of phononic crystals and integrated with suitable transduction techniques. Here, we demonstrate one-dimensional (1D) phononic transmission using electrostatic transduction, enabling the realization of high-quality mechanical oscillators. Using a double-ended tuning fork resonator embedded in a 1D phononic crystal, we observe degenerate flexural modes (in-phase and out-phase) exhibiting enhanced and comparable quality factors within the same device due to mode degeneracy. The in-phase mode, whose frequency lies inside the phononic bandgap, shows an approximately two-fold increase in quality factor compared to an anchored resonator, while this enhancement diminishes for the out-phase mode (frequency outside the bandgap) at temperatures where thermoelastic dissipation is negligible. This approach offers a promising route toward low-loss, encapsulated phononic devices for sensing and signal processing applications.

### [125] [3D tomography of exchange phase in a Si/SiGe quantum dot device](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16025)
*Dylan Albrecht,Sarah Thompson,N. Tobias Jacobson,Ryan Jock*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究开发了一种从自旋量子比特（spin qubit）设备中稳健提取交换相互作用（exchange interaction）相位信息的方法，通过结合相位偏移数字全息术（phase-shifting digital holography）和三维相位展开技术，解决了交换系数测量中的相位模糊和噪声敏感性问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 交换相互作用（exchange interaction）是自旋量子处理器操作的基础构建模块。提取交换相互作用系数J(V)作为栅极电压的函数，对于理解器件无序性、准确模拟器件性能以及高保真度操作自旋量子比特至关重要。然而，从实验数据中提取J(V)存在困难，主要源于余弦函数反演的模糊性、相位展开对噪声的敏感性以及积分反演问题。

Method: 研究采用了一种结合多领域技术的测量方法。首先使用相位偏移数字全息术（phase-shifting digital holography）获取包裹相位（wrapped phase），然后利用最大流/最小割相位展开方法（max-flow/min-cut phase unwrapping method, PUMA）在三维电压空间中展开相位。该方法通过一系列二维测量构建三维相位体积（phase volume），并对提取的相位建立模型。

Result: 该方法对器件中观察到的最小漂移具有鲁棒性，通过增加扫描分辨率得到验证。在构建提取相位的模型后，通过模型优化定位了电压空间中具有最小梯度的π交换脉冲点。测量协议能够提供详细信息，有助于理解控制器件产率的器件变异性起源。

Conclusion: 该测量协议可为理解器件变异性起源提供详细信息，在操作期间校准特定器件的器件模型以实现更复杂的误差归因，并实现量子比特控制的系统优化。预计所提出的方法可能适用于其他量子比特平台。

Abstract: The exchange interaction is a foundational building block for the operation of spin-based quantum processors. Extracting the exchange interaction coefficient $J(\mathbf{V})$, as a function of gate electrode voltages, is important for understanding disorder, faithfully simulating device performance, and operating spin qubits with high fidelity. Typical coherent measurements of exchange in spin qubit devices yield a modulated cosine of an accumulated phase, which in turn is the time integral of exchange. As such, extracting $J(\mathbf{V})$ from experimental data is difficult due to the ambiguity of inverting a cosine, the sensitivity to noise when unwrapping phase, as well as the problem of inverting the integral. As a step toward obtaining $J(\mathbf{V})$, we tackle the first two challenges to reveal the accumulated phase, $φ(\mathbf{V})$. We incorporate techniques from a wide range of fields to robustly extract and model a 3D phase volume for spin qubit devices from a sequence of 2D measurements. In particular, we present a measurement technique to obtain the wrapped phase, as done in phase-shifting digital holography, and utilize the max-flow/min-cut phase unwrapping method (PUMA) to unwrap the phase in 3D voltage space. We show this method is robust to the minimal observed drift in the device, which we confirm by increasing scan resolution. Upon building a model of the extracted phase, we optimize over the model to locate a minimal-gradient $π$ exchange pulse point in voltage space. Our measurement protocol may provide detailed information useful for understanding the origins of device variability governing device yield, enable calibrating device models to specific devices during operation for more sophisticated error attribution, and enable a systematic optimization of qubit control. We anticipate that the methods presented here may be applicable to other qubit platforms.

Abstract: This technical note provides a high-level overview of the present state of basic field electron emission (FE) theory, as suitable for use in the context of technological applications of FE theory. At present there is much theoretical confusion in FE literature, and a partial breakdown of the peer review system. Even in sensitive technological contexts, many papers have stated and used out-of-date theory that makes current-density predictions that are several hundred times less than those of modern FE theory. A primary aim of this note is to help reduce the confusion and error in future published FE literature. It is not intended as a detailed review of FE theory.

Conclusion: 纳米尺度磁性点接触在磁阻变化方面具有高效率，且由于其结构简单，在应用方面具有良好前景。该统一理论框架为理解自旋分辨电子输运提供了重要工具。

Abstract: This work presents a unified theoretical framework for spin-resolved electron transport in magnetic point contacts (PCs) in nanoscale dimensions. This work advances existing research by presenting a model which seamlessly transitions between Sharvin ballistic and Maxwell-Holm diffusive limits across the wide range of relevant contact sizes without incorporating empirical fitting factors. We analyzed the magnetoresistance (MR) of magnetic PCs formed with two ferromagnetic monodomains that may have parallel and antiparallel magnetization alignment, forming a constrained domain wall approximately 1.0 nm wide. The calculated MR exhibits strong dependence on scaling parameter (normalized contact radius), ratios of spin-dependent mean free paths, and Fermi wave-vectors. Furthermore, the calculated MR exhibits physically meaningful behavior over a wide range of spin-asymmetry parameters. In most regimes, the MR decreases with increasing normalized point-contact radius, becoming negative at some conditions. These results demonstrate that nanoscaled magnetic PCs have great efficiency in terms of magnetoresistnace change and promising for application due to their simplicity.

Abstract: Understanding how defects influence charge separation in WS$_2$-graphene heterostructures is crucial for future applications in light harvesting and detection. Previous studies have reported widely varying lifetimes for the charge-separated state, all supposedly linked to electron trapping at sulphur vacancies. The exact impact of these defects, however, has remained unclear. Here, we deliberately introduce sulphur vacancies by annealing the heterostructures at high temperatures in ultrahigh vacuum. Angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy (ARPES) reveals that these vacancies modify both the band alignment and doping level of the heterostructure. Guided by model calculations, we attribute this behaviour to shifts in the energy alignment between sulphur vacancy states and graphene's Dirac point, combined with a reduced excitonic absorption. The model also yields a transfer time for electrons tunneling from sulphur vacancies into graphene's Dirac cone of $\sim$4ps, consistent with our trARPES measurements. Our study clarifies the role of sulphur vacancies in WS$_2$-graphene heterostructures, further improving our microscopic understanding of charge dynamics for future optoelectronic applications.

Here we chart the topological phase space of tMoTe2 at a relatively large twist angle of approximately 4.54deg, accessing a moderately correlated regime with enhanced bandwidth. ### [130] [Twist-angle evolution from valley-polarized fractional topological phases to valley-degenerate superconductivity in twisted bilayer MoTe2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16412)

Abstract: Moiré superlattices formed by semiconducting transition metal dichalcogenides (TMDs) provide a highly tunable platform for investigating strongly correlated and topological quantum phases. However, how these correlated topological phases evolve with twist angle and compete with other quantum phases in tMoTe2 remains largely unexplored. Here we report a systematic transport study of twist-angle-dependent phase diagrams in tMoTe2 across a range of 3.8°-5.78°, revealing an evolution from fractionalized states of matter with spontaneous valley polarization to valley-degenerate superconductivity. At relatively small twist angles, partially-filled Chern bands of tMoTe2 host FQAH states following the Jain sequence, together with signatures of an anomalous composite Fermi liquid at moiré hole filling factor νh = 1/2. At νh = 1, we observe a transition from robust integer quantum anomalous Hall (IQAH) insulators at small angles to displacement-field-tuned, topologically trivial correlated insulators at larger angles. Remarkably, at a twist angle of 5.78°, superconductivity emerges adjacent to the correlated insulating phase, with a phase diagram closely resembling that recently reported in twisted bilayer WSe2 (tWSe2). Our results uncover a unified twist-angle-driven phase evolution linking fractional topology, symmetry breaking, magnetic order, and superconductivity, providing new insight into the emergent quantum phenomena in moiré systems.

Motivation: 尽管电子-电子频繁碰撞可诱导集体性、类流体电子输运，为探索多体现象提供了有力框架，但目前仍缺乏主动利用电子流体动力学行为的功能性电子器件。

Method: 研究引入了固态特斯拉阀（Tesla valve）类似物——一种无移动部件的被动流体二极管。该器件通过光刻技术在高迁移率GaAs二维电子气（two-dimensional electron gas）中定义制造。

Result: 器件表现出急剧的整流特性，正反向电阻差异超过十倍。这种阈值行为类似于流体特斯拉阀中湍流起始，指向电子液体中湍流态（turbulent regime）的出现——这是长期预测但尚未观察到的电子物质状态。

Conclusion: 该工作证明了流体动力学类比的有效性：流体技术可被直接采用以创造新型电子器件。具体通过固态整流器实现，其运作依赖于粒子间碰撞（interparticle collisions）这一新物理机制。

Abstract: In solids, frequent electron-electron collisions can induse collective, fluid-like electron transport. While this regime offers a powerful framework for exploring many-body phenomena, there is still a lack in functional electronic device actively exploting hydrodynamic behaviour of electrons. Here, we introduce a solid-state analogue of a Tesla valve $\unicode{x2013}$ a passive fluidic diode that rectifies flow without moving parts. Lithographically defined in high-mobility GaAs two-dimensional electron gas, the device exhibits abrupt rectification producing a more than tenfold difference between forward and reverse resistances. This threshold behaviour, reminiscent of the onset of turbulence in fluidic Tesla valves, points to the emergence of turbulent regime in the electron liquid $\unicode{x2013}$ a long-predicted, but yet unobserved state of electronic matter. More broadly, our work demonstrates the fruitfulness of the hydrodynamic analogy: fluidic technologies can be readily adopted to create novel electronic devices. Here, this is realized through a solid-state rectifier whose operation relies on a new physical mechanism, interparticle collisions.

</details>


### [132] [Correlated Quantum Phenomena in Confined Two-Dimensional Hexagonal Crystals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16677)
*Xiang Liua,Zheng Taoa,Wenchen Luoa,Tapash Chakraborty*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维材料中的低能费米子激发偏离传统的薛定谔描述，受狄拉克方程（Dirac equations）支配，产生传统凝聚态系统中没有的非常规量子现象。量子限制为增强库仑相互作用和稳定关联量子态提供了有效途径。

Method: 本文采用综述方法，从理论和实验两个视角分析二维六方材料中的限制效应。重点考察石墨烯和TMDs量子点中的外部限制，以及扭曲范德华异质结构中莫尔超晶格（moiré superlattices）产生的涌现限制。

Result: 量子限制导致离散的电子和激子谱，强烈放大相互作用效应。莫尔超晶格产生涌现限制并诱导非平凡能带拓扑（nontrivial band topology），引发丰富的新现象。降维和空间局域化促进了多种关联态的形成。

Conclusion: 限制在塑造二维材料的量子行为中起核心作用，为基于这些态的应用提供了新机遇。近期实验和理论进展突显了限制诱导关联现象的重要性，需要从多角度深入理解这些系统。

Abstract: Low-energy fermionic excitations in two-dimensional materials deviate from the conventional Schrödinger description and are instead governed by Dirac equations. Such Dirac fermions give rise to a variety of unconventional quantum phenomena that have no direct analogues in traditional condensed matter systems. Among these materials, graphene and transition metal dichalcogenides (TMDs) represent two prototypical platforms, hosting massless and massive Dirac particles, respectively, and exhibiting rich electronic, optical, and valley dependent properties. Here we review the effect of the quantum confinement in these two-dimensional hexagonal materials that provides a powerful route to enhance Coulomb interactions and stabilizing correlated quantum states. In graphene- and TMD-based quantum dots, externally imposed confinement leads to discrete electronic and excitonic spectra, where interaction effects are strongly amplified. In twisted van der Waals heterostructures, the moiré superlattices generate emergent confinement and induce nontrivial band topology, giving rise to a wealth of novel phenomena. More generally, reduced dimensionality and spatial localization in two-dimensional materials promote a diverse range of correlated states. Recent experimental and theoretical advances highlight the central role of confinement in shaping quantum behavior and reveal new opportunities for applications based on these states. In this review, we provide an overview of recent progress in confinement-induced correlated phenomena in two-dimensional materials from both theoretical and experimental perspectives.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Recent experiments in rhombohedral graphene report an unusual superconducting phase emerging from a spin- and valley-polarized quarter-metal state. The prevailing interpretation invokes chiral topological superconductivity, but the role of the `Fulde-Ferrell' phase factor due to intra-valley pairing has remained largely unexplored. Here we show, via a gauge transformation, that this phase is equivalent to an ordinary chiral topological superconductor on the triangular lattice, while simultaneously forming an extraordinary Majorana crystal on the dual honeycomb lattice reminiscent of the Haldane model.

### [135] [Complex Wannier centers and drifting Wannier functions in non-Hermitian Hamiltonians](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16838)
*Pedro Fittipaldi de Castro,Wladimir A. Benalcazar*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究将拓扑能带理论拓展至具有线性能隙的非厄米哈密顿量体系，引入复Wannier中心概念，揭示了其物理意义在于Wannier函数的互易性破缺导致的定向漂移，并建立了基于Krein签名的体边对应关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管早期迹象表明非厄米哈密顿量具有丰富的物理内涵，但将拓扑能带理论扩展到具有线性能隙（line energy gaps）的非厄米体系仍缺乏系统研究。特别是Wilson loop在非厄米情况下变为非幺正（nonunitary）的物理后果尚不明确。

Method: 在双正交量子力学（biorthonormal quantum mechanics）框架下，引入复Wannier中心（complex Wannier centers）概念，定义为非幺正Wilson loop的规范不变特征值。分析对称性如何约束复Wannier中心，并识别伪厄米（pseudo-Hermitian）哈密顿量中的对称性保护Wannier构型。

Result: 复Wannier中心通过其关联Wannier函数的互易性破缺获得物理意义：当Wannier函数质心移至复平面时，会产生有效动量偏移，导致随时间的方向性漂移。在具有反对易伪厄米度规和（伪）反演对称性的系统中，复Wannier中心的行为可预测占据能带的填充异常（filling anomaly）及边缘模式经历增益或损耗。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了Wilson loop的Krein结构与体边对应（bulk-boundary correspondence）的联系，并提出了光子波导实现方案以实验验证理论预测，为非厄米拓扑系统的研究提供了新视角。

Abstract: The extension of topological band theory to non-Hermitian Hamiltonians with line energy gaps remains largely unexplored, despite early indications of rich underlying physics. In this setting, Wilson loops-the quantities underlying polarization-generally become nonunitary, yet the physical consequences of this nonunitarity have remained unclear. Within the framework of biorthonormal quantum mechanics, we introduce the concept of complex Wannier centers, defined from the gauge-invariant eigenvalues of nonunitary Wilson loops. Complex Wannier centers acquire physical meaning through reciprocity breaking in their associated Wannier functions: when the centroid of a Wannier function shifts into the complex plane, it acquires an effective momentum offset that produces directional drift over time. We analyze how symmetries constrain complex Wannier centers and identify symmetry-protected Wannier configurations in pseudo-Hermitian Hamiltonians, where the centers are either real or form complex-conjugate pairs, as determined by conserved "Krein signatures" of the projected metric operator of pseudo-Hermiticity. We further show that the Krein structure of the Wilson loop can establish a bulk-boundary correspondence: in a system with anticommuting pseudo-Hermitian metric and (pseudo) inversion symmetries, the behavior of complex Wannier centers predicts the existence of a filling anomaly in the occupied bands and whether the resulting edge modes experience gain or loss. Finally, we propose a photonic waveguide implementation of this system that enables experimental tests of our predictions.

### [136] [Dicovering the emergent nonlinear dynamics of acoustically levitated cube clusters](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15894)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多自然和工程系统的复杂行为源于少量有效自由度之间的相互作用。直接从实验观测中发现这些自由度之间相互作用的物理基础是一个长期挑战，特别是在预测具有未知运动方程的动力系统的长时间动力学方面。

Method: 开发了一种数据驱动方法，能够为具有弱吸引流形（weakly attracting manifold）的系统产生长时间动力学行为的生成模型。应用数值拟合程序提取最小非线性动力学模型，该模型能捕捉系统的长时间动力学和向动力学稳态的收敛。

Result: 在声悬浮立方体粒子簇实验中，发现了三个不同的非线性动力学吸引子（nonlinear dynamical attractors）持续数百个周期。动力学模型揭示了质心运动与铰链自由度之间的非线性、非互易耦合（non-reciprocal coupling）稳定了动力学吸引子，这一发现通过独立的有限元方法得到证实。

Conclusion: 研究结果展示了一种新颖的数据驱动方法，用于发现具有长时间尺度稳定预测的非线性模型，为从实验数据中提取物理相互作用提供了有效途径。

Abstract: The complex behavior of many natural and engineered systems emerges from the interaction of a small number of effective degrees of freedom. Discovering the physical basis of the interactions between these degrees of freedom directly from experimental observations has been a longstanding challenge, particularly with respect to predicting the long-time dynamics of dynamical systems with unknown equations of motion. Here, we introduce a data-driven approach that is able to produce a generative model for the long-time dynamical behavior of systems with a weakly attracting manifold. We apply this method to an experimental dynamical system with two degrees of freedom: acoustically levitated pairs of cube-shaped particles, which cluster by sharing a single edge. In the acoustic trap, the center-of-mass of the cube cluster oscillates vertically about the levitation plane, while also oscillating about their flexible hinge-like connection. Depending on their initial condition, the hinge dynamics evolve about three distinct nonlinear dynamical attractors persisting for hundreds of cycles. In order to capture the underlying physics, we develop a numerical fitting procedure and extract a minimal nonlinear dynamical model that captures both the long-time dynamics of the cluster as well as the convergence onto the dynamical steady state. This dynamical model uncovers the nonlinear, non-reciprocal coupling between the center-of-mass motion and the hinge degree of freedom that stabilizes the dynamical attractors, which we subsequently confirm by independent finite-element methods. Our results demonstrate a novel data-driven method for the discovery of nonlinear models with long-timescale stable predictions.

Abstract: We introduce an optimized protocol of fracture pattern classification using an artificial neural network to identify the solvent involved in the desiccation cracking process of starch-liquid slurries, even after it has been completely evaporated. For this purpose, image analysis techniques were used to characterize patterns obtained from drying suspensions using single solvents (water, ethanol, acetone) and two-component solvents (water-ethanol mixtures at different concentrations). Frequency histograms were generated based on nine morphological features, taking into account their size, shape, geometry and orientational ordering. Subsequently, we used these histograms as input data into artificial neural network variants to determine the set of features that lead to the higher accuracy in solvent identification. We obtained an average accuracy of $96(\pm 1)\%$ considering all solvents in the analysis. The highest accuracy was obtained with sets of features that include the crack area distribution. The proposed protocol can help to determine the combination of features that optimize pattern recognition in other fields of science and engineering.

### [138] [Condensate-mediated shape transformations of cellular membranes by capillary forces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15904)
*Lukas Hauer,Katharina Sporbeck,Joseph F. McKenna,Dmytro Puchkov,Alexander I. May,Lorenzo Frigerio,Roland L. Knorr,Amir H. Bahrami*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了生物分子凝聚体（biomolecular condensates）介导的毛细管力如何驱动膜结构形态转变，通过活细胞成像、体外重构系统和计算机模拟，揭示了界面张力调控膜管、膜片和膜杯三种形态形成的机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 具有液体特性的相分离生物分子凝聚体在细胞内组织和区室化中起关键作用。凝聚体介导的毛细管力作用于膜结构，驱动液泡和自噬体等膜结合细胞器的生理性重塑，但相关形态转变机制尚不清楚。

Method: 研究采用三种互补方法：植物活细胞成像（in planta live-cell imaging）、可调界面张力的体外重构系统（in vitro reconstitution system），以及弹性膜模型的计算机模拟（computer simulations of an elastic membrane model）。

Result: 研究发现高界面张力驱动稳定膜片形成，而低界面张力下膜管和膜杯占主导。通过计算各膜形状的自由能，识别了形态转变的能量壁垒，并发现转变过程具有膜管-膜杯滞后现象（tube-to-cup hysteresis），依赖于界面膜的历史状态。

Conclusion: 凝聚体表面特性的时间调控可介导细胞内杯状结构（如植物液泡中的"球茎"结构）的形态发生。研究结果进一步概括了凝聚体与膜相互作用如何促进细胞内组织化。

Abstract: Phase-separated biomolecular condensates with liquid-like properties play a key role in the organization and compartmentalization of the intracellular environment. Condensate-mediated capillary forces acting on membranes drive physiologically important reshaping of membrane-bound organelles, such as vacuoles and autophagosomes. Here, we explore condensate-mediated membrane shape transformations. We employ {\textit{in planta}} live-cell imaging, an \textit{in vitro} reconstitution system with tunable interfacial tension, and computer simulations of an elastic membrane model to describe three morphologies of membrane structures localized at condensate interfaces: tubes, sheets, and cups. We find that the forces associated with high interfacial tension drive the formation of stable sheets, while tubes and cups prevail at lower interfacial tension. We calculate the free energies of each membrane shape and identify the energy barriers that govern the transitions between the shapes. With this approach, we find that shape transformations depend on the history of the interfacial membrane and exhibit a tube-to-cup hysteresis. These findings indicate that temporal control of condensate surface properties can mediate the morphogenesis of cup-like structures in cells, such as the formation of "bulbs" within plant vacuoles. Our results further generalize how the interplay of condensates and membranes contributes to intracellular organization.
