### [139] [Dynamics of particle lane formation in confined viscoelastic fluids under shear](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16027)
*Hiroto Yokoyama,Masanori Honda,Rinya Miyakawa,Yuki Shinohara,Kota Nakamura,Kojiro Otoguro,Kiwamu Yoshii,Yutaka Sumino*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究开发了一种基于平行旋转盘的实验平台，用于原位观察粘弹性流体中粒子在剪切流下的链状排列动力学。研究发现排列发生在局部粒子魏森贝格数超过1时，并揭示了伴随排列过程的往复穿梭运动源于粒子的垂直位移。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管剪切流诱导粘弹性流体中粒子形成流动对齐链的现象已被报道数十年，但对排列动力学和粒子轨迹的原位直接测量仍然有限。本研究旨在开发实验平台以实时观察链形成过程中的粒子对齐动态。

Method: 开发了基于平行旋转盘的实验平台，间隙与粒子直径相当，可在径向变化的剪切速率下同时观察粒子排列。使用嵌入锆石粒子的粘弹性流体作为样品，通过粒子追踪和图像亮度分析粒子运动。建立了基于代理的最小模型，其中垂直位置遵循金兹堡-朗道型双势阱势。

Result: 研究发现当局部粒子魏森贝格数（Wiₚ）超过1时发生排列，该参数基于壁面速度和可用间隙宽度定义的有效剪切速率。粒子追踪揭示了伴随排列过程的往复穿梭运动，图像亮度分析表明该运动源于粒子的垂直位移。数值模拟显示碰撞驱动的聚集现象在强约束几何结构中通过有效吸引力实现排列。

Conclusion: 在强约束几何结构中，排列通过碰撞产生的有效吸引力实现，这让人联想到活性物质中常见的运动诱导聚集现象。研究为理解粘弹性流体中剪切诱导粒子链形成的动力学机制提供了新的实验和理论见解。

Abstract: Simple shear flow can induce flow-aligned chain formation of particles suspended in viscoelastic fluids. Although this phenomenon has been reported for decades, direct {\it in situ} measurements of the alignment dynamics and particle trajectories during chain formation remain limited. Here, we develop an {\it in situ} observation platform based on parallel rotating disks separated by a gap comparable to the particle diameter, enabling simultaneous observation of particle alignment under radially varying shear rates. The narrow gap strongly confines particle motion, thereby enhancing hydrodynamic interactions and collision events between particles. Using a viscoelastic fluid embedding zircon particles as the sample, we find that alignment occurs once the local particle Weissenberg number exceeds unity (Wi$_\mathrm{p} \geq 1$), defined using an effective shear rate based on the wall velocity and the available gap width. Particle tracking further reveals a back-and-forth shuttling motion that accompanies the alignment process. Using the image brightness in a colored fluid as a proxy for out-of-plane position, we show that the shuttling originates from vertical displacement of the particles. We further construct a minimal agent-based model in which the vertical particle position follows a Ginzburg-Landau-type double-well potential, and demonstrate that collision-driven accumulation emerges in numerical simulations. In the strongly confined geometry, alignment occurs by an effective attraction due to collision, which is reminiscent of motility-induced clustering often observed in active matter.

</details>


### [140] [Mechanical anisotropy of 3D-printed digital materials at large strains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16149)
*Seunghwan Lee,Gisoo Lee,Seounghee Yun,Sumin Lee,Jeonyoon Lee,Hansohl Cho*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究通过实验测试、显微分析和微机械建模，系统研究了3D打印数字材料（digital materials）从小应变到大应变范围内打印取向依赖的非线性力学行为，揭示了微结构异质性导致的力学各向异性机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 3D打印数字材料的力学性能可在热塑性塑料与橡胶聚合物之间变化，但其力学功能尚未充分利用，主要由于微结构异质性导致的本征力学各向异性（intrinsic mechanical anisotropy）。

Method: 结合力学测试、显微分析和微机械建模（micromechanical modeling），构建了考虑打印取向依赖扩散和混合效应的代表性体积单元（representative volume elements），以分析高度各向异性微结构特征。

Result: 微机械分析表明，软橡胶基体中排列良好的椭圆形硬热塑性夹杂物的稳定压缩变形导致了初始弹性各向异性；高长径比硬域的屈曲失稳（buckling instability）与塑性变形之间的相互作用控制了大应变下的力学各向异性，以及打印取向依赖的回弹性和能量耗散能力。

Conclusion: 该研究为理解3D打印数字材料复杂变形机制提供了综合框架，揭示了微结构特征与宏观力学性能之间的关联，特别是打印取向对材料各向异性力学行为的关键影响。

Abstract: 3D-printed digital materials whose mechanical behavior travels between those from thermoplastic to rubbery polymers have become increasingly important. However, their mechanical functionalities have not been fully exploited due to intrinsic mechanical anisotropy resulting from microstructural heterogeneity. Here, we combine mechanical testing, microscopy analysis and micromechanical modeling for a comprehensive understanding of complex deformation mechanisms responsible for the printing-orientation-dependent nonlinear mechanical behavior of digital materials at small to large strains. Towards this end, we construct representative volume elements that account for highly anisotropic microstructural features resulting from the printing-orientation-dependent diffusion and mixing between photocurable base resins. We then demonstrate, through micromechanical analysis, that stable compressive deformation of well-aligned elliptical hard thermoplastic inclusions embedded within the surrounding soft rubbery matrix gives rise to initial elastic anisotropy. Our experimental and micromechanical modeling results also show that the interplay between buckling instability and plastic deformation of the high-aspect-ratio hard domains governs mechanical anisotropy at large strains as well as the printing-orientation-dependent resilience and energy dissipation capabilities in these digital materials.

</details>


### [141] [Energy-Efficient Control of Interacting Microscopic Systems: When Longer Paths Save Energy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16205)
*Samuel Monter,Lars T. Stutzer,Sarah A. M. Loos,Clemens Bechinger*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过实验和理论探讨了多粒子系统的最优热力学控制，发现在低噪声极限下，保守相互作用不会改变最优轨迹的几何形状（保持直线运动），而非保守相互作用（如流体动力学耦合）则会产生弯曲的最优轨迹以降低能耗。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索相互作用多粒子系统在固定时间内以最节能方式在预定光阱配置间传输的最优控制问题。重点关注如何通过优化控制策略降低系统的能量消耗。

Method: 采用实验与理论相结合的方法，研究光学陷阱中囚禁的胶体粒子集合。对于具有保守成对相互作用的马尔可夫系统，在低噪声极限下建立了一般性理论结果；对于流体动力学耦合的典型情况，进行了实验验证。

Result: 在低噪声极限下，无论具体相互作用势如何，最优粒子轨迹在空间和时间上都是线性的，对应稳态直线运动。保守相互作用不改变最优路径的几何形状，但这一性质在强噪声或非保守相互作用下失效。对于流体动力学耦合，实验证明最优控制涉及弯曲轨迹，通过利用集体产生的流体流动显著降低能量成本。

Conclusion: 弯曲路径作为最优解的出现突显了非相互作用系统与相互作用系统之间的根本区别，并揭示了一种用于节能控制的合作机制。非保守相互作用可以改变最优轨迹的几何形状，为实现能量高效控制提供了新途径。

Abstract: We experimentally and theoretically study the thermodynamically optimal control of interacting multiple-particle systems, focusing on collections of colloidal particles individually confined in optical traps. We investigate protocols that transport the system between prescribed trap configurations within a fixed time in the most energy efficient way. For Markovian systems with conservative pairwise interactions, we establish a general result in the low-noise limit: optimal particle trajectories are linear in space and time, corresponding to steady straight-line motion, irrespective of the specific interaction potential, even for nonlinear forces. Thus, conservative interactions do not modify the geometry of the optimal paths. This property breaks down in the presence of strong noise or nonconservative interactions. For the paradigmatic case of hydrodynamic coupling, we demonstrate experimentally that optimal control can involve curved trajectories that significantly reduce the energetic cost by exploiting collectively generated fluid flows. The emergence of curved paths as optimal solutions highlights a fundamental distinction between non-interacting and interacting systems and reveals a cooperative mechanism for energy-efficient control.

</details>

Conclusion: 研究结果阐明了交联密度和有效网络连接性如何控制刚度、应力局部化和失效特性。该多尺度方法为连接微观结构设计参数与宏观力学性能提供了预测平台，并为下一代PSAs的配方设计和优化提供了理论基础。

Abstract: Pressure-sensitive adhesives (PSAs) are soft polymeric materials that exhibit complex rheological and mechanical behavior gov- erned by the interplay between polymer architecture, crosslink density, and entanglement constraints. Predicting their rheological properties from underlying microstructure remains a central challenge in adhesive design. In this work, we adopt a multiscale com- putational framework based on the Lagrangian Heterogeneous Multiscale Method (LHMM), coupling a macroscopic continuum description with a mesoscale polymer network model featuring breakable bonds embedded in a viscous medium. The approach enables consistent information transfer across scales and captures both elastic network response and viscous dissipation. The framework is calibrated using experimental rheological data and tensile measurements for four PSA formulations with varying gel fractions and crosslink densities. The simulations reproduce key experimental trends in storage modulus (G'), loss modulus (G"), and tensile stress-strain behavior under planar extension, while differentiating the distinct mechanical signatures of each formula- tion. The results elucidate how crosslink density and effective network connectivity control stiffness, stress localization, and failure characteristics. Overall, the proposed multiscale methodology provides a predictive platform for linking microstructural design pa- rameters to macroscopic mechanical properties and offers a rational basis for the formulation and optimization of next-generation PSAs.

### [143] [Time reversal breaking of colloidal particles in cells](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16517)

TL;DR: 该研究利用平均反向弛豫（mean back relaxation）三点关联方法检测随机轨迹数据中的时间反演对称性破缺，应用于简单驱动模型和活细胞/被动化细胞中的胶体粒子，发现微管存在是时间反演对称性破缺的主要因素，并建立了熵产生与活性能量之间的关系。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用先前提出的三点关联方法——平均反向弛豫（mean back relaxation, MBR），分析简单驱动模型以及活细胞和被动化细胞中胶体粒子的轨迹数据，并通过药物处理确定关键细胞结构的作用。

Result: MBR成功检测到模型和细胞数据中的时间反演对称性破缺，并能确定活性的相关时间和长度尺度；药物实验表明微管（microtubules）的存在是时间反演对称性破缺的主要必要条件；熵产生界限与先前确定的违反涨落耗散定理的活性能量（active energies）存在显著关联。

Conclusion: 平均反向弛豫是检测随机轨迹中时间反演对称性破缺的有效工具，在细胞系统中微管是驱动非平衡活性的关键结构，熵产生与活性能量之间的关联为量化非平衡过程提供了新视角。

Abstract: We investigate signatures of broken time reversal symmetry in stochastic trajectory data, employing the previously introduced three point correlation called mean back relaxation. We specifically investigate data from a simple driven model, as well as from colloidal particles within living or passivated biological cells. Both in the model as well as in cell data, MBR detects broken time reversal symmetry, and furthermore, allows to determine relevant time and length scales of activity. For the cells, we show, by applying various drugs, that it is predominantly the presence of microtubules which is needed for a time reversal symmetry breaking. We employ a bound for entropy production, finding that it is in striking relation to previously determined active energies that quantify violation of the fluctuation dissipation theorem.

### [144] [Optimal multi-parameter control of trapped active matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16778)
*Luke K. Davis*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文开发了一个基于自动微分精确梯度下降的计算框架，用于多参数活性物质系统的热力学优化控制，揭示了参数间动力学耦合产生的新策略，为远离平衡态的活性物质控制提供了可扩展方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高效活性物质微机器（active matter micro-machines）的实现需要远离平衡态的精确热力学控制。现有理论多关注单参数驱动且依赖严格理论假设，难以捕捉现代多参数控制实验的复杂性。

Method: 基于严谨理论考量，开发了基于自动微分（automatic differentiation）精确梯度下降的透明计算框架。该框架用于推导涉及阱刚度（trap stiffness）、阱中心（trap center）和粒子活性（particle activity）等多参数问题的最优协议，以最小化热力学功或热。

Result: 研究发现平滑且实验可行的协议（通过为控制分配动力学成本获得）能达到接近不连续"bang-bang"解的效率。探索开环和闭环控制发现，参数间的动力学耦合产生全新策略，包括最优活性循环中的对称性破缺和非单调阱刚度控制。此外，识别了初始测量与多参数灵活性结合提升效率的机制，并揭示同时执行独立优化控制仅比完整多参数解略多耗功。

Conclusion: 该工作阐明了多参数控制的非平衡物理（non-equilibrium physics），为活性物质控制提供了稳健且可扩展的策略，推动了远离平衡态热力学控制的理论与实验结合。

Abstract: The realization of efficient micro-machines built from active matter requires precise thermodynamic control far from equilibrium. Despite theoretical progress, the focus on single-parameter driving, coupled with strict theoretical assumptions, limits efforts to capture modern multi-parameter control experiments. Here, guided by careful theoretical considerations, we develop a transparent computational framework based on exact-gradient descent via automatic differentiation. We derive optimal protocols for a wide range of multi-parameter problems -- involving trap stiffness, trap center, and particle activity -- to minimize the thermodynamic work or heat. We demonstrate that smoothed, experimentally plausible protocols -- obtained by assigning kinetic costs to the controls -- achieve near-optimal efficiencies comparable to discontinuous ``bang-bang'' solutions. By exploring both open- and closed-loop control, we find the dynamical coupling between parameters leads to genuinely new strategies, including symmetry breaking in optimal activity cycles and non-monotonic trap stiffness controls. Further, we identify regimes where initial measurement and multi-parameter flexibility combine to improve efficiency. Finally, we reveal that the naive simultaneous execution of independently optimized controls incurs only slightly more work than the full multi-parameter solutions. Taken together, our work elucidates the non-equilibrium physics of multi-parameter control and provides robust, scalable strategies for controlling active matter.

### [145] [Visualizing shear-induced structures in carbon black gels by tomo-rheoscopy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16804)
*Julien Bauland,Stéphane G. Roux,Stefan Gstöhl,Christian M. Schlepütz,Michael Haist,Thibaut Divoux*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究通过X射线断层流变成像技术（X-ray tomo-rheoscopy）揭示了炭黑凝胶（carbon black gels）的弹性特性对预剪切强度的非单调依赖性，并发现流动记忆不仅由局部粒子重排决定，还编码在延伸至粒子尺寸100倍的中尺度结构组织中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 胶体凝胶（colloidal gels）的微观结构对剪切历史和溶胶-凝胶转变路径极为敏感，导致其粘弹性特性可通过剪切调控。然而，传统散射技术（如超小角X射线散射）无法探测数十至数百微米的大尺度结构异质性，限制了对其流动记忆机制的理解。

Method: 采用原位X射线断层流变成像实验，在精确控制的流变学协议下直接观察炭黑凝胶的微观结构。该方法能够揭示传统散射技术无法探测的大尺度结构特征，特别关注预剪切强度对凝胶弹性特性的影响。

Result: 实验发现凝胶弹性特性对预剪切强度呈现非单调依赖性，并观察到从数十到数百微米的显著结构异质性。低剪切增强弹性与增长的中尺度关联长度相关，而高剪切强化则未检测到中尺度重组。流动记忆不仅由局部粒子重排控制，还编码在延伸至粒子尺寸100倍的中尺度结构组织中。

Conclusion: X射线断层流变成像技术能够揭示软材料中流动历史的大尺度结构特征，为调控其力学性能开辟了新视角。胶体凝胶的流动记忆机制涉及超越局部重排的中尺度结构组织，这一发现深化了对复杂流体结构-性能关系的理解。

Abstract: Suspensions of attractive particles form space-spanning networks that endow the suspension with solid-like behavior at rest. The microstructure of these colloidal gels depends sensitively on the shear history and on the path followed across the sol-gel transition, resulting in viscoelastic properties that can be tuned by shear. Here, we report in situ X-ray tomo-rheoscopy experiments on carbon black gels whose elastic properties exhibit a non-monotonic dependence on the shear intensity applied prior to flow cessation. By directly imaging the gel microstructure under a well-controlled rheological protocol, we reveal the emergence of pronounced structural heterogeneities extending from tens to hundreds of microns -- length scales far larger than those accessible by conventional scattering techniques such as Ultra-Small Angle X-ray Scattering. In particular, we show that only the low-shear reinforcement of elasticity correlates with a growing mesoscale correlation length, while high-shear strengthening occurs without detectable mesoscale reorganization. These observations demonstrate that flow memory in colloidal gels is not solely governed by local particle rearrangements, but is also encoded in a mesoscale structural organization extending up to 100 times the particle size. More broadly, this work highlights the power of X-ray tomo-rheoscopy to uncover large-scale structural signatures of flow history in soft materials, opening new perspectives to tailor their mechanical properties.

### [146] [Thermo-Rheological Memory of $κ$-Carrageenan Fluid Gels Formed Under Flow](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16820)
*Julien Bauland,Tim J. Wooster,Peter Fischer,Jan Vermant*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 流体凝胶（fluid gels）作为在溶胶-凝胶转变过程中通过剪切形成的软材料，在食品、医疗等领域具有应用潜力。然而，尽管已知其微观结构和力学性能取决于凝胶化过程中的剪切条件，但连接这些特征的统一物理框架仍然缺乏。

Method: 以κ-卡拉胶（κ-carrageenan）凝胶为模型体系，结合流变学（rheology）和共聚焦显微镜（confocal microscopy）技术，研究其剪切诱导的结构化过程。通过分析剪切与颗粒间粘附力的竞争关系，引入粘附数（Adhesion number）进行量化表征。

Result: 研究发现κ-卡拉胶凝胶在流动条件下形成时存在热流变记忆（thermo-rheological memory），这源于剪切与颗粒间粘附力的竞争。其微观结构演化类似于简单剪切流下吸引性颗粒分散体的行为，从而连接了大分子凝胶和颗粒凝胶。

Conclusion: 该物理框架为在不改变组成的情况下调控流体凝胶性能提供了途径，建立了连接剪切条件、微观结构和力学性能的统一理论框架。

Abstract: Fluid gels are soft materials formed by shearing biopolymer solutions during the sol-gel transition. Their ability to yield and flow beyond a critical stress makes them attractive for designing versatile, biocompatible materials in food, health care and medical applications. Although it is well established that both microstructure and mechanical properties depend on the shear applied during gelation, a unified physical framework linking these features remains lacking. Here, using $κ$-carrageenan gels as a model system, we use a combination of rheology and confocal microscopy to tackle their shear-induced structuring in fluid gels. We identify a thermo-rheological memory in $κ$-carrageenan gels formed under flow and show that it arises from a competition between shear and interparticle adhesion, captured by an Adhesion number. The resulting microstructural evolution is reminiscent of the behavior of attractive particulate dispersions under simple shear flow, thereby bridging gels made of macromolecules and particulate gels. This framework provides a route to tune fluid gel properties without altering their composition.

### [147] [Three-Dimensional Modified Dirac Oscillator in Standard and Generalized Doubly Special Relativity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15632)
*Abdelmalek Boumali,Nosratollah Jafari*

Main category: physics.gen-ph

TL;DR: 本文为双狭义相对论（DSR）中的狄拉克振子（Dirac oscillator）构建了三维可精确求解的基准模型，研究了普朗克尺度变形对相对论性能谱的影响，发现变形会改变量子数与能量间的代数关系，产生分支依赖的能移。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 双狭义相对论（Doubly Special Relativity, DSR）引入了除光速c外另一个与观测者无关的高能标度，这会改变相对论运动学。本文旨在为自旋-½领域的此类变形开发一个三维可精确求解的基准模型。

Method: 基于Moshinsky和Szczepaniak的原始构造，通过线性非最小动量耦合引入狄拉克振子（Dirac oscillator）。随后在两种标准DSR实现（Amelino-Camelia和Magueijo-Smolin）以及基于普朗克长度一阶展开的广义DSR框架中纳入普朗克尺度变形。

Result: 在所有情况下，束缚态本征函数保持了球对称性决定的振子旋量结构，而DSR变形改变了量子数(N,j,ℓ)与相对论能量之间的代数关系，对粒子和反粒子解都产生了分支依赖的能移。未变形极限（k→∞或l_p→0）可平滑恢复，且变形信号随激发通过振子标度和自旋-轨道分裂而增强。

Conclusion: 狄拉克振子为研究DSR变形提供了有效的三维可精确求解基准模型，揭示了普朗克尺度效应如何通过改变量子数与能量的代数关系来影响相对论性能谱，为理解高能标度下的物理提供了理论工具。

Abstract: % Doubly Special Relativity (DSR) introduces, besides the invariant speed of light $c$, an observer-independent high-energy % scale that deforms relativistic kinematics and can be implemented through modified dispersion relations or effective % wave equations with energy-dependent spatial operators. In this work we develop a three-dimensional, exactly solvable % benchmark for such deformations in the spin-$\tfrac12$ sector: the Dirac oscillator. Following the original % construction of Moshinsky and Szczepaniak, the oscillator is introduced through a linear non-minimal momentum coupling, % which preserves Hermiticity and yields, after decoupling the Dirac equation into large and small components, a % three-dimensional isotropic harmonic-oscillator operator supplemented by a strong spin--orbit term. % We then incorporate Planck-scale deformations in two standard DSR realizations (Amelino--Camelia and % Magueijo--Smolin, characterized by an invariant energy scale $k$) and in a generalized DSR framework based on a % first-order expansion in the Planck length $l_p$. In all cases the bound-state eigenfunctions retain the % oscillator-spinor structure dictated by spherical symmetry, while DSR deforms the algebraic relation between quantum % numbers $(N,j,\ell)$ and the relativistic energy, producing branch-dependent shifts for both particle and antiparticle % solutions. The undeformed limit ($k\to\infty$ or $l_p\to0$) is recovered smoothly and the deformation signal increases % with excitation through the oscillator scale and spin--orbit splitting.

</details>


<div id='astro-ph.HE'></div>

# astro-ph.HE [[Back]](#toc)

### [148] [Hankel low-rank matrix approximation for gravitational-wave data analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15740)
*Nicholas Geissler,Vladimir Strokov,Christian Kümmerle,Sergey Kushnarev,Emanuele Berti*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文探索了基于汉克尔矩阵（Hankel matrices）的降噪技术，用于下一代引力波（gravitational-wave）探测器的信号提取，通过三种算法（ESPRIT、Cadzow迭代、迭代重加权最小二乘法）实现了接近最优的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 下一代引力波探测器（如激光干涉空间天线LISA）将观测到大量重叠信号，从仪器噪声和相互干扰中分离这些信号构成重大数据分析挑战。

Method: 采用基于汉克尔矩阵嵌入的降噪技术：将时间序列嵌入汉克尔矩阵，n个（阻尼）正弦波的叠加对应秩为2n的矩阵，从而将信号提取问题转化为结构化低秩逼近问题。使用针对引力波应用合成的数据，对三种汉克尔基算法进行基准测试：ESPRIT、Cadzow迭代和迭代重加权最小二乘法（IRLS）。

Result: 三种算法均实现了接近费希尔矩阵界限的最优性能，表现为失配与信噪比的平方反比缩放关系。测试场景包括孤立和多分量单色信号、紧密间隔频率源的分辨以及黑洞准正则模（QNM）的恢复。数值相对论波形的概念验证应用证实了这些算法从铃荡信号中提取准正则模频率的能力。

Conclusion: 汉克尔低秩逼近为预处理引力波时间序列提供了一条透明且计算高效的途径。

Abstract: Next-generation gravitational-wave (GW) detectors, such as the Laser Interferometer Space Antenna (LISA), will observe vast numbers of overlapping signals. Disentangling these signals from instrumental noise and from one another constitutes a significant data analysis challenge. We explore a denoising technique based on embedding time series into Hankel matrices: a superposition of $n$ (damped) sinusoids corresponds to a matrix of rank $2n$. Thus, the problem of signal extraction is reduced to a structured low-rank approximation problem. Using synthetic data tailored to GW applications, we benchmark three Hankel-based algorithms: ESPRIT, Cadzow iterations, and iteratively reweighted least squares (IRLS). Our test scenarios include isolated and multi-component monochromatic signals, the resolution of sources with closely spaced frequencies, and the recovery of black hole quasinormal modes (QNM). All three algorithms achieve near-optimal performance consistent with Fisher matrix bounds, evidenced by an inverse-square scaling of the mismatch with the signal-to-noise ratio. Furthermore, a proof-of-concept application to numerical relativity waveforms validates the ability of these algorithms to extract QNM frequencies from ringdown signals. Hankel low-rank approximation therefore offers a transparent, computationally efficient avenue for preprocessing GW time series.

</details>


### [149] [Detectability of Nearby Binary Neutron Stars with Future sub-mHz Gravitational Wave Missions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16386)
*Zhiwei Chen,Youjun Lu,Yuchao Luo,Jihui Zhang,Xiao Guo,Jifeng Liu,Wei-Tou Ni*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 该研究评估了下一代亚毫赫兹引力波探测器（包括LISAmax、Folkner和eASTROD）对银河系内双中子星系统的探测能力。通过种群合成模拟和信噪比计算，发现这些探测器在5-10年观测期内可探测数百至上千个银河系双中子星，其中LISAmax特别擅长探测高偏心率系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 双中子星（binary neutron stars, BNSs）是重要的引力波源，为研究大质量双星演化和核物理提供关键信息。超越现有LISA、Taiji和Tianqin任务，下一代空间引力波观测站旨在探索亚毫赫兹（sub-mHz）至微赫兹（μHz）频段，预期在探测银河系偏心双中子星系统方面表现更优。

Method: 采用致密双星种群合成模拟生成模拟双中子星样本，并计算每个引力波探测器在5-10年观测期内的信噪比（signal-to-noise ratios, SNRs）。研究评估了LISAmax、Folkner和eASTROD等下一代亚毫赫兹探测器的探测能力。

Result: LISAmax可探测约520-900个银河系双中子星，而Folkner和eASTROD可探测约780-1370个。LISAmax在探测高偏心率系统（e>0.90）方面表现突出，因其在相对较高的亚毫赫兹频率具有更高灵敏度。研究还识别了7个已观测的射电双中子星作为验证候选，其中J0737-3039的信噪比可达约100。

Conclusion: 下一代亚毫赫兹引力波任务在揭示双中子星形成和演化物理方面具有显著潜力。这些探测器在5-10年观测期内预计可探测约4-18个大麦哲伦云（LMC）内的双中子星，但探测小麦哲伦云（SMC）内的双中子星仍具挑战性。

Abstract: Binary neutron stars (BNSs) are one of the most important gravitational wave (GW) sources, which provide key insights to evolution of massive binary stars and nuclear physics. Beyond Laser Interferometer Space Antenna (LISA), Taiji, and Tianqin missions, proposed concepts for next generation space-based GW observatories, including LISAmax, Folkner, and eASTROD, aim to explore the sub-millihertz (mHz) to microhertz ($μ$ Hz) frequency band. Because the proposed designs substantially suppress low-frequency noise, these detectors are expected to outperform LISA, Taiji, and Tianqin in detecting eccentric Galactic BNS systems. In this paper, we estimate the detectability of nearby inspiraling BNSs using future sub-mHz GW detectors. By utilizing compact binary population synthesis simulations to generate mock BNS samples and estimate their signal-to-noise ratios (SNRs) correspondingly for each GW detector over an observation period of $5-10$\,years, we find that LISAmax may detect $\sim 520-900$ Galactic BNSs, whereas Folkner and eASTROD may detect $\sim 780-1370$ Galactic BNSs. Notably, LISAmax excels in detecting highly eccentric systems $(e>0.90)$ owing to its higher sensitivity at relatively higher sub-mHz frequencies. We further identify seven observed radio BNSs as viable candidates for validation, in particular J0737-3039, which reaches an SNR of $\sim 100$. The expected detection number of LMC inspiraling BNSs is about $\sim 4-18$ for these sub-mHz detectors over an observation period of $5-10$\,years, while detecting inspiraling BNSs in SMC is challenging. This study highlights the significant potential of future sub-mHz GW missions in unraveling BNS formation and evolution physics.

</details>

### [150] [Towards high-pressure noble gaseous detectors for coherent elastic neutrino-nucleus scattering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15866)
*Leire Larizgoitia*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 该论文系统研究了相干弹性中微子-原子核散射（CEνNS）的探测，评估了多种中微子源（反应堆、散裂、太阳）和目标材料，重点分析了欧洲散裂中子源（ESS）作为理想探测场址的可行性，并开发了新型探测技术包括紧凑型中子散射相机和高气压惰性气体时间投影室。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 相干弹性中微子-原子核散射（CEνNS）是低能中微子的主导相互作用过程，但由于其弱尺度截面和微小的核反冲能量，实验探测极具挑战性。本研究旨在探索CEνNS探测的科学动机和技术可行性，推动这一重要物理过程的实验研究。

Method: 研究采用多种方法：评估不同中微子源（反应堆、散裂、太阳）和目标材料；通过模拟确定欧洲散裂中子源（ESS）的最佳探测位置；开发紧凑型4π中子散射相机，集成光学成像并使用先进鉴别算法和神经网络；设计并测试GanESS高气压惰性气体时间投影室，采用电致发光放大技术；使用Garfield++和COMSOL进行详细模拟分析。

Result: 模拟显示在ESS钨靶约24米处可实现最佳信噪比，仅需最小屏蔽。开发的中子散射相机能有效表征中子本底并定位源。GanESS的气体原型（GaP）在8.62巴氩气压力下达到0.42±0.04 keVee的能量阈值，表现出稳定的高压性能。虽然低E/p区域存在非线性响应问题，但整体为散裂源CEνNS研究奠定了坚实基础。

Conclusion: 该工作为散裂源CEνNS研究建立了坚实基础，并推进了探测技术的发展，对中微子物理和稀有事件搜寻具有更广泛的意义。欧洲散裂中子源被确认为特别有前景的探测场址，同时开发的GanESS时间投影室技术展现出良好的探测性能。

Abstract: Coherent elastic neutrino-nucleus scattering (CE$ν$NS) is a dominant low-energy neutrino interaction that remains experimentally challenging due to its weak-scale cross section and the small nuclear recoil energies involved. This thesis explores the scientific motivations and technical feasibility of CE$ν$NS\ detection, emphasizing the use of diverse neutrino sources -reactor, spallation, and solar- and multiple target materials. The European Spallation Source (ESS) is identified as a particularly promising site, with simulations indicating an optimal signal-to-background ratio achievable with minimal shielding at a location $\sim$24 meters from the tungsten target. Alternative facilities, such as JPARC-MFL, are also evaluated given construction delays at ESS. A significant contribution of this work is the development of a compact, low-cost, 4$π$ neutron scatter camera with integrated optical imaging, capable of characterizing neutron backgrounds and localizing sources using advanced discrimination algorithms and neural networks. Additionally, the thesis presents the design and early testing of GanESS, a novel high-pressure noble gas time projection chamber with electroluminescence amplification, optimized for CE$ν$NS detection using argon, xenon, or krypton. The Gaseous Prototype (GaP) demonstrates a promising energy threshold of 0.42$\pm$0.04 $\rm{keV}_{\rm{ee}}$ at 8.62 bar of argon and stable high-pressure performance. Detailed simulations using Garfield++ and COMSOL provide insights into electroluminescence behavior and threshold estimation, although some non-linear detector responses at low E/p remain unresolved. Overall, this work establishes a robust foundation for CE$ν$NS studies at spallation sources and advances detection technologies with broader implications for neutrino physics and rare-event searches.

</details>


### [151] [Investigating Ultra-Low Energy Ionization Yield from Nuclear Recoils in Semiconductor Detectors via Molecular Dynamics Simulations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16702)
*Chang-Hao Fang*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于分子动力学模拟的新方法，用于评估晶体半导体探测器中的核反冲电离产额，解决了传统Lindhard模型的局限性，并在硅和锗探测器中取得了与实验数据的最佳一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 核反冲电离产额（nuclear recoil ionization yield）是暗物质（dark matter, DM）和相干弹性中微子-原子核散射（coherent elastic neutrino-nucleus scattering, CEνNS）实验低能探测中的关键不确定性来源。传统Lindhard模型存在固有局限性，需要新的方法来准确评估电离产额。

Method: 采用分子动力学模拟（molecular dynamics simulations）的非参数化方法，通过显式纳入晶体凝聚态效应（crystal condensed matter effects），克服了传统Lindhard模型的限制。该方法能够实现从高能区（E>10 keV）到电子-空穴对（electron-hole pair, EHP）区域的无缝可靠评估。

Result: 该模型在硅探测器中取得了迄今为止与实验数据的最佳一致性，特别是在单个EHP的最小能量水平上。对离子输运机制的细致考虑揭示了基本的电离产额分布，取代了传统的单值模型。分布范式将DM-核子弹性散射排除极限扩展到0.29 GeV/c²（在单EHP灵敏度下）。

Conclusion: 该方法为晶体半导体探测器中的电离产额评估提供了创新解决方案，显著提高了低能探测的准确性。进一步报告了在高纯锗探测器中影响电离产额的量子效应和沟道现象（channeling phenomena）建模方面的进展。

Abstract: Nuclear recoil ionization yield constitutes a critical uncertainty source in low-energy detection for dark matter (DM) and coherent elastic neutrino-nucleus scattering (CE$ν$NS) experiments. We present a novel methodology employing molecular dynamics simulations to assess ionization yields in crystalline semiconductor detectors. This non-parameterized approach resolving inherent limitations of traditional Lindhard model through explicit incorporation of crystal condensed matter effects, facilitating a seamless reliability from high-energy ($E>10$\,keV) to electron-hole pair (EHP) regimes. Our model achieves the best agreement with experimental data in silicon to date, especially at the minimal energy level of a single EHP. Meticulously consideration of ion transport mechanisms reveals fundamental ionization yield distributions, superseding conventional single-value models. The distributional paradigm extends the DM-nucleon elastic scattering exclusion limit to 0.29\,GeV/$c^2$ under single-EHP sensitivity. We further report advancements in modeling quantum effects and channeling phenomena affecting ionization yields in high-purity germanium detectors.

</details>


### [152] [Advances in the Fabrication of On-chip Superconducting Integral Field Units for CMB and Line-Intensity Astronomy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16627)
*L. G. G. Olde Scholtenhuis,D. Perez Capelo,K. Karatsu,D. J. Thoen,A. J. van der Linden,S. O. Dabironezare,L. H. Marting,J. J. A. Baselmans,S. Vollebregt,A. Endo*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 该论文针对宇宙微波背景（CMB）和宇宙红外背景（CIB）的大规模光谱与偏振测量需求，开发了新型片上超导光谱仪组件与制造技术，成功制备了十四像元积分视场单元（IFU）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究宇宙微波背景（Cosmic Microwave Background, CMB）的偏振和光谱畸变，结合宇宙红外背景（Cosmic Infrared Background, CIB）的强度涨落，有助于验证宇宙暴胀假设并探究过去100亿年星系团的动力学与演化。然而，CMB的宽带发射和全天延展特性使得详细观测非常耗时且昂贵。

Method: 论文提出了多项片上超导光谱仪技术改进：引入交叉结构以区分信号偏振；通过局部优化共面波导（coplanar-waveguide, CPW）光刻技术最小化信号损耗；通过沉积介质层降低微带滤波器的光谱分辨率；通过移除单个线路短路提高光谱仪阵列的成品率。

Result: 这些技术改进共同促成了十四像元积分视场单元（integral field unit, IFU）的成功制备，为CMB大规模光谱和偏振巡天提供了关键的技术基础。

Conclusion: 片上超导光谱仪技术因其紧凑尺寸和背景极限灵敏度，特别适合在相对未充分探索的电磁频谱范围内进行快速大面积观测。论文开发的新型组件和制造技术解决了当前技术尚未满足CMB大规模光谱偏振巡天要求的问题。

Abstract: Studying the polarization and spectral distortion of the Cosmic Microwave Background (CMB) in tandem with intensity fluctuations of the Cosmic Infrared Background (CIB) allows us to verify our assumptions on cosmic inflation and investigate the dynamics and evolution of galaxy clusters in the last 10 billion years. Because of its broadband emission and being an all-sky extended source, observing the entire CMB in detail is a very time-consuming and expensive exercise. Fortunately, in the last few years, the on-chip superconducting spectrometer technology has moved out of the lab and into the telescope. With its compact size and background-limited sensitivity, this family of instruments is particularly well-suited for fast and large area observations in a relatively unexplored range of the electromagnetic spectrum. However, recent examples of this technology do not yet reach the requirements needed for large spectroscopic and polarimetric surveys of the CMB. We formulate several of these requirements and introduce novel on-chip components and fabrication techniques. We introduce a cross-over to enable distinguishing signal polarization, minimize signal loss by locally optimized lithography of a coplanar-waveguide (CPW), lower the spectral resolution of microstrip filters by deposition of a dielectric layer, and increase the yield of the spectrometer array by removing individual line shorts. These together have culminated in the successful fabrication of a fourteen-spaxel IFU.

</details>

### [153] [Correlated inhomogeneous absorption profiles across distinct optical transitions in a rare-earth doped crystal](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15630)
*Flora Segur,Sacha Welinski,Alban Ferrier,Perrine Berger,Anne Louchet-Chauvet*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 该研究首次在Er³⁺:YSO晶体中揭示了两个光学跃迁之间的光谱相关性，通过在一个跃迁上烧孔同时监测另一个跃迁，为稀土掺杂晶体中非均匀分布的微观起源提供了新见解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 稀土离子掺杂晶体中的非均匀吸收谱反映了单个离子所处局部环境的分布。虽然每个光学跃迁以不同方式探测这一分布，但其精细光谱结构可能保留由共享局部扰动产生的相关性。研究旨在探索不同跃迁之间的光谱关联性。

Method: 采用低温高分辨光谱技术，在Er³⁺:YSO晶体中研究980 nm处的⁴I₁₅/₂ - ⁴I₁₁/₂跃迁，并与已知的1.5 μm处⁴I₁₅/₂ - ⁴I₁₃/₂跃迁进行比较。通过在一个跃迁上进行光谱烧孔（spectral hole burning）同时监测另一个跃迁，揭示跃迁间的光谱相关性。

Result: 首次在两个光学跃迁之间发现了光谱相关性，这一发现为理解稀土掺杂晶体中非均匀分布的微观起源提供了新的视角。

Conclusion: 该研究通过光谱烧孔技术成功揭示了Er³⁺:YSO晶体中不同光学跃迁之间的光谱关联性，为稀土离子局部环境分布的微观机制提供了重要实验证据。

Abstract: In rare-earth ion-doped crystals, inhomogeneous absorption profiles reflect the distribution of local environments experienced by individual ions. While each optical transition probes this distribution differently, their fine spectral structures may retain correlations arising from shared local perturbations. In this paper, we present a low-temperature, high-resolution spectroscopic study in Er$^{3+}$:YSO of the transition $^{4}I_{15/2}$ - $^{4}I_{11/2}$ at 980 nm and compare it to the well-known transition $^{4}I_{15/2}$ - $^{4}I_{13/2}$ at 1.5 $μ$m. Using spectral hole burning on one transition while monitoring the other, we uncover for the first time spectral correlations between two optical transitions, providing new insight into the microscopic origin of inhomogeneous distributions in rare-earth-doped crystals.

### [154] [A Route to Pure Optical Rotation in Self-Assembled Materials through Energetic Non-Degeneracy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15938)
*Daniel J. Gracias,Thomas J. Ugras,Richard D. Robinson*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于非简并耦合（non-degenerate coupling）的理论指导设计原则，用于在自组装系统中实现"纯"光学旋转（pure optical rotation），即大光学旋转同时具有最小椭圆率和吸收。通过实验验证和结构设计，展示了在光谱非共振区域产生强圆双折射（circular birefringence）而弱圆二色性（circular dichroism）和吸收的机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实现"纯"光学旋转（即大光学旋转同时具有最小椭圆率和吸收）是手性光子学（chiral photonics）的核心挑战。溶液处理的自组装材料虽然能表现出优异的手性光学响应（g因子>1），但其圆双折射（CB）通常与圆二色性（CD）和共振损耗（吸收）重叠，导致椭圆化、衰减的信号。

Method: 建立了一个通用的理论指导设计原则，表明非简并性（non-degeneracy）为自组装系统中的纯光学旋转提供了一条途径。使用广义耦合振子框架（generalized coupled-oscillator framework），证明打破相互作用发色团激发态之间的简并性可以在CD和吸收自然较弱的光谱区域产生CB。通过α-和β-CdS魔幻尺寸团簇（magic-sized clusters）的混合组装进行实验验证，并设计了交替发色团平面的层状结构以最大化非简并邻居。

Result: 实验验证了预测的非共振、涌现的圆双折射（CB）。层状结构设计产生了优化纯旋转的光学响应线型。模拟预测了一个50 meV（12 THz）的窗口，表现出约20°的低色散光学旋转、>40%的透射率和<1°的椭圆率，这些性能基准通常与光刻超材料（lithographic metamaterials）相关。

Conclusion: 非简并耦合被确立为工程化手性光学响应的通用机制，并为在自组装系统中实现纯光学旋转提供了策略。该机制仅依赖于偶极耦合（dipolar coupling）和能量失谐（energetic detuning），因此可推广到包括紫外（~310 nm）在内的不同波长范围。

Abstract: Achieving large optical rotation with minimal ellipticity and absorption, 'pure' optical rotation, remains a central challenge in chiral photonics. Solution-processed self-assembled materials can exhibit exceptional chiroptical responses (g-factors > 1), yet their circular birefringence (CB) typically overlaps with circular dichroism (CD) and resonant loss (Absorption), leading to elliptical, attenuated signals. Here, we establish a general, theory-guided design principle showing that non-degeneracy provides a route towards pure optical rotation in self-assembled systems. Using a generalized coupled-oscillator framework, we demonstrate that breaking degeneracy between the excited states of interacting chromophores produces CB in spectral regions where CD and absorption are naturally weak. We experimentally validate this mechanism using mixed assemblies of $α$- and $β$-CdS magic-sized clusters, which exhibit the predicted off-resonant, emergent CB. Guided by this principle, we design a layered architecture that maximizes non-degenerate neighbors through alternating chromophore planes. This structural architecture results in optical response lineshapes optimized for pure rotation. Because the mechanism relies solely on dipolar coupling and energetic detuning, it is generalizable across wavelengths, including in the ultraviolet (~310 nm), where suitable nanocrystal and organic chromophores are readily available. Simulations predict a 50 meV (12 THz) window exhibiting low-dispersion optical rotation of ~20°, >40% transmission, and <1° ellipticity-strong performing benchmarks typically associated with lithographic metamaterials. These results establish non-degenerate coupling as a general mechanism for engineering chiroptical response and provide a strategy for realizing pure optical rotation in self-assembled systems.

</details>


### [155] [Superballistic transport of thermal photons in confined many-body systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16296)
*Jian Dong,Junming Zhao,Philippe Ben-Abdallah,Linhua Liu*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 该研究预测了一种超越传统弹道极限的超弹道辐射热输运（superballistic radiative heat transport）机制，在受限腔内的等离子体纳米粒子稀链中实现了热导率随系统尺寸的超线性增长（k ~ L^1.5）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点认为弹道输运（ballistic transport）是能量传输的终极极限，但本研究旨在探索超越这一极限的可能性，为超快光子热输运建立新框架。

Method: 研究分析了受限腔内等离子体纳米粒子（plasmonic nanoparticles）稀链中的辐射热输运，重点关注腔引导模式（cavity-guided modes）介导的长程相互作用放大效应。

Result: 发现了超弹道热输运机制，其有效热导率呈现超线性标度关系（k ~ L^1.5），超越了传统弹道输运极限，这一异常机制源于腔引导模式对长程相互作用的放大。

Conclusion: 该研究为超快光子热输运建立了新框架，为量子与纳米尺度系统中的热管理、信息处理和能量传输开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Ballistic transport, realized when the system size is smaller than the mean free path of energy carriers, is traditionally regarded as the ultimate limit for energy transfer. Here, we predict a superballistic radiative heat transport regime that surpasses this limit in dilute chains of plasmonic nanoparticles confined within cavities. This anomalous regime exhibits superlinear scaling of the effective thermal conductivity (k ~L^1.5) and originates from the amplification of long-range interactions mediated by cavity-guided modes. Our results establish a framework for ultrafast photonic heat transport and open pathways for thermal management, information processing and energy transfer in quantum and nanoscale systems.

### [156] [Optical Magnus effect on gravitational lensing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15697)
*Yusuke Nishida*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究从弯曲时空中的麦克斯韦方程组出发，推导了圆偏振光波包的运动方程，研究了光学马格努斯效应（optical Magnus effect）对引力透镜的影响，发现该效应会阻止点源形成爱因斯坦环（Einstein ring）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 光学马格努斯效应是光轨迹因其偏振态而产生的横向偏移，作为几何光学的波长线性阶修正。研究旨在从弯曲时空的麦克斯韦方程组出发，系统推导并澄清该效应的理论框架，并探索其在引力透镜中的可能后果。

Method: 从弯曲时空中的麦克斯韦方程组出发，推导圆偏振光波包的运动方程。通过构建包含光学马格努斯效应的修正透镜方程，研究施瓦西时空（Schwarzschild spacetime）和膨胀时空中弱引力势下的引力透镜效应。

Result: 推导结果确认了已知的螺旋度依赖异常速度（helicity-dependent anomalous velocity）并进行了推广和澄清。研究发现，对于任何轴对称薄透镜，点源都无法形成爱因斯坦环。针对简单透镜模型获得了修正透镜方程的解析解，阐明了光学马格努斯效应如何影响成像过程。

Conclusion: 光学马格努斯效应作为几何光学的偏振相关修正，对引力透镜成像具有显著影响，特别是阻止了点源形成完美的爱因斯坦环，为弯曲时空中偏振光传播提供了更精确的理论描述。

Abstract: The optical Magnus effect refers to transverse shift of a trajectory of light caused by its polarization and appears as a correction to geometrical optics at the linear order in wavelength. Here, we start from Maxwell's equations in a curved spacetime to derive the equation of motion for a wave packet of circularly polarized light, which confirms the known result involving the helicity-dependent anomalous velocity with some generalization and clarification. We then study possible consequences of the optical Magnus effect on gravitational lensing in the Schwarzschild spacetime as well as under a weak gravitational potential in an expanding spacetime. Among others, by formulating the lens equation modified to incorporate the optical Magnus effect, the Einstein ring is found impossible to emerge from a point source for any axially symmetric thin lens. Analytic solutions to the modified lens equation are also obtained for simple lens models, illuminating how image formation is affected by the optical Magnus effect.

</details>


### [157] [Impact of numerical-relativity waveform calibration on parametrized post-Einsteinian tests](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15765)
*Simone Mezzasoma,Carl-Johan Haster,Nicolás Yunes*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 研究发现引力波波形模型IMRPhenomD的数值相对论校准误差可能导致在参数化后爱因斯坦框架中虚假检测广义相对论偏离，而使用包含校准不确定性的改进模型可避免此类误报。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前引力波观测为强场高动态区域检验广义相对论提供了可能，但参数化后爱因斯坦框架通常假设基础波形模型的系统不确定性可忽略。本研究旨在探究数值相对论校准误差如何导致广义相对论偏离的虚假检测。

Method: 采用包含不确定性的IMRPhenomD改进版本，该模型重新校准至一组数值相对论替代波形并配备拟合系数的概率描述。将广义相对论一致信号注入O5地基探测器网络，使用原始IMRPhenomD模型结合参数化后爱因斯坦相位变形进行恢复分析。

Result: 使用原始模型时，网络信噪比低至60即可产生广义相对论的虚假违反；而使用不确定性感知模型时，即使信噪比高达330，推断的参数化后爱因斯坦相位变形仍保持与零一致。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，为可靠进行广义相对论的螺旋阶段检验，必须考虑数值相对论校准不确定性。将校准不确定性明确纳入波形模型可保持稳健检验广义相对论的能力。

Abstract: Testing general relativity in the strong-field and highly dynamical regime is now possible through current gravitational-wave observations, where even a single high-quality detection can place competitive constraints on deviations from Einstein's theory. The parametrized post-Einsteinian framework provides a theory-agnostic approach to search for such deviations, but it typically assumes that systematic uncertainties in the base waveform model, particularly those arising from calibration to numerical relativity, are negligible. In this work, we investigate how calibration errors in the late-inspiral fitting coefficients of the IMRPhenomD waveform model can lead to spurious detections of departures from general relativity in parametrized tests. We use an uncertainty-aware version of IMRPhenomD, recalibrated to a set of numerical relativity surrogate waveforms and equipped with a probabilistic description of its fitting coefficients, to simulate general-relativity-consistent signals. We inject these signals into an O5 ground-based detector network and recover them with the original IMRPhenomD model augmented with a parametrized post-Einsteinian phase deformation. We find that false violations of general relativity using this model arise for network signal-to-noise ratios as low as 60. When the uncertainty-aware model is used instead, the inferred parametrized post-Einsteinian phase deformation remains consistent with zero even for signals with a signal-to-noise ratio up to 330. These results demonstrate the need to account for numerical relativity calibration uncertainty in order to perform reliable inspiral tests of general relativity. They also illustrate that explicitly incorporating numerical relativity calibration uncertainty into the waveform model preserves our ability to robustly test general relativity.

</details>


### [158] [Quasi-pole quintessential inflation in metric-affine gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15776)
*Konstantinos Dimopoulos,Christian Dioguardi,Ioannis D. Gialamas,Antonio Racioppi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在度量仿射引力（metric-affine gravity）框架下研究精粹暴胀（quintessential inflation），发现Holst不变量的非最小耦合可产生类Starobinsky现象学，同时该机制也能在暗能量时期"压平"标量势，为精粹暴胀提供成功框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索度量仿射引力框架下的精粹暴胀模型，该模型旨在统一描述宇宙早期暴胀和晚期暗能量加速膨胀两个阶段。

Method: 采用度量仿射引力理论框架，通过引入与Holst不变量的非最小耦合（non-minimal couplings），利用准极点（quasi-pole）行为机制来构建模型。

Result: 模型与所有观测约束一致，将标量谱指数（scalar spectral index）的预测范围缩小到狭窄窗口：$0.966 \lesssim n_s \lesssim 0.967$，使模型具有高度可检验性和可证伪性。

Conclusion: 该研究成功构建了一个在度量仿射引力框架下统一描述暴胀和暗能量的精粹暴胀模型，其预测的标量谱指数范围狭窄，为未来观测检验提供了明确目标。

Abstract: We study quintessential inflation in the framework of metric-affine gravity. It is well known that non-minimal couplings with the Holst invariant can generate a quasi-pole inflationary behaviour resulting in a Starobinsky-like phenomenology. The same quasi-pole behaviour can also be used in order to "flatten" the scalar potential in the Dark Energy era providing a successful framework for quintessential inflation. Agreement with all the observational constraints, reduces the predicted scalar spectral index to a narrow window: $0.966 \lesssim n_s \lesssim 0.967$, making the model highly testable and falsifiable.

</details>


### [159] [Non-metricity effects on electron scattering in bumblebee gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15959)
*A. A. Araújo Filho*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了度量仿射大黄蜂引力（metric-affine bumblebee gravity）中非度量性（non-metricity）对电子散射的影响，其中自发洛伦兹对称性破缺（spontaneous Lorentz symmetry breaking）由获得非零真空期望值（vacuum expectation value）的矢量场诱导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索度量仿射大黄蜂引力理论中非度量性效应如何影响电子散射过程，特别是洛伦兹对称性破缺背景下非度量性对色散关系（dispersion relation）和相互作用的修正。

Method: 方法包括将仿射联络（affine connection）作为独立变量处理并积分掉，得到有效描述；从完整动量空间传播子（full momentum-space propagator）确定支配相互作用的极点结构（pole structure），并构建相应的静态格林函数（static Green function）和粒子间势（interparticle potential）。

Result: 结果显示：纯类时背景（purely timelike background）下色散关系保持各向同性，产生具有均匀重标度有效耦合的库仑势（Coulomb potential），散射振幅保持卢瑟福角依赖关系；类空背景（spacelike background）则诱导色散关系的各向异性，产生具有四极调制（quadrupolar modulation）特征的取向依赖势。

Conclusion: 结论表明各向异性结构传播到微分和积分截面（differential and integrated cross sections），引入方向依赖性同时保持相互作用的长程特性；氢光谱学（hydrogen spectroscopy）约束与类时构型相关的各向同性部分，而对各向异性的搜索为四极贡献提供了更强的限制。

Abstract: We investigate non-metricity effects on electron scattering in metric-affine bumblebee gravity, where spontaneous Lorentz symmetry breaking is induced by a vector field acquiring a nonzero vacuum expectation value. Treating the affine connection as an independent variable and integrating it out leads to an effective description in which non-metricity modifies the dispersion relation of the bumblebee modes. From the full momentum-space propagator, we determine the pole structure that governs the interaction and construct the corresponding static Green function and interparticle potential. For a purely timelike background, the dispersion relation remains isotropic and produces a Coulomb potential with a uniformly rescaled effective coupling; consequently, the scattering amplitude preserves the Rutherford angular dependence, with the Lorentz-violating parameter entering only as an overall multiplicative factor. In contrast, a spacelike background induces anisotropy in the dispersion relation, leading to an orientation-dependent potential characterized by a quadrupolar modulation. This anisotropic structure propagates to the differential and integrated cross sections, introducing directional dependence while preserving the long-range character of the interaction. Finally, we consider phenomenological constraints from atomic physics. Hydrogen spectroscopy constrains the isotropic sector associated with the timelike configuration, whereas searches for anisotropies provide stronger limits on the quadrupolar contribution governed by $ξb^{2}$.

</details>


### [160] [Ringdown waves from hairy black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15979)
*Ariadna Uxue Palomino Ylla,Kosuke Makino,Akane Tanaka,Akihiro Ishibashi,Chul-Moon Yoo*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文利用准正规模-测地线对应关系，推导了毛状黑洞准正规模频率的通用公式，为广泛类别的毛状黑洞提供了系统计算方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究毛状黑洞（hairy black holes）的准正规模（quasi-normal mode, QNM）频率计算问题。传统方法可能受限于能量条件约束，需要发展更通用的计算框架。

Method: 利用准正规模-测地线对应关系（QNM--geodesic correspondence），将黑洞毛发（hair）处理为各向异性流体（anisotropic fluid），并作为微扰项添加到真空黑洞（史瓦西黑洞和克尔黑洞）背景中。

Result: 推导出独立于能量条件的通用公式，为广泛类别的毛状黑洞提供了系统计算准正规模频率的方法。该方法适用于史瓦西黑洞和克尔黑洞背景下的毛发微扰。

Conclusion: 基于准正规模-测地线对应关系建立的通用公式框架，能够系统处理毛状黑洞的准正规模频率计算问题，且不受能量条件限制，具有广泛的适用性。

Abstract: We derive general formulas for quasi-normal mode (QNM) frequencies of hairy black holes by exploiting the QNM--geodesic correspondence. The black hole hair is treated as an anisotropic fluid perturbatively added to the vacuum black holes (Schwarzschild and Kerr black holes). Under this setting, independent of energy conditions, our formulas offer a systematic method to compute quasi-normal mode frequencies for a broad class of hairy black holes.

### [161] [A minimal fractional deformation of Newtonian gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16009)
*S. M. M. Rasouli*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了一个具有单一参数α的最小分数阶牛顿引力变形模型。当α→1时，该理论退化为标准牛顿引力。该模型使用单一势能统一描述了从太阳系尺度（水星近日点进动、光线引力偏折）到宇宙学尺度（ΛCDM宇宙学、宇宙演化序列）的引力现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究的动机是探索一个最小分数阶牛顿引力框架，该框架能够统一描述从太阳系尺度到宇宙学尺度的引力现象。先前工作已证明该框架能一致地产生ΛCDM宇宙学，本研究旨在进一步验证其在弱场检验中的适用性。

Method: 研究采用一个具有单一参数α的最小分数阶牛顿引力变形模型。该方法使用统一的势能函数，在|α-1|≪1的约束条件下，分析该模型对关键弱场检验的预测，包括水星近日点进动和光线引力偏折。

Result: 研究结果表明，该分数阶牛顿模型能够使用同一势能函数和相同的α约束条件，成功描述水星近日点进动和光线引力偏折等关键弱场检验。这些结果与当前观测数据一致。

Conclusion: 该最小分数阶牛顿框架可能为从太阳系尺度到宇宙学尺度的引力动力学提供一个统一的现象学描述。此外，该分数阶宇宙学框架可能为解决宇宙学常数、宇宙尺度层次结构和哈勃张力等问题提供新的视角。

Abstract: We consider a minimal fractional deformation of Newtonian gravity characterized by a single parameter $α$. In the limit $α\to 1$, the theory reduces to standard Newtonian gravity. Previous works showed that the $Λ$CDM cosmology consistently emerges from this framework. Using a single potential, the model reproduces the full sequence of cosmic evolution (from a nonsingular pre--inflationary phase and a stable inflationary attractor to the radiation- and matter-dominated eras and the present accelerated expansion) and accounts for the growth of large-scale structure for $|α-1|\ll1$, in agreement with current observations. Here we show that the same fractional Newtonian model also describes key weak--field tests, including the perihelion precession of Mercury and the gravitational deflection of light, using a unified potential with the same constraint on $α$. These results suggest that the minimal fractional Newtonian framework may provide a unified phenomenological description of gravitational dynamics from Solar-System scales to cosmology. Finally, this fractional cosmological framework may offer new perspectives on problems such as the cosmological constant, the hierarchy of cosmological scales, and the Hubble tension.

### [162] [Ringdown bounds and spectral density limits from GWTC-3](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16026)
*Christian Balfagon*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究首次利用引力波观测数据对具有正谱密度的延迟Stieltjes型核的因果非局域引力扩展建立了观测约束，通过分析LIGO-Virgo GWTC-3目录中的17个双黑洞事件，设定了准正则模变形的上限，并排除了红外扩展谱密度的广泛类别。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在建立对因果非局域引力扩展（characterized by retarded Stieltjes-type kernels with positive spectral density）的首次观测约束，这类理论在引力波（gravitational-wave）观测中尚未得到充分检验。

Method: 采用两种互补的引力波通道：首先对LIGO-Virgo GWTC-3目录中的17个双黑洞事件进行贝叶斯（Bayesian）环降分析；其次将已发表的GWTC-3修正色散关系约束与GW170817传播速度约束映射到Stieltjes谱参数空间（mu_char, M0）。

Result: 设定了准正则模（quasi-normal mode）变形的观测上限|epsilon_Omega| < 0.05（90%置信水平），排除了mu ≤ 10^{-6} m^{-2}的红外扩展谱密度（infrared-extended spectral densities），理论预期的基准范围mu_char ~ M_*^2 ~ 10^8-10^{10} m^{-2}满足所有当前约束。

Conclusion: 亚毫米引力实验（sub-millimetre gravity experiments）在预测的因果尺度l_* ~ 10^{-4} m上运行，为直接检验提供了最有前景的路径，这些结果为未来引力波、短程引力和宇宙学领域的观测建立了定量基准。

Abstract: We establish the first observational bounds on causal nonlocal extensions of gravity characterized by retarded Stieltjes-type kernels with positive spectral density rho(mu) >= 0, using two complementary gravitational-wave channels. From a Bayesian ringdown analysis of 17 binary black hole events in the LIGO-Virgo GWTC-3 catalogue, we set an observational ceiling on universal fractional quasi-normal mode deformations of |epsilon_Omega| < 0.05 (90% C.L.), with a cumulative log Bayes factor ln B = -0.46 +/- 0.77. By mapping published GWTC-3 modified dispersion relation bounds together with the GW170817 propagation speed constraint onto the Stieltjes spectral parameter space (mu_char, M0), we exclude a broad class of infrared-extended spectral densities with mu <= 10^{-6} m^{-2}, thereby ruling out non-trivial regions of the nonlocal kernel parameter space for the first time. The theoretically motivated fiducial range mu_char ~ M_*^2 ~ 10^8-10^10 m^{-2} satisfies all current bounds. We further show that sub-millimetre gravity experiments, which already operate at the predicted causal scale l_* ~ 10^{-4} m, provide the most promising path toward a direct test. These results define quantitative benchmarks against which future observations across the gravitational-wave, short-range gravity, and cosmological sectors can be compared.

</details>


### [163] [Repetitive Penrose process in Konoplya-Zhidenko rotating non-Kerr black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16147)
*Xiao-Xiong Zeng,Dong-Ping Su,Ke Wang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了Konoplya-Zhidenko旋转非Kerr黑洞中的重复彭罗斯过程（repetitive Penrose process），分析了变形参数对能量提取效率的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索Konoplya-Zhidenko旋转非Kerr黑洞中变形参数对重复彭罗斯过程的影响，特别是对能量提取效率的调控作用。

Method: 方法包括：简要回顾Konoplya-Zhidenko旋转非Kerr黑洞，研究该时空中的彭罗斯过程基本方程，检查重复彭罗斯过程所需的迭代停止条件，并获取相应的数值结果。

Result: 结果表明：在相同衰变半径下，较大的初始无量纲变形参数$\hatη$导致更高的能量投资回报率（energy return on investment）和能量利用效率，特别是在较高衰变半径时。较小的初始$\hatη$产生更大的最大能量投资回报率。对于能量利用效率，初始$\hatη$应取中间值以最大化其峰值。此外，较大的初始$\hatη$对应较小的最大提取能量值。

Conclusion: 结论是变形参数$\hatη$对重复彭罗斯过程的能量提取特性具有显著影响，不同参数选择会优化不同的能量提取指标，为黑洞能量提取过程提供了新的调控维度。

Abstract: This paper investigates the repetitive Penrose process in Konoplya-Zhidenko rotating non-Kerr black hole, exploring the influence of the deformation parameter on the repetitive Penrose process. After a brief review of the Konoplya-Zhidenko rotating non-Kerr black hole, we study the fundamental equations of the Penrose process in this spacetime, examine the iterative stopping conditions required for the repetitive Penrose process, and obtain the corresponding numerical results. It is concluded that, in addition to previously observed phenomena, under the same decay radius, a larger initial dimensionless deformation parameter $\hatη$ leads to greater values of the energy return on investment and energy utilization efficiency, particularly at higher decay radii. Furthermore, a smaller initial $\hatη$ results in a larger maximum value of the energy return on investment. For energy utilization efficiency, the initial $\hatη$ should take an intermediate value to maximize its peak. Additionally, we find that a larger initial $\hatη$ corresponds to a smaller maximum value of the extracted energy.

</details>


### [164] [Violation of Cosmic Censorship in Einstein-Maxwell-Scalar Models with Fractional Coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16395)
*Yan-Qing Xu,Rui-Feng Zheng,Yu-Peng Zhang,Cheng-Yong Zhang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 弱宇宙监督猜想（weak cosmic censorship conjecture）在经典引力理论中具有基础性地位，它断言时空奇点通常被隐藏在事件视界之后。本研究旨在探索该猜想在带有分数耦合的爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-标量理论中的鲁棒性。

Method: 研究采用两种方法：分析静态黑洞解，并进行完全非线性动力学演化数值模拟。通过研究标量化黑洞（scalarized black holes）及其受扰配置的演化，探索分数耦合对黑洞结构的影响。

Result: 研究发现一类标量化黑洞在事件视界附近产生负能量密度，违反了经典能量条件。数值演化显示，足够强的分数耦合会驱动视界附近区域的快速曲率增长和几何退化，并伴随持续的负能量密度。

Conclusion: 虽然模拟未能解析最终状态，但观测到的动力学一致指向视界支撑结构的弱化，暗示着初生裸奇点（incipient naked singularity）的形成。这些结果揭示了一种经典机制，通过该机制分数耦合可以挑战渐近平坦时空中弱宇宙监督猜想的有效性。

Abstract: The weak cosmic censorship conjecture plays a foundational role in classical gravity by asserting that spacetime singularities are generically hidden behind event horizons. In this work, we explore its robustness in the Einstein-Maxwell-Scalar theory with fractional coupling by studying both static black hole solutions and their fully nonlinear dynamical evolution. We identify a class of scalarized black holes that develop negative energy density near the event horizon, indicating violations of the classical energy conditions. Numerical evolutions of perturbed configurations reveal that sufficiently strong fractional coupling drives rapid curvature growth and geometric degeneration in the near-horizon region, accompanied by persistent negative energy density. While the simulations do not resolve the ultimate end state, the observed dynamics consistently point toward a weakening of the horizon-supporting structure and are suggestive of incipient naked singularity formation. These results uncover a classical mechanism through which fractional coupling can challenge the validity of the weak cosmic censorship conjecture in asymptotically flat spacetimes.

### [165] [Hawking-Page phase transitions of black holes in the Hamiltonian formalism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16560)
*Tran Ngoc Thien,Vo Quoc Phong*

Main category: gr-qc

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Hawking-Page相变是黑洞热力学中的关键现象，描述反德西特时空（anti-de Sitter spacetime）中热辐射态的不稳定性。现有研究主要关注on-shell情况，而off-shell配置下的相变行为尚未充分探索。

Method: 采用哈密顿形式（Hamiltonian formalism）研究Banados-Teitelboim-Zanelli（BTZ）、Reissner-Nordstrom（RN）和Kerr-Newmann（KN）黑洞的Hawking-Page相变。该方法应用于on-shell和off-shell两种配置，并比较了现有on-shell结果。

Result: 黑洞系统的哈密顿量对应其热力学自由能（thermodynamic free energy）。在RN和KN黑洞的off-shell情况下，电荷和旋转参数影响Hawking-Page相变，使得黑洞态与热孤子态（thermal soliton states）能够共存。

Conclusion: 哈密顿形式成功应用于黑洞相变研究，揭示了电荷和旋转参数对Hawking-Page相变的重要影响。在off-shell配置下，带电和旋转黑洞能够与热孤子态共存，扩展了对黑洞热力学相变行为的理解。

Abstract: The Hawking-Page phase transition represents a critical phenomenon in black hole thermodynamics, marking the point at which a thermal radiation state in anti-de Sitter (AdS) spacetime becomes unstable. In this work, we apply the Hamiltonian formalism to study the Hawking-Page phase transition of the Banados-Teitelboim-Zenelli (BTZ) black hole in on-shell and off-shell configuration. The results show that the Hamiltonian of the black hole system corresponds to its thermodynamic free energy. Next, we examine the Hawking-Page phase transition of the Reissner-Nordstrom (RN) black hole and the Kerr-Newmann (KN) black hole, and compare our results with existing results in on-shell case. We then further extend this method to the previously unexplored off-shell case of the RN and KN black holes, thereby demonstrating the influence of the electric charge and the rotation of the black hole on their Hawking-Page phase transition. The results show that, in the presence of electric charge and totation, enables the coexistence of black hole and the thermal soliton states.

### [168] [Dyonic Einstein-Maxwell-scalar black holes: the cold, the hot and the plunge](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16701)
*Shun Chen,Xiao Yan Chew,Jutta Kunz*

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-标量理论中的动态非线性标量化黑洞，发现其存在域包含三个分支，其中第三个分支在霍金温度上表现出突然下降的特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-标量理论中动态非线性标量化黑洞的性质，特别是存在两种电磁荷时对黑洞结构和热力学行为的影响。

Method: 采用爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-标量理论框架，分析动态标量化黑洞的存在域结构，特别关注耦合函数f(φ)=exp(αφ³)的情况，研究标量场方程中源项Δ(φ)的行为。

Result: 研究发现动态标量化黑洞的存在域包含三个分支：冷分支和热分支在电荷最小值处分叉，而第三种分支则表现出霍金温度的突然下降。极端黑洞的标量场在视界处取特定值φ_H=φ_c，此时耦合函数等于电荷比值。

Conclusion: 两种电磁荷的存在引入了标量场方程源项中的Δ(φ)因子，这导致了动态标量化黑洞存在域的复杂结构，包括第三个分支中霍金温度的突然下降现象，为理解非线性标量化黑洞的热力学行为提供了新见解。

Abstract: We investigate dyonic nonlinearly scalarized black holes in Einstein-Maxwell-scalar theory. The domain of existence of scalarized dyonic black holes consists of three branches. The cold branch and the hot branch bifurcate at a minimal value of the charge, analogous to the purely electrically charged scalarized black holes. However, the presence of both charges allows for regular extremal black holes, leading to a third branch featuring a sudden plunge in Hawking temperature. In fact, the presence of both electromagnetic charges introduces a factor $Δ(φ)$ in the source term of scalar field equations that vanishes when the coupling function $f(φ)$ equals the ratio of the charges for some value of the scalar field $φ_c$. The scalar field of extremal black holes assumes precisely this value at the horizon, $φ_H=φ_c$. We demonstrate the plunge for the coupling function $f(φ)=\exp(αφ^3)$.

### [169] [Flow of yield stress fluid in a percolating network](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16224)
*Nathan Abitbol,Alex Hansen,Alberto Rosso,Laurent Talon*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本文研究了宾汉姆屈服应力流体（Bingham yield-stress fluid）在孔隙网络模型中的流动特性，重点关注部分最大半径孔道被阻塞的情况。研究识别了两种不同的流动状态：高于渗流阈值（percolation threshold）时流动曲线具有确定性特征，而在渗流阈值处则表现出非自平均（non-self-averaging）行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于理解屈服应力流体在非均匀孔隙介质中的流动行为，特别是当部分最大孔道被阻塞时，系统如何从确定性流动过渡到临界渗流状态。这种研究对于理解多孔介质中复杂流体的输运特性具有重要意义。

Method: 采用孔隙网络模型（pore network model）方法，其中孔道半径服从均匀分布。研究考虑部分最大半径孔道被阻塞的情况，流体只能通过渗流簇（percolating cluster）流动。通过分析临界压力降（critical pressure drop）、渗透率（permeability）等可观测量的统计特性来表征流动行为。

Result: 识别出两种不同的流动状态：高于渗流阈值时，流动曲线可由临界压力降、渗透率等观测量的确定性值表征，同时存在可量化的次要波动（subleading fluctuations）。在渗流阈值处，这些量变为非自平均的，其标度行为完全由临界渗流骨架（critical percolation backbone）主导，与半径的具体实现无关。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了宾汉姆流体在孔隙网络中流动的相变行为：高于渗流阈值时系统表现出确定性特征，而在临界点则呈现普适的标度行为，完全由渗流骨架的临界性质决定。这一发现强调了渗流理论在理解多孔介质中屈服应力流体流动中的核心作用。

Abstract: We study the flow of a Bingham yield-stress fluid in a pore network model where the throats have radii drawn from a uniform distribution. We consider the case in which a fraction of the largest radii is blocked. The fluid can flow only through the percolating cluster that exists when the fraction is above the percolation threshold. Two distinct flow regimes are identified: above the percolation threshold the flow curve can be characterized by deterministic values of the critical pressure drop, permeability, and other observables, with subleading fluctuations that we quantify. At the percolation threshold these quantities become non-self-averaging, and their scaling is governed exclusively by the critical percolation backbone, independent of the specific realization of the radii.

</details>

### [170] [Curvature inequalities and rigidity for constant mean curvature and spacetime constant mean curvature surfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16707)
*Alejandro Peñuela Diaz*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 该论文在黎曼几何和洛伦兹几何中建立了满足常平均曲率类型条件的曲面的曲率不等式和刚性结果，包括对CMC曲面和STCMC曲面的稳定性理论与刚性分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于扩展常平均曲率（CMC）曲面在黎曼几何中的经典不等式和刚性结果，并将其推广到洛伦兹几何中的时空常平均曲率（STCMC）曲面。旨在建立更弱的稳定性条件下的刚性现象，并发展STCMC曲面的稳定性理论。

Method: 方法基于Christodoulou-Yau不等式$H^2\leq 16π/|Σ|$，在黎曼几何中通过仅控制二阶变分常数模式的较弱稳定性概念，结合外在曲率符号条件进行分析。在洛伦兹几何中，引入STCMC曲面的稳定性理论，并在主导能量条件下证明尖锐不等式。

Result: 主要结果包括：在黎曼几何中，刚性现象在较弱稳定性条件下持续存在，无需内在对称性或近圆性假设，并可推广到高维及双曲和球面情形。在洛伦兹几何中，证明了尖锐不等式$|\vec{H}|^2\leq 16π/|Σ|$，并在等式情况下获得刚性：曲面内在为圆形，其界定的时空区域平坦，且最大整体双曲发展等距于闵可夫斯基时空中的因果菱形。

Conclusion: 结论表明，在黎曼和洛伦兹几何中，常平均曲率类型曲面在较弱稳定性条件下仍保持刚性特征。STCMC曲面的稳定性理论为洛伦兹几何中的类似问题提供了分析框架，且已知的渐近STCMC叶状结构的叶面相对于该稳定性概念是稳定的。

Abstract: We establish curvature inequalities and rigidity results for surfaces satisfying constant mean curvature type conditions in both Riemannian and Lorentzian geometry. In the Riemannian setting we study constant mean curvature (CMC) surfaces in three-dimensional manifolds with scalar curvature bounds. Building on the Christodoulou-Yau inequality $H^2\leq 16π/ |Σ|$ (with $H$ the mean curvature and $|Σ|$ the area), we show that the associated rigidity phenomena persist under a weaker notion of stability controlling only the constant mode of the second variation, combined with an extrinsic curvature sign condition. This yields Euclidean rigidity without imposing intrinsic symmetry or near-roundness assumptions and extends to higher dimensions and to the hyperbolic and spherical settings.
  In the Lorentzian setting we consider spacetime constant mean curvature (STCMC) surfaces, a natural generalization of CMC surfaces. We introduce a stability theory for STCMC surfaces and prove the sharp inequality $|\vec{H}|^2\leq 16π/ |Σ|$ under the dominant energy condition. We also obtain rigidity for the equality case: under suitable geometric assumptions the surface is intrinsically round and the spacetime region it bounds is flat, with maximal globally hyperbolic development isometric to a causal diamond in Minkowski spacetime. Finally, we show that the canonical asymptotic STCMC foliations known in both the spacelike and null settings have leaves that are stable with respect to this notion of stability.

### [171] [Strangeness neutrality and the QCD phase diagram](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13455)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We map out the phase structure of $N_f=2+1$ flavour QCD at strangeness neutrality with functional QCD. We find a critical end point at $(T_{\rm CEP},μ_{B,{\rm CEP}})|_{n_S=0} = (92, 696)$\,MeV. The computation is done with the functional renormalisation group, and we systematically improve on previous works, hence reducing the systematic error significantly. Our results pass relevant QCD benchmarks: they agree well with and corroborate the QCD phase structure from functional QCD results at vanishing strangeness chemical potential. Moreover, they agree well with lattice QCD results at vanishing chemical potential. Specifically, the ratio of the second order curvature coefficient $κ_2$ agrees with that obtained from lattice computations, $κ_2(n_S=0)/κ_2(μ_S=0)=0.897(20)$.

### [172] [$gg \to ZH$ at NLO matched to parton showers with ggxy and POWHEG](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15762)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 寻找量子色动力学临界终点（QCD critical end point, CEP）是重离子物理的重要目标，这推动了对临界动力学敏感的涨落观测量研究。重子数涨落是天然探针，因为净重子密度在CEP附近可作为有效序参量。

Method: 本研究对有限空间尺度的系统进行了动量空间两点关联函数（momentum-space two-point correlation function）的理论分析，特别关注有限尺寸效应的影响。

Result: 研究显示有限尺寸效应导致了一个有效标度指数（effective scaling exponent），该指数仅在实验可及动量范围内的规定标度区域（prescribed scaling region）与无限扩展系统的标度指数一致。

Conclusion: 有限尺寸约束显著改变了涨落的可观测结构，特别是在实验进行测量的动量空间。重离子碰撞中产生的火球（fireball）的有限尺寸和有限寿命施加了内在截断，调节了关联长度（correlation length）的增长。

Abstract: The search for the QCD critical end point (CEP) is a major objective of contemporary heavy-ion physics, motivating the study of fluctuation observables that are sensitive to critical dynamics. In particular, baryon-number fluctuations provide a natural probe because the net-baryon density can serve as an effective order parameter in the vicinity of the CEP. Near criticality, long-range correlations and power-law scaling are expected to emerge in the real-space two-point function of the baryon density, yet the finite size and finite lifetime of the fireball created in heavy-ion collisions impose intrinsic cutoffs that regulate the growth of the correlation length. These finite-size constraints significantly modify the observable structure of fluctuations, especially in momentum space, where experiments perform measurements. In this work we present a theoretical analysis of the momentum-space two-point correlation function for a system of finite spatial extent. We show that finite size effects lead to an effective scaling exponent which coincides with that of the infinitely extended system only in a prescribed scaling region within the experimentally accessible momentum range.

Abstract: Black hole superradiance is a powerful probe of ultralight axions. If nature contains a boson with a mass of order $10^{-12}\,$eV, $\textit{mere vacuum fluctuations}$ will lead to its efficient production around spinning stellar mass black holes, forming a gravitational atom that both drains the black hole spin and decays to produce near-monochromatic gravitational waves. Existing superradiance constraints derive primarily from spin measurements of a handful of identified black holes. Here we instead present a detailed study of the population level effect: gravitational waves arising from both the 100 million black holes in the Milky Way and the stochastic signal from axion clouds throughout the universe. We study the impact of a broad range of systematic uncertainties on the black hole properties and compute the projected axion sensitivity for LIGO, as well as the future instruments Einstein Telescope, Cosmic Explorer, and a high-frequency Magnetic Weber Bar. Abstract: We evaluate the feasibility of high-precision coherent elastic neutrino-nucleus scattering measurements exploiting mono-energetic neutrinos produced by electron-capture (EC) decays of intense radioactive sources, such as $^{51}$Cr or $^{37}$Ar. ### [179] [Observing Micro Black Hole Dark Matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15764)
*Manuel Ettengruber,Florian Kühnel*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 原初微黑洞（primordial micro black holes）可作为暗物质候选者，前提是短距离引力通过额外维度或大量粒子种类被修正，且记忆负担效应（memory-burden effect）充分抑制霍金蒸发（Hawking evaporation）。这类黑洞在质量-半径关系、温度、熵和寿命方面与四维爱因斯坦理论的黑洞不同，使极轻物体也能保持宇宙学稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于修正引力理论框架（包括额外维度和大量粒子种类模型），分析微黑洞的物理性质变化。考虑记忆负担效应对霍金蒸发的抑制作用，计算黑洞在过渡区域（transition regime）的质量-半径关系、温度、熵和寿命。

Result: 中子星存活提供了最稳健的约束条件，而参数空间的狭窄区域可同时保持可行性并解释银河系中心缺失脉冲星问题。在中微子望远镜中的弥散蒸发信号主要在额外维度情景中相关，而在一般粒子种类模型中，可见辐射因蒸发到暗区而被强烈抑制。在额外维度实现中，合并诱导的蒸发爆发可作为额外探测手段。

Abstract: Primordial micro black holes can constitute dark matter if short-distance gravity is modified by extra dimensions or a large number of species and if the memory-burden effect sufficiently suppresses Hawking evaporation. The resulting black holes in the transition regime differ from their four-dimensional Einsteinian counterparts through their mass--radius relation, temperature, entropy, and lifetime, which can render even very light objects cosmologically stable. The most promising observational consequences of such micro black holes dark matter are analysed. Neutron star survival yields the most robust constraints, while a narrow region of parameter space can simultaneously remain viable and address the missing-pulsar problem in the Galactic center. Diffuse evaporation signals in neutrino telescopes are found to be relevant mainly in extra-dimensional scenarios, whereas in generic species models, visible emission is strongly suppressed by evaporation into dark sectors. Merger-induced evaporation bursts can provide an additional probe in extra-dimensional realisations if the post-merger remnant briefly returns to the semiclassical phase. Overall, micro black holes dark matter remains phenomenologically viable in constrained regions, with neutron stars, neutrino telescopes, and merger signatures providing complementary tests.

### [180] [Cosmological Collider Searches beyond the Hubble Scale with Planck Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15728)
*Soubhik Kumar,Qianshu Lu,Zhong-Zhi Xianyu,Yisong Zhang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究通过有效场论方法寻找原初非高斯性（NG），首次使用Planck数据搜索重标量粒子介导的非高斯性信号，并发现质量为M≫H的粒子在化学势激发下存在1.7σ的微弱证据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究原初非高斯性（primordial non-Gaussianity）不仅能够揭示宇宙暴胀（cosmic inflation）的物理机制，还能探索极高能标下的基本相互作用结构。宇宙对撞机（cosmological collider）物理计划展示了通过寻找振荡非高斯性实现极重粒子质量-自旋谱学的可能性。

Method: 采用有效场论（effective field theory）方法，识别出能够产生由重标量粒子介导的最大非高斯性的费曼图（Feynman diagrams）类别。计算非高斯性的完整形状（full shape），并首次使用Planck数据搜索这些信号。

Result: 对于质量M∼H（暴胀哈勃尺度）的重标量粒子，未发现非高斯性的证据。当M≫H时，量子真空涨落无法有效产生此类重粒子，导致搜索灵敏度下降。然而，在化学势（chemical potential）激发机制下，对于满足ω-M≃3H的化学势ω和质量M参数范围，发现了全局1.7σ的非零非高斯性证据（考虑了多重检验效应）。

Conclusion: 该研究首次使用Planck数据对参数化重于H的粒子进行了宇宙对撞机搜索，在化学势激发机制下发现了微弱的非高斯性证据，为探索极高能标物理提供了新的观测约束。

Abstract: Searches for primordial non-Gaussianity (NG) has the potential to not only reveal the physics of cosmic inflation, but also the structure of fundamental interactions at the highest energies. The cosmological collider (CC) physics program exemplifies this possibility and demonstrates how searches for oscillatory NG can lead to mass-spin spectroscopy of extremely heavy states. Adopting an effective field theory approach, we find the class of Feynman diagrams that can give the largest NG mediated by a heavy scalar particle with mass $M\sim H$, the inflationary Hubble scale. We compute the full shape of the NG and perform the first search for this shape using Planck data, finding no evidence for NG. This search loses its sensitivity as $M\gg H$ since quantum vacuum fluctuations cannot efficiently produce such heavier particles. We then focus on a mechanism where a chemical potential excites on-shell scalar particles with mass $M\gg H$. Computing the full shapes, we perform the first CC search for particles parametrically heavier than $H$ using Planck data. For a range of chemical potential $ω$ and $M$ satisfying $ω-M \simeq 3H$, we find a global $1.7σ$ evidence for non-zero NG, after taking into account the look-elsewhere effect.

</details>


### [181] [Effect of gravity on Neutrino Oscillations in $κ$-deformed space-time](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16381)
*Harsha Sreekumar,E. Harikumar*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究分析了时空量子化（quantisation of space-time）如何影响引力背景下的费米子传播，探讨了非对易时空（non-commutative space-time）中引力相互作用对中微子振荡概率的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索时空量子化对引力背景下费米子传播的影响，特别是将引力效应通过自旋联络（spin connection）纳入考虑，该联络包含无挠的Levi-Civita联络和Contortion张量。

Method: 方法包括使用自旋联络描述引力效应，该联络由Levi-Civita联络和Contortion张量组成，导致拉格朗日量中出现四费米子相互作用项。由于时空的非对易性，相互作用项的形变通过tetrads依赖于背景度规。

Result: 研究发现引力效应导致拉格朗日量中出现四费米子相互作用项，且该相互作用项的形变通过tetrads依赖于背景度规。进一步将该相互作用项纳入分析，研究了非对易时空中中微子与背景物质的引力相互作用对中微子振荡概率的影响。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了时空量子化背景下引力相互作用对费米子传播的影响机制，特别是通过自旋联络引入的四费米子相互作用项及其对中微子振荡概率的潜在影响，为非对易时空中引力与量子场相互作用的深入研究提供了理论基础。

Abstract: In this study, we analyse how quantisation of space-time affects propagating fermions in the presence of gravity. Effect of gravity is incorporated using spin connection which consists of universal torsion-free Levi-Civita connection and the Contortion tensor. This leads to the appearance of a four-fermion interaction term in the Lagrangian and because of non-commutativity of space-time, the deformation of the interaction term is found to depend on the background metric through tetrads. Further, we incorporate this interaction term to see the effect of gravitational interactions of neutrinos with the background matter in non-commutative space-time and study its effect on neutrino oscillation probabilities.

</details>


### [182] [Light baryon spectra and Regge trajectories from anomalous holographic hard wall models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16727)
*Rafael A. Costa-Silva,Henrique Boschi-Filho*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出三种反常全息硬壁模型（AHW₁、AHW₂、AHW₃）来描述自旋1/2和3/2的轻重子谱，通过引入对数形式或幂律形式的反常维度修正，显著改进了对PDG实验数据的拟合，并获得了近似线性的Regge轨迹。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统全息硬壁模型（holographic hard wall model）在描述轻重子（light baryons）质量谱时存在局限性。本文旨在通过引入反常维度修正来改进对自旋1/2和3/2轻重子谱的描述，以获得更符合实验数据的Regge轨迹。

Method: 基于AdS/CFT对应关系的半经典分析，提出了三种反常硬壁模型：AHW₁模型采用Δ_anom.=a ln L +b形式；AHW₂模型采用Δ_anom.=a ln(L+S+1/2)+b形式；AHW₃模型采用Δ_Lin.=a L^c +b形式。通过调整参数a、b、c来拟合PDG实验数据。

Result: 三种反常硬壁模型均能更好地描述轻重子质量，相比原始硬壁模型有显著改进。AHW₁和AHW₂模型产生了近似线性的Regge轨迹（M²×L），而AHW₃模型则产生了渐近线性的Regge轨迹，与PDG数据兼容性良好。

Conclusion: 引入反常维度修正的全息硬壁模型能够有效改进对轻重子谱的描述，特别是对数形式和幂律形式的反常维度都能产生符合实验数据的Regge轨迹，为强子谱学研究提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: In this work we propose anomalous versions of the holographic hard wall (HW) model to describe the spectra of light baryons of spin 1/2 and 3/2, and obtain their Regge trajectories. The anomalous contributions to the dimensions of the baryonic operators of logarithm form come from a semiclassical analysis of the AdS/CFT correspondence and were used recently for glueballs and light unflavoured mesons. Inspired by these results, we first propose an anomalous dimension of the form $Δ_{\rm anom.}=a\ln L +b$, where $a$ and $b$ are phenomenological constants to be adjusted numerically to better fit the experimental data of the PDG, and $L$ is the angular momentum of each baryonic state. Second, we discuss the case where the anomalous dimension also depends on the spin $S$ as $Δ_{\rm anom.}=a\ln (L+S+1/2) +b$, and fix the parameters $a$ and $b$ targeting PDG data. These two models, called AHW$_1$ and AHW$_2$, give better results for light baryon masses $(M)$ in comparison with the original HW model and show approximately linear Regge trajectories $(M^2\times L)$. We also consider a third anomalous HW model in which the dimension of the baryonic operator increases as $Δ_{\rm Lin.}=a L^c +b$, where $a$, $b$, and $c$ are constants adjusted to fit the light baryonic masses of PDG. Apart from compatible masses with PDG data, this case produces Regge trajectories that are asymptotically linear.

</details>


### [183] [Two-loop Six-point Planar Massless Feynman Integrals to Higher $ε$ Orders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16831)
*Yuanche Liu,Antonela Matijašić,Tiziano Peraro,Yingxuan Xu,Zihua Yang,Yang Zhang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究计算了两圈六点平面无质量费曼积分（two-loop six-point planar massless Feynman integrals）在维度正规化参数ε更高阶的贡献，对应更高超越权重（higher transcendental weights），将结果扩展到权重六，并开发了高效数值计算方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前研究仅计算到权重四以满足两圈规范理论振幅（two-loop gauge theory amplitudes）需求，需要扩展到更高权重以支持未来三圈振幅计算，并为符号（symbols）和簇代数（cluster algebra）的形式研究提供新数据。

Method: 采用现代有理重构方法（modern rational reconstruction methods）识别包含269个字母的完整字母表（complete alphabet），推导解析正则微分方程（analytic canonical differential equation），并利用切比雪夫伪谱传输（Chebyshev pseudospectral transport）新方法高效数值计算纯基（pure basis）。

Result: 获得了权重六的符号结果（symbols up to weight six），在物理散射区域（physical scattering region）内将纯基高效计算到ε²阶，完整字母表包含269个字母，为未来三圈振幅提供了计算基础。

Conclusion: 该工作将两圈六点平面无质量费曼积分的计算扩展到更高超越权重，开发了高效数值方法，结果可直接应用于未来三圈振幅计算，并为符号和簇代数的形式理论研究提供了新数据。

Abstract: In this work, we calculate two-loop six-point planar massless Feynman integrals at higher orders in the dimensional regulator $ε$, corresponding to higher transcendental weights. In previous works, these integrals were calculated up to weight four for the purpose of two-loop gauge theory amplitudes. Using modern rational reconstruction methods, we identify the complete alphabet with $269$ letters relevant for the all-weight orders, derive the analytic canonical differential equation and obtain the symbols up to weight six. As a proof of concept, using a new method with Chebyshev pseudospectral transport, we show that the corresponding pure basis can be efficiently evaluated up to weight six, i.e., to $ \mathcal{O}(ε^2)$ in a physical scattering region. The results of this work can be applied to future three-loop amplitudes and provide new data for the formal study of symbols and cluster algebra.

</details>
