### [184] [A unified variational framework for phase-field fracture and third-medium contact in finite deformation hyperelasticity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15635)
*Jaemin Kim,Gukheon Kim,Sungmin Yoon,Dong-Hwa Lee*

Main category: physics.comp-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个统一的变分框架，将相场断裂（PFF）和第三介质接触（TMC）整合到有限变形超弹性理论中，通过正则化方法同时处理裂纹和接触问题，无需显式界面追踪算法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究的动机在于建立一个统一的框架来处理接触与断裂的耦合现象。传统方法需要分别处理裂纹拓扑和接触界面，而本文旨在通过正则化策略消除对显式接触检测或裂纹追踪算法的需求。

Method: 方法基于变分框架，将尖锐裂纹拓扑正则化为弥散损伤场，同时将离散接触界面正则化为具有辅助场的柔性虚拟介质。该框架将相场断裂（phase-field fracture）和第三介质接触（third-medium contact）整合到有限变形超弹性（finite deformation hyperelasticity）理论中。

Result: 通过二维三点弯曲和三维巴西圆盘试验模拟验证了该框架的有效性。模拟结果展示了接触诱导应力集中与裂纹成核/扩展之间的相互作用，特别是巴西圆盘模拟自然再现了接触区域附近的二次压碎型断裂带，这一现象在实验中常见但简化加载模型无法捕捉。

Conclusion: 该统一变分框架为预测性模拟耦合接触-断裂现象提供了新途径，无需依赖显式界面追踪。研究结果表明该方法能够捕捉实验观察到的复杂断裂模式，为相关工程应用提供了有效的数值工具。

Abstract: This paper presents a unified variational framework that integrates phase-field fracture (PFF) and third-medium contact (TMC) within finite deformation hyperelasticity. The key idea is that both crack and contact are treated through regularization: the sharp crack topology is regularized into a diffuse damage field, while the discrete contact interface is regularized by a compliant fictitious medium with auxiliary fields. This strategy eliminates the need for explicit contact detection or crack tracking algorithms. The framework is validated through two-dimensional three-point bending and three-dimensional Brazilian disk test simulations, demonstrating the interplay between contact-induced stress concentration and crack nucleation/propagation. In particular, the Brazilian disk simulation naturally reproduces secondary crushing-type fracture zones near the contact regions -- a phenomenon consistently observed in experiments yet inaccessible to simplified loading models. These results pave the way for predictive simulation of coupled contact-fracture phenomena without recourse to explicit interface tracking.

</details>


### [185] [Tuning Cu/Diamond Interfacial Thermal Conductance via Nitrogen-Termination Engineering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16347)
*Guang Yang,Xinling Tang,Zhongkang Lin,Yulin Gu,Wei Hao,Yujie Du,Xiaoguang Wei*

Main category: physics.comp-ph

TL;DR: 本研究提出氮终止（nitrogen-termination）策略提升Cu/金刚石界面热导（ITC），通过机器学习原子间势（MLIP）模拟揭示氮化夹层调控声子传输的原子机制，相比裸界面提升21%热导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Cu-金刚石复合材料作为高导热电子冷却材料具有前景，但其性能受限于Cu/金刚石界面热导（ITC）较差。现有金属涂层易导致石墨化问题，需要开发非金属改性策略。

Method: 基于MACE机器学习原子间势（MLIP）框架，微调预训练的MACE-MPA-0基础模型，整合定制的C-N-Cu训练数据集。通过MLIP驱动的晶格动力学模拟，分析氮终止界面的声子传输特性。

Result: 金刚石表面的原子级平坦氮终止使界面热导相比裸Cu/金刚石界面提升21%。模式分辨声子谱分析显示，频率高于4 THz的LA声子在Γ-X和Γ-U方向波矢附近被选择性调制。局域振动态和界面键合分析表明氮终止通过表面质量修饰和键合调控来调节界面热传导。

Conclusion: 氮终止策略为通过非金属改性调控Cu/金刚石界面热传输开辟了新途径，避免了金属涂层的石墨化问题，为提升Cu-金刚石复合材料中声子介导的热传输提供了新指导原则。

Abstract: Cu-diamond composites are recognized as promising high-thermal-conductivity candidates for electronic cooling, offering tunable properties and competitive cost. However, their performance is significantly limited by the poor Cu/diamond interfacial thermal conductance (ITC). Here, we propose a nitrogen-termination strategy to tune the ITC of Cu/diamond interfaces and unravel atomistic mechanisms by which nitride interlayers tailor phonon transport. Based on the MACE machine-learning interatomic potential (MLIP) framework, we fine-tune the pre-trained MACE-MPA-0 foundation model by incorporating customized C-N-Cu training datasets. Through MLIP-driven lattice dynamics simulations, we demonstrate that an atomically flat N-termination on diamond enhances the ITC by 21% compared to the bare Cu/diamond interface. Mode-resolved phonon spectroscopy reveals that the LA phonons with frequency above 4 THz and wavevectors near Γ-X and Γ-U directions are selectively modulated by N-termination engineering. Analyses of local vibrational states and interfacial bonding further indicate that the N-termination on diamond tunes the interfacial heat conduction via surficial mass modification and bonding regulation, as evidenced by variations in LDOS overlap and COHP spectra. These findings open venues for tuning heat transfer across Cu/diamond interfaces via non-metallic modification, which avoids the graphitization issues associated with metallic coatings, and provide novel guidelines for upgrading the phonon-mediated heat transfer in Cu-diamond composites.

</details>
